        <div n="17" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.1"><label>ci.17.1</label> athāto
            visarpanāḍīstanarogacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.2"><label>ci.17.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.3"><label>ci.17.3</label> sādhyā visarpāstraya ādito ye na
            sannipātakṣatajau hi sādhyau | sādhyeṣu tatpathyagaṇairvidadhyād ghṛtāni
            sekāṃś ca tathopadehān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.4"><label>ci.17.4</label>
            mustāśatāhvāsuradārukuṣṭhavārāhikustumburukṛṣṇagandhāḥ | vātātmako coṣṇagaṇāḥ
            prayojyāḥ sekeṣu lepeṣu tathā <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
              >*</ref>śṛteṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.5"><label>ci.17.5</label> yat pañcamūlaṃ khalu
            kaṇṭakākhyamalpaṃ mahaccāpyatha vallijaṃ ca | taccopayojyaṃ bhiṣajā pardehe
            seke ghṛte cāpi tathaiva taile || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.6"><label>ci.17.6</label> kaseruśṛṅgāṭakapadmagundrāḥ
            saśaivalāḥ sotpalakardamāś ca | vastrāntarāḥ pittakṛte visarpe lepā vidheyāḥ
            saghṛtāḥ suśītāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.7"><label>ci.17.7</label> hrīveralāmajjakacandanāni
            srotojamuktāmaṇigairikāś ca | kṣīreṇa piṣṭāḥ saghṛtāḥ suśītā lepāḥ
            prayojyāstanavaḥ sukhāya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.8"><label>ci.17.8</label> prapauṇḍarīkaṃ madhukaṃ payasyā
            mañjiṣṭhikā padmakacandane ca | sugandhikā ceti sukhāya lepaḥ paitte visarpe
            bhiṣajā prayojyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.9"><label>ci.17.9</label> nyagrodhavargaiḥ pariṣecanaṃ ca
            ghṛtaṃ ca kuryāt svarasena tasya | śītaiḥ payobhiś ca madhūdakaiśca
            saśarkarairikṣurasaiś ca sekān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.10"><label>ci.17.10</label> ghṛtasya
            gaurīmadhukāravindarodhrāmburājādanagairikeṣu | tatharṣabhe padmakasārivāsu
              kākolimedākumudotpaleṣu<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.11"><label>ci.17.11</label> sacandanāyāṃ madhuśarkarāyāṃ
            drākṣāsthirāpṛśniśatāhvayāsu | kalkīkṛtāsūdakamatra dattvā nyagrodhavargasya
            tathā sthirādeḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.12"><label>ci.17.12</label> gaṇasya
            bilvādikapañcamūlyāścaturguṇaṃ kṣīramathāpi tadvat | prasthaṃ vipakvaṃ
            pariṣecanena paittīrnihanyāt tu visarpanāḍīḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.13"><label>ci.17.13</label> visphoṭaduṣṭavraṇaśīrṣarogān
            pākaṃ tathā++āsyasya nihanti pānāt | grahārdite śoṣiṇi cāpi bāle ghṛtaṃ hi
            gauryādikametadiṣṭam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.14"><label>ci.17.14</label> ajā 'śvagandhā saralā sakālā
            saikaiṣikā cāpyathavā 'jaśṛṅgī | gomūtrapiṣṭo vihitaḥ pradeho hanyādvisarpaṃ
            kaphajaṃ sa śīghram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.15"><label>ci.17.15</label>
            kālānusāryāgurucocaguñjārāsnāvacāśītaśivedraparṇyaḥ |
            pālindimuñjātamahīkadambā hitā visarpeṣu kaphātmakeṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.16"><label>ci.17.16</label> gaṇas tu yojyo varuṇapravṛttaḥ
            kriyāsu sarvāsu vicakṣaṇena | saṃśodhanaṃ śoṇitamokṣaṇaṃ ca śreṣṭhaṃ
            visarpeṣu cikitsitaṃ hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.17"><label>ci.17.17</label> sarvāṃś ca pakvān pariśodhya
            dhīmān vraṇakrameṇopacaredyathoktam | nāḍī tridoṣaprabhavā na
            sidhyeccheṣāścatasraḥ khalu<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>
            yatnasādhyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.18"><label>ci.17.18</label> tatrānilotthām upanāhya
            pūrvamaśeṣataḥ pūyagatiṃ vidārya | tilair apāmārgaphalaiś ca piṣṭvā
            sasaindhavairbandhanamatra kuryāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.19"><label>ci.17.19</label> prakṣālane cāpi sadā varaṇasya
            yojyaṃ mahadyat khalu pañcamūlam | hiṃsrāṃ haridrāṃ kaṭukāṃ balāṃ ca
            gojihvikāṃ cāpi sabilvamūlām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.20"><label>ci.17.20</label> saṃhṛtya tailaṃ vipacedvraṇasya
            saṃśodhanaṃ pūraṇaropaṇaṃ ca | pittātmikāṃ prāgupanāhya dhīmānutkārikābhiḥ
            sapayoghṛtābhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.21"><label>ci.17.21</label> nipātya śastraṃ
            tilanāgadantīyaṣṭyāhvakalkaiḥ paripūrayettām | prakṣālane cāpi sasomanimbā
            niśā prayojyā kuśalena nityam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.22"><label>ci.17.22</label> śyāmātribhaṇḍītriphalāsu siddhaṃ
            haridrayo rodhrakavṛkṣayoś ca | ghṛtaṃ sadugdhaṃ vraṇatarpaṇena hanyād gatiṃ
            koṣṭhagatā 'pi yā syāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.23"><label>ci.17.23</label> nāḍīṃ kaphotthām upanāhya samyak
            kulatthasiddhārthakaśaktukiṇvaiḥ | mṛdūkṛtāmeṣya gatiṃ viditvā
            nipātayecchastramaśeṣakārī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.24"><label>ci.17.24</label> dadyādvraṇe nimbatilān <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>sadantīn
            surāṣṭrajāsaindhavasaṃprayuktān | prakṣālane cāpi
            karañjanimbajātyakṣapīlusvarasāḥ prayojyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.25"><label>ci.17.25</label> suvarcikāsaindhavacitrakeṣu
            nikumbhatālītalarūpikāsu | phaleṣv apāmārgabhaveṣu caiva kuryāt samūtreṣu
            hitāya tailam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.26"><label>ci.17.26</label> nāḍīṃ tu śalyaprabhavāṃ vidārya
            nirhṛtya śalyaṃ praviśodhya mārgam | saṃśodhayet
            kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhais tilais tato ropaṇamāśu kuryāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.27"><label>ci.17.27</label>
            kumbhīkakharjūrakapitthabilvavanaspatīnāṃ ca śalāṭuvargaiḥ | kṛtvā kaṣāyaṃ
            vipacet tu tailamāvāpya mustāsaralāpriyaṅgūḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.28"><label>ci.17.28</label> sugandhikāmocarasāhipuṣoaṃ
            rodhraṃ vidadhyādapi dhātakīṃ ca | etena śalyaprabhavā tu nāḍī rohedvraṇo vā
            sukhabhāśu caiva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.29"><label>ci.17.29</label> kṛśadurbalabhīrūṇāṃ nāḍī
            marmāśritā ca yā | kṣārasūtreṇa tāṃ cchindyānna tu śastreṇa buddhimān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.30"><label>ci.17.30</label> eṣaṇyā gatimanviṣya
            ārasūtrānusāriṇīm | sūcīṃ nidadhyād gatyante tahonnamyāśu nirharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.31"><label>ci.17.31</label> sūtrasyāntaṃ samānīya gāḍhaṃ
            bandhaṃ samācaret | tataḥ kṣārabalaṃ vīkṣya sūtramanyat praveśayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.32"><label>ci.17.32</label> kṣārāktaṃ matimān vaidyo yāvanna
              <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>chidyate gatiḥ |
            bhagandare 'pyeṣa vidhiḥ kāryo vaidyena jānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.33"><label>ci.17.33</label> sūcībhiryavavaktrābhirācitān vā
            samantataḥ | mūle sūtreṇa badhnīyācchinne copavaredvraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.34"><label>ci.17.34</label> yā dvivraṇīye 'bhihitāstu
            vartyastāḥ sarvanāḍīṣu bhiṣagvidadhyāt | ghoṇṭāphalatvaglavaṇāni
            lākṣāpūgīphalaṃ cālavaṇaṃ ca patram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.35"><label>ci.17.35</label> sruhyarkadugdhena tu kalka eṣa
            vartīkṛto hantyacireṇa nāḍīḥ | bibhītakāmrāsthivaṭapravālā
            hareṇukāśaṅkhinibījamasyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.36"><label>ci.17.36</label> vārāhikandaś ca tathā pradeyo
            nāḍīṣu tailena ca miśrayitvā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.37"><label>ci.17.37</label> dhattūrajaṃ madanakodravajaṃ ca
            bījaṃ kośātakī śukanasā mṛgabhojinī ca | aṅkoṭabījakusumaṃ gatiṣu prayojyaṃ
            lākṣodakāhṛtamalāsu vikṛtya<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>
            cūrṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.38"><label>ci.17.38</label> tathā ca gomāṃsamasīṃ hitāya
            koṣṭhāśritasyādarato diśanti | varīkṛtaṃ mākṣikasaṃprayuktaṃ nāḍīghnamuktaṃ
            lavaṇottamaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.39"><label>ci.17.39</label> duṣṭavraṇe yadvihitaṃ ca tailaṃ
            tat sarvanāḍīṣu bhiṣagvidadhyāt | cūrṇīkṛtair atha vimiśritamebhir eva tailaṃ
            prayuktamacireṇa gatiṃ nihanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.40"><label>ci.17.40</label> eṣveva mūtrasahiteṣu vidhāya
            tailaṃ tat sādhitaṃ gatimapohati saptarātrāt | piṇḍītakasya tu
            varāhavibhāvitasya mūleṣu kandaśakaleṣu ca sauvaheṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.41"><label>ci.17.41</label> tailaṃ kṛtaṃ gatimapohati
            śīghrametat kandeṣu cāmaravarāyudhasāhvayeṣu |
            bhallātakārkamaricairlavaṇottamena siddhaṃ viḍaṅgarajanīdvayacitrakaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.42"><label>ci.17.42</label> syan mārkavasya ca rasena nihanti
            tailaṃ nāḍīṃ kaphānilakṛtāmapacīṃ vraṇāṃś ca | stanye gate vikṛtimāśu bhiṣak
            tu dhātrīṃ pītāṃ ghṛtaṃ pariṇate 'hani vāmayet tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.43"><label>ci.17.43</label> nimbodakena madhumāgadhikāyutena
            vāntāgate 'hani ca mudgarasāśanā syāt | evaṃ tryahaṃ caturahaṃ ṣaḍahaṃ vamedvā
            sarpiḥ pibettriphalayā saha saṃyutaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.44"><label>ci.17.44</label> bhārgīṃ pibet tu payasaḥ
            pariśodhanārthamāragvadhādiṣu varaṃ madhunā kaṣāyam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.45"><label>ci.17.45</label> sāmānyametadupadiṣṭamato
            viśeṣāddoṣān payonipatitān śamayedyathāsvam | rogaṃ stanotthitamavekṣya
            bhiṣagvidadhyādyadvidradhāvabhihitaṃ bahuśo vidhānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.46"><label>ci.17.46</label> saṃpacyamānam api taṃ tu
            vinopanāhaiḥ saṃbhojanena khalu pācayituṃ yateta | śīghraṃ stano hi
            mṛdumāṃsatayopanaddhaḥ sarvaṃ prakotham upayātyavadīryate ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.17.47"><label>ci.17.47</label> pakve tu dugdhahariṇīḥ parihṛtya
            nāḍīḥ kṛṣṇaṃ ca cūcukayugaṃ vidadhīta śastram | āme vidāhini tathaiva gate ca
            pākaṃ dhātryāḥ stanau satatam eva ca nirduhīta ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
            visarpanāḍīstanarogacikitsitaṃ nāma saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||17 || </p>
        </div>
        <div n="18" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>aṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.1"><label>ci.18.1</label> athāto
            granthyapacyarbudagalagaṇḍacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.2"><label>ci.18.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.3"><label>ci.18.3</label> granthiṣvathāmeṣu
            bhiṣagvidadhyācchophakriyāṃ vistaraśo<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
              >*</ref> vidhijñaḥ | rakṣedbalaṃ cāpi narasya nityaṃ tadrakṣitaṃ
            vyādhibalaṃ nihanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.4"><label>ci.18.4</label> tailaṃ pibet sarpiratho dvayaṃ vā
            dattvā vasāṃ vā trivṛtaṃ vidadhyāt | apehivātādaśamūlasiddhaṃ
            vaidyaścatuḥsnehamatho dvayaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.5"><label>ci.18.5</label> hiṃsrā 'tha rohiṇyamṛtā 'tha bhargī
            śyonākabilvāgurukṛṣṇagandhāḥ | gojī ca piṣṭā saha tālapatryā granthau
            vidheyo 'nilaje pralepaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.6"><label>ci.18.6</label> svedopanāhān vividhāṃśca
            kuryāttathā prasiddhānaparāṃś ca lepān | vidārya vā pakvamapohya pūyaṃ
            prakṣālya bilvārkanarendratoyaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.7"><label>ci.18.7</label> tilaiḥ sapañcāṅgulapatramiśraiḥ
            saṃśodhayet saindhavasaṃprayuktaiḥ | śuddhaṃ vraṇaṃ vā 'pyuparopayet tu tailena
            rāsnāsaralānvitena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.8"><label>ci.18.8</label> viḍaṅgayaṣṭīmadhukāmṛtābhiḥ
            siddhena vā kṣīrasamanvitena | jalaukasaḥ pittakṛte hitās tu kṣīrodakābhyāṃ
            paribecanaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.9"><label>ci.18.9</label> kākolivargasya ca śītalāni pibet
            kaṣāyāṇi saśarkarāṇi | drākṣārasenekṣurasena vā 'pi cūrṇaṃ pibeccāpi
            harītakīnām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.10"><label>ci.18.10</label> madhūkajambvarjunavetasānāṃ
            tvagbhiḥ pradehānavacārayeta | saśarkarair vā tṛṇaśūnyakandairdihyādabhīkṣṇaṃ
            muculundajair vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.11"><label>ci.18.11</label> vidārya vā pakvamapohya pūyaṃ
            dhāvet kaṣāyeṇa vanaspatīnām | tilaiḥ sayaṣṭīmadhukairviśodhya sarpiḥ
            prayojyaṃ madhurairvipakvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.12"><label>ci.18.12</label> hṛteṣu doṣeṣu yathānupūrvyā
            granthau bhiṣak śleṣmasamutthite tu | svinnasya vimlāpanam eva kuryād
            aṅguṣṭhalohopalaveṇudaṇḍaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.13"><label>ci.18.13</label>
            vikaṅkatāragvadhakākaṇantīkākādanītāpasavṛkṣamūlaiḥ | ālepayet
            piṇḍaphalārkabhārgīkarañjakālāmadanaiś ca vidvān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.14"><label>ci.18.14</label> amarmajātaṃ
            śamamaprayāntamapakvamevāpaharedvidārya | dahet sthite cāsṛji siddhakarmā
            sadyaḥkṣatoktaṃ ca vidhiṃ vidadhyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.15"><label>ci.18.15</label> yā māṃsakandyaḥ kaṭhinā
            bṛhatyastāsveṣa yojyaś ca vidhirvidhijñaiḥ | śastreṇa vā++āpāṭhya supakvamāśu
            prakṣālayet pathyatamaiḥ kaṣāyaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.16"><label>ci.18.16</label> saṃśodhanais taṃ ca viśodhayettu
            kṣārottaraiḥ kṣaudraguḍapragāḍhaiḥ | śuddhe ca tailaṃ tvavacāraṇīyaṃ
            viḍaṅgapāṭhārajanīvipakvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.17"><label>ci.18.17</label> medaḥsamutthe tilakalkadigdhaṃ
            dattvopariṣṭādviguṇaṃ paṭāntam | hutāśataptena muhuḥ pramṛjyāllohena
            dhīmānadahan hitāya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.18"><label>ci.18.18</label> pralipya dārvīmatha lākṣayā vā
            prataptayā svedanamasya kāryam | nipātya vā śastramapohya medo dahet supakvaṃ
            tvathavā vidārya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.19"><label>ci.18.19</label> prakṣālya mūtreṇa tilaiḥ
            supiṣṭaiḥ suvarcikādyair haritālamiśraiḥ | sasaindhavaiḥ
            kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhaiḥ kṣārottarair enam abhipraśodhya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.20"><label>ci.18.20</label> tailaṃ
            vidadyāddvikarañjaguñjāvaṃśāvalekheṅgudamūtrasiddham | jīmūtakaiḥ
            kośavatīphalaiś ca dantīdravantītrivṛtāsu caiva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.21"><label>ci.18.21</label> sarpiḥ kṛtaṃ hantyapacīṃ
            pravṛddhāṃ dvidhā pravṛttaṃ tadudāravīryam | nirguṇḍijātībarihiṣṭhayuktaṃ
            jīmūtakaṃ mākṣikasaindhavāḍhyam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.22"><label>ci.18.22</label> abhiprataptaṃ vamanaṃ pragāḍhaṃ
            duṣṭāpacīṣūttamamādiśanti | kaiḍaryabimbīkaravīrasiddhaṃ tailaṃ hitaṃ
            mūrdhavirecanaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.23"><label>ci.18.23</label> śāsvoṭakasya svarasena siddhaṃ
            tailaṃ hitaṃ nasyavirecaneṣu | madhūkasāraś ca hito 'vapīḍe phalāni śigroḥ
            kharamañjarervā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.24"><label>ci.18.24</label>
            granthīnamarmaprabhavānapakvānuddhṛtya cāgniṃ vidadhīta paścāt | kṣāreṇa
            vā 'pi pratisārayet tu saṃlikhya śastreṇa yathopadeśam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.25"><label>ci.18.25</label> pārṣṇi prati dve daśa cāṅgulāni
            mitvendrabastiṃ parivarjya dhīmān | vidārya matsyāṇḍanibhāni vaidyo niṣkṛṣya
            jālānyanalaṃ vidadhyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.26"><label>ci.18.26</label> ā gulphakarṇāt sumitasya
            jantostasyāṣṭabhāgaṃ khuḍakādvibhajya | ghoṇarjuvedhaḥ
            surarājabasterhitvā 'kṣimātraṃ tvapare vadanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.27"><label>ci.18.27</label> maṇibandhopariṣṭādvā kuryād
            rekhātrayaṃ bhiṣak | aṅgulyantaritaṃ samyagapacīnāṃ nivṛttaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.28"><label>ci.18.28</label> cūrṇasya kāle
            parcalākakākagodhāhikūrmaprabhavāṃ masīṃ tu | dadyāc ca tailena saheṅgudīnāṃ
            yadvakṣyate ślīpadināṃ ca tailam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.29"><label>ci.18.29</label> virecanaṃ dhūmamupādadīta
            bhavec ca nityaṃ yavamudgabhojī |
            karkārukair vārukanāsirkelapriyālapañcāṅgulabījacūrṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.30"><label>ci.18.30</label> vātārbudaṃ
            kṣīraghṛtāmbusiddhair uṣṇaiḥ satailair upanāhayet tu | kuryācca
            mukhyānyupanāhanāni siddhaiś ca māṃsair atha vesavāraiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.31"><label>ci.18.31</label> svedaṃ vidadhyāt kuśalas tu nāḍyā
            śṛṅgeṇa raktaṃ bahuśo harec ca | vātaghnaniryūhapayomlabhāgaiḥ siddhaṃ
            śatākhyaṃ trivṛtaṃ pibedvā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.32"><label>ci.18.32</label> svedopanāhā mṛdavas tu <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>kāryāḥ pittārbude
            kāyavirecanaṃ ca | vighṛṣya codumbaraśākagojīpatrairbhṛśaṃ kṣaudrayutaiḥ
            pralimpet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.33"><label>ci.18.33</label> ślakṣṇīkṛtaiḥ
            sarjarasapriyaṅgupattaṅgarodhrāñjanayaṣṭikāhvaiḥ | visrāvya
            cāragvadhāgojisomāḥ śyāmā ca yojyā kuśalena lepe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.34"><label>ci.18.34</label> śyāmāgirihvāñjanakīraseṣu
            drākṣārase saptalikārase ca | ghṛtaṃ pibet klītakasaṃprasiddhaṃ pittārbudī
            tajjaṭharī ca jantuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.35"><label>ci.18.35</label> śuddhasya jantoḥ kaphaje 'rbude tu
            rakte 'vasikte tu tato 'rbudaṃ tat | dravyāṇi yānyūrdhvamadhaś ca doṣān haranti
            taiḥ kalkakṛtaiḥ pradihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.36"><label>ci.18.36</label> kapotapārāvataviṅvimiśraiḥ
            sakāṃsyanīlaiḥ śukalāṅgalākhyaiḥ | mūtrais tu kākādanimūlamiśraiḥ
            kṣārapradigdhair athavā pradihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.37"><label>ci.18.37</label>
            niṣpāvapiṇyākakulatthakalkairmāṃsapragāḍhairdadhimastuyuktaiḥ | lepaṃ
            vidadhyāt kṛmayo yathā 'tra mūrcchanti muñcantyatha makṣikāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.38"><label>ci.18.38</label> alpāvaśiṣṭe kṛmibhakṣite<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> ca likhettato 'gniṃ vidadhīta
            paścāt | yadalpamūlaṃ traputāmrasīsapaṭṭaiḥ samāveṣṭya tadāyasair vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.39"><label>ci.18.39</label> kṣārāgniśastrāṇyasakṛdvidadhyāt
            prāṇānahiṃsan bhiṣagpramattaḥ | āsphotajātīkaravīrapatraiḥ kaṣāyamiṣṭaṃ
            vraṇaśodhanārtham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.40"><label>ci.18.40</label> śuddhe ca tailaṃ vidadhīta
            bhārgīviḍaṅgapāṭhātriphalāvipakvam | yadṛcchayā copagatāni pākaṃ
            pākakrameṇopacaredvidhijñaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.41"><label>ci.18.41</label> medorbudaṃ svinnamatho vidārya
            viśodhya sīvyedgataraktamāśu | tato haridrāgṛhadhūmarodhrapataṅgacūrṇaiḥ
            samanaḥ śilālaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.42"><label>ci.18.42</label> vraṇaṃ pratigrāhya
            madhupragāḍhaiḥ karañjatailaṃ vidadhīta śuddhe | saśeṣadoṣāṇi hi yo 'rbudāni
            karoti tasyāśu punarbhavanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.43"><label>ci.18.43</label> tasmādaśeṣāṇi samuddharettu
            hanyuḥ saśeṣāṇi yathā hi vahniḥ | saṃsvedya gaṇḍaṃ pavanotthamādau
            nāḍyā 'nilaghnauṣadhapatrabhaṅgaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.44"><label>ci.18.44</label> amlaiḥ samūtrairvividhaiḥ
            payobhiruṣṇaiḥ satailaiḥ piśitaiś ca vidvān | visrāvayet svinnamatandriyaśca
            śuddhaṃ vraṇaṃ cāpy upanāhayet tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.45"><label>ci.18.45</label>
            śaṇātasīmūlakaśigrukiṇvapriyālamajjānuyutais tilais tu |
            kālāmṛtāśigrupunarnavārkagajādināmākarahāṭakuṣṭhaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.46"><label>ci.18.46</label> ekaiṣikāvṛkṣakatilvakaiśca
            surāmlapiṣṭair asakṛt pradihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.47"><label>ci.18.47</label> tailaṃ
            pibeccāmṛtavallinimbahaṃsāhvayāvṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ | siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ ca
            sadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.48"><label>ci.18.48</label> svedopanāhaiḥ kaphasaṃbhavaṃ tu
            saṃsvedaya visrāvaṇam eva kuryāt |
            tato 'jagandhātiviṣāviśalyāviṣāṇikākuṣṭhaśukāhvayābhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.49"><label>ci.18.49</label> palāśabhasmodakapeṣitābhirdihyāt
            suguñjābhiraśītalābhiḥ | daśārdhasaṅkhyairlavaṇaiś ca yuktaṃ tailaṃ
            pibenmāgadhikādisiddham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.50"><label>ci.18.50</label> pracchardanaṃ mūrdhavirecanaṃ ca
            dhūmaś ca vairecaniko hitas tu | pākakramo vā 'pi sadā vidheyo vaidyena
            pākaṅgatayoḥ kathañcit || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.51"><label>ci.18.51</label> kaṭutrikakṣaudrayutāḥ samūtrā
            bhakṣyā yavānnāni rasāś ca maudgāḥ | saśṛṅgaverāḥ sapaṭolanimbā hitāya deyā
            galagaṇḍaroge || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.52"><label>ci.18.52</label> medaḥsamutthe tu yathopadiṣṭāṃ
            vidhyet sirāṃ snigdhatanornarasya | śyāmāsudhālohapurīṣadantīrasāñjanaiścāpi
            hitaḥ pradehaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.53"><label>ci.18.53</label> mūtreṇa vā+āloḍya hitāya sāraṃ
            prātaḥ pibet sālamahīruhāṇām | śastreṇa vā++āpāṭya vidārya cainaṃ medaḥ
            samuddhṛtya hitāya sīvyet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.54"><label>ci.18.54</label> majjājyamedomadhubhirdahedvā
            dagdhe ca sarpirmadhu cāvacāryam | kāsīsatutthe ca tato 'tra deye cūrṇīkṛte
            rocanayā samete || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.18.55"><label>ci.18.55</label> tailena cābhyajya hitāya dadyāt
            sārodbhavaṃ gomayajaṃ ca bhasma | hitaś ca nityaṃ triphalākaṣāyo gāḍhaś ca
            bandho yavabhojanaṃ ca ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
            granthyapacyarbudagalagaṇḍacikitsitaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||18 ||</p>

        <div n="19" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>ekonaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.1"><label>ci.19.1</label> athāto
            vṛddhyupadaṃśaślīpadacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.2"><label>ci.19.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.3"><label>ci.19.3</label> antravṛddhyā vinā ṣaḍyā
            vṛddhayastāsu varjayet | aśvādiyānaṃ vyāyāmaṃ maithunaṃ veganigraham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.4"><label>ci.19.4</label> atyāsanaṃ caṅkramaṇam upavāsaṃ
            gurūṇi ca | tatrādito vātavṛddhau traivṛtasnigdhamāturam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.5"><label>ci.19.5</label> svinnaṃ cainaṃ yathānyāyaṃ pāyayeta
            virecanam | kośāmratilvakair aṇḍaphalatailāni vā naram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.6"><label>ci.19.6</label> sakṣīraṃ vā pibenmāsaṃ
            tailameraṇḍasaṃbhavam | tataḥ kāle 'nilaghnānāṃ kvāthaiḥ kalkaiś ca buddhimān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.7"><label>ci.19.7</label> nirūhayennirūḍhaṃ ca bhuktavantaṃ
            rasaudanam | yaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena tatastailena yojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.8"><label>ci.19.8</label> snehopanāhau kuryācca
            pradehāṃścānilāpahān | vidagdhāṃ pācayitvā vā sevanīṃ parivarjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.9"><label>ci.19.9</label> bhindyāttataḥ prabhinnāyāṃ
            yathoktaṃ kramamācaret | pittajāyāmapakvāyāṃ pittagranthikramo hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.10"><label>ci.19.10</label> pakvāṃ vā bhedayedbhinnāṃ
            śodhayet kṣaudrasarpiṣā | śuddhāyāṃ ca bhiṣagdadyāttailaṃ kalkaṃ ca ropaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.11"><label>ci.19.11</label> raktajāyāṃ jalaukobhiḥ <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>śoṇitaṃ nirharedbhiṣak |
            pibedvirecanaṃ vā 'pi śarkarākṣaudrasaṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.12"><label>ci.19.12</label> pittagranthikramaṃ kuryādāme
            pakve ca sarvadā | vṛddhiṃ kaphātmikāmuṣṇairmūtrapiṣṭaiḥ pralepayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.13"><label>ci.19.13</label> pītadārukaṣāyaṃ ca pibenmūtreṇa
            saṃyutam | vimlāpanādṛte vā 'pi śleṣmagranthikramo hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.14"><label>ci.19.14</label> pakvāyāṃ ca vibhinnāyāṃ tailaṃ
            śodhanamiṣyate | sumanāruṣkarāṅkoṭhasaptaparṇeṣu sādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.15"><label>ci.19.15</label> medaḥsamutthāṃ saṃsvedya lepayet
            surasādinā | śirovirekadravyair vā sukhoṣṇairmūtrasaṃyutaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.16"><label>ci.19.16</label> svinnāṃ cāveṣṭya paṭṭena
            samāśvāsya tu mānavam | rakṣan phale sevanīṃ ca vṛddhipatreṇa dārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.17"><label>ci.19.17</label> medastataḥ samuddhṛtya dadyāt
            kāsīsasaindhave | badhnīyāc ca yathoddiṣṭaṃ śuddhe tailaṃ ca dāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.18"><label>ci.19.18</label> manaḥśilālalavaṇaiḥ
            siddhamāruṣkareṣu ca | mūtrajāṃ svedayitvā tu vastrapaṭṭena veṣṭayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.19"><label>ci.19.19</label> sevanyāḥ pārśvato 'dhastādvidhyed
            vrīhimukhena tu | athātra dvimukhāṃ nāḍīṃ dattvā visrāvayedbhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.20"><label>ci.19.20</label> mūtraṃ nāḍīmathoddhṛtya
            sthagikābandhamācaret | śuddhāyāṃ ropaṇaṃ dadyādvarjayedantrahaitukīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.21"><label>ci.19.21</label> aprāptaphalakoṣāyāṃ
            vātavṛddhikramo hitaḥ | tatra yā vaṅkhaṇasthā <ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref>tāṃ dahedardhenduvattrayā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.22"><label>ci.19.22</label> samyaṅmārgāvarodhārthaṃ
            kośaprāptāṃ tu varjayet | tvacaṃ bhittvā 'ṅguṣṭhamadhye daheccāṅgaviparyayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.23"><label>ci.19.23</label> anenaiva vidhānena vṛddhī
            vātakaphātmike | pradahet prayataḥ kiṃtu snāyucchedo 'dhikastayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.24"><label>ci.19.24</label> śaṅkhopari ca karṇānte tyaktvā
            yatnena sevanīm | vyatyāsādvā sirāṃ vidhyedantravṛddhinivṛttaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.25"><label>ci.19.25</label> upadaṃśeṣu sādhyeṣu
            snigdhasvinnasya dehinaḥ | sirāṃ vidhyenmeḍhramadhye pātayedvā jalaukasaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.26"><label>ci.19.26</label> haredubhayataścāpi
            doṣānatyarthamucchritān | sadyo 'pahṛtadoṣasya rukśophāvupaśāmyataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.27"><label>ci.19.27</label> yadi vā durbalo janturna vā
            prāptaṃ virecanam | nirūheṇa harettasya doṣānatyarthamucchritān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.28"><label>ci.19.28</label>
            prapauṇḍarīkayaṣṭyāhvavarṣābhūkuṣṭhadārubhiḥ | saralāgururāsnābhirvātajaṃ
            saṃpralepayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.29"><label>ci.19.29</label> niculair aṇḍabījāni
            yavagodhūmasaktavaḥ | etaiś ca vātajaṃ snigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇaiḥ saṃpralepayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.30"><label>ci.19.30</label> prapauṇḍarīkapūrvaiś ca dravyaiḥ
            sekaḥ praśasyate | gaurikāñjanayaṣṭyāhvārivośīrapadmakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.31"><label>ci.19.31</label> sacandanotpalaiḥ snigdhaiḥ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.32"><label>ci.19.32</label> sarpiḥsnigdhaiḥ samadhukaiḥ
            paittikaṃ saṃpralepayet | secayec ca ghṛtakṣīraśarkarekṣuadhūdakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.33"><label>ci.19.33</label> athavā 'pi suśītena kaṣāyeṇa
            vaṭādinā | sālāśvakarṇājakarṇadhavatvagbhiḥ kaphotthitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.34"><label>ci.19.34</label> surāpiṣṭābhiruṣṇābhiḥ satailābhiḥ
            pralepayet | rajanyativiṣāmustāsurāsuradārubhiḥ<ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.35"><label>ci.19.35</label> saptrapāṭhāpattūrair athavā
            saṃpralepayet | surasāragvadhādyoś ca kvāthābhyāṃ paribecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.36"><label>ci.19.36</label> evaṃ
            saṃśodhanālepasekaśoṇitamokṣaṇaiḥ | pratikuryāt kriyāyogaiḥ
            prāksthānoktairhitair api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.37"><label>ci.19.37</label> na yāti ca yathā pākaṃ prayateta
            tathā bhiṣak | vidagdhais tu sirāsnāyutvaṅmāṃsaiḥ kṣīyate dhvajaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.38"><label>ci.19.38</label> śastreṇopacareccāpi
            pākamāgatamāśu vai | tadā 'pohya tilaiḥ sarpiḥkṣaudrayuktaiḥ pralepayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.39"><label>ci.19.39</label> karavīrasya patrāṇi
            jātyāragvadhayos tathā | prakṣālane prayojyāni vaijayantyarkayorapi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.40"><label>ci.19.40</label> saurāṣṭrīṃ gairikaṃ tutthaṃ
            puṣpakāsīsasaindhavam | rodhraṃ rasāñjanaṃ dārvīṃ haritālaṃ manaḥśilām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.41"><label>ci.19.41</label> hareṇukaile ca tathā

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.42"><label>ci.19.42</label>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.44"><label>ci.19.44</label> asminneva kaṣāye tu tailaṃ dhīro

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.45"><label>ci.19.45</label> etat sarvopadaṃśeṣu śreṣṭhaṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.46"><label>ci.19.46</label> manaḥśilāsamaiścūrṇaṃ
            vraṇavīsśarpanāśanam | gundrāṃ dagdhvā kṛtaṃ bhasma haritālaṃ manaḥśilā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.47"><label>ci.19.47</label> upadaṃśabisarpāṇāmetacchantikaraṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.48"><label>ci.19.48</label> upadaṃśaṃ nihantyeṣa

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.49"><label>ci.19.49</label> tayoreva ca yā yogyā vīkṣya

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.50"><label>ci.19.50</label> duṣṭavraṇavidhiṃ kuryāt kuthitaṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.52"><label>ci.19.52</label> snehasvedopapanne tu

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.54"><label>ci.19.54</label>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.56"><label>ci.19.56</label> sirāṃ suviditāṃ vidhyedaṅguṣṭhe

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.57"><label>ci.19.57</label> pibedvā 'pyabhayākalkaṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.60"><label>ci.19.60</label> pibet sarṣapatailaṃ vā ślīpadānāṃ
            nivṛttaye | pūtīkarañjapatrāṇāṃ rasaṃ vā 'pi yathābalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.61"><label>ci.19.61</label> anenaiva vidhānena
            putrañjīvakajaṃ rasam | prayuñjīta bhiṣak prājñaḥ kālasātmyavibhāgavit || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.62"><label>ci.19.62</label> kevukākandaniryāsaṃ lavaṇaṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.63"><label>ci.19.63</label> kākādanīṃ kākajaṅghāṃ bṛhatīṃ
            kaṇṭakārikām | kadambapuṣpīṃ mandārīṃ lambāṃ śukanasāṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.64"><label>ci.19.64</label> dagdhvā mūtreṇa tadbhasma
            srāvayet kṣārakalpavat | tatra dadyāt pratīvāpaṃ kākodumbarikārasam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.65"><label>ci.19.65</label> madanāc ca phalāt kvāthaṃ
            śukākhyasvarasaṃ tathā | eṣa kṣāras tu pānīyaḥ ślīpadaṃ hanti sevitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.66"><label>ci.19.66</label> apacīṃ galagaṇḍaṃ ca
            grahaṇīdoṣam eva ca | bhaktasyānaśanaṃ caiva hanyāt sarvaviṣāṇi ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.67"><label>ci.19.67</label> eṣveva tailaṃ saṃsiddhaṃ
            nasyābhyaṅgeṣu pūjitam | etānevāmayān hanti ye ca duṣṭavraṇā nṛṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.68"><label>ci.19.68</label> dravantīṃ trivṛtāṃ dantīṃ nīlīṃ
            śyāmāṃ tathaiva ca | saptalāṃ śaṅkhinīṃ caiva dagdhvā mūtreṇa gālayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.19.69"><label>ci.19.69</label> dadyāc ca triphalākvāthameṣa
            kṣāras tu sādhitaḥ | adho gacchati pītas tu pūrvaiścāpyāśiṣaḥ samāḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.37"><label>ci.20.37</label> yauvane piḍakāsveṣa

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.38"><label>ci.20.38</label> kustumburuvacālodhrakuṣṭharvā
            lepanaṃ hitam | padminīkaṇṭake roge chardayennimbavāriṇā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.39"><label>ci.20.39</label> tenaiva siddhaṃ sakṣaudraṃ
            sarpiḥpānaṃ pradāpayet | nimbāragvadhayoḥ kalko hita utsādane bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.40"><label>ci.20.40</label> parivṛttiṃ ghṛtābhyaktāṃ
            susvinnām upanāhayet | tato 'bhyajya śanaiścarma cānayet pīḍayenmaṇim || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.41"><label>ci.20.41</label> praviṣṭe ca maṇau carma
            svedayedupanāhanaiḥ | trirātraṃ pañcarātraṃ vā vātaghnaiḥ sālvaṇādibhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.42"><label>ci.20.42</label> dadyādvātaharān bastīn
            snigdhānyannāni bhojayet | vapāṭikāṃ jayedevaṃ yathādoṣaṃ cikitsakaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.43"><label>ci.20.43</label> niruddhaprakaśe nāḍīṃ
            lauhīmubhayatomukhīm | dāravīṃ vā jatukṛtāṃ ghṛtābhyaktāṃ praveśayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.44"><label>ci.20.44</label> pariṣeke
            vasāmajjaśiśumāravarāhayoḥ | cakratailaṃ tathā yojyaṃ
            vātaghnadravyasaṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.45"><label>ci.20.45</label> tryahāttryahāt sthūlatarāṃ
            samyaṅnāḍīṃ praveśayet | sroto vivardhayedevaṃ snigdhamannaṃ ca bhojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.46"><label>ci.20.46</label> bhittvā vā sevanīṃ muktvā
            sadyaḥkṣatavadācaret | sanniruddhagudaṃ rogaṃ valmīkaṃ vahnirohiṇīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.47"><label>ci.20.47</label> pratyākhyāya yathāyogaṃ
            cikitsitamathācaret | visarpoktena vidhinā sādhayedagnirohiṇīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.48"><label>ci.20.48</label> sanniruddhagude yojyā
            niruddhaprakaśakriyā | śastreṇotkṛtya valmīkaṃ kṣārāgnibhyāṃ prasādhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.49"><label>ci.20.49</label> vidhānenārbudoktena śodhayitvā ca
            ropayet | valmīkaṃ tu bhavedyasya nātivṛddhamamarmajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.50"><label>ci.20.50</label> tatra saṃśodhanaṃ kṛtvā śoṇitaṃ
            mokṣayedbhiṣak | kulatthikāyā mūlaiś ca guḍūcyā lavaṇena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.51"><label>ci.20.51</label> ārevatasya mūlaiśca
            dantīmūlais tathaiva ca | śyāmāmūlaiḥ sapalalaiḥ śaktumiśraiḥ pralepayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.52"><label>ci.20.52</label> susnigdhaiś ca sukhoṣṇaiśca
            bhiṣak tam upanāhayet | pakvaṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>vā tadvijānīyād gatīḥ sarvā yathākramam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.53"><label>ci.20.53</label> abhijñāya tataśchittvā
            pradahenmatimān bhiṣak | saṃśodhya duṣṭamāṃsāni kṣāreṇa pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.54"><label>ci.20.54</label> vraṇaṃ viśuddhaṃ vijñāya
            ropayenmatimān bhiṣak | sumanā granthayaścaiva bhallātakamanaḥśile || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.55"><label>ci.20.55</label> kālānusārī sūkṣmailā
            candanāguruṇī tathā | etaiḥ siddhaṃ nimbatailaṃ valmīke ropaṇaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.56"><label>ci.20.56</label> pāṇipādopariṣṭāttu
            chidrairbahubhirāvṛtam | valmīkaṃ yat saśophaṃ syād varjyaṃ tat tu vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.57"><label>ci.20.57</label> dhātryāḥ stanyaṃ śodhayitvā bāle
            sādhyā 'hipūtanā | paṭolapatratriphalārasāñjanavipācitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.58"><label>ci.20.58</label> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ nāśayati
            kṛcchrāmapyahipūtanām | triphalākolakhadirakaṣāyaṃ vraṇaropaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.59"><label>ci.20.59</label>
            kāsīsarocanātutthaharitālarasāñjanaiḥ | lepo 'mlapiṣṭo badarītvagvā
            saindhavasaṃyutā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.60"><label>ci.20.60</label> kapālatutthajaṃ cūrṇaṃ cūrṇakāle
            prayojayet | cikitsenmuṣkakacchūṃ cāpyahipūtanapāmavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.61"><label>ci.20.61</label> gudabhraṃśe gudaṃ svinnaṃ
            snehābhyaktaṃ praveśayet | kārayedgophaṇābandhaṃ madhyacchidreṇa carmaṇā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.62"><label>ci.20.62</label> vinirgamārthaṃ vāyoś ca svedayecca
            muhurmuhuḥ | kṣīre mahatpañcamūlaṃ mūṣikāṃ cāntravarjitām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.20.63"><label>ci.20.63</label> paktvā tasmin pacetailaṃ
            vātaghnauṣadhasaṃyutam | gudabhraṃśamidaṃ kṛcchraṃ pānābhyaṅgāt
            prasādhayet ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne kṣudrarogacikitsitaṃ nāma
            viṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||20 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="21" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>ekaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.1"><label>ci.21.1</label> athātaḥ śūkadoṣacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.2"><label>ci.21.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.3"><label>ci.21.3</label> saṃlikhya sarṣapīṃ samyak kaṣāyair
            avacūrṇayet | kaṣāyeṣveva tailaṃ ca kurvīta vraṇaropaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.4"><label>ci.21.4</label> aṣṭhīlikāṃ
              jalaukobhirgrāhayecca<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>
            punaḥ punaḥ | tathā cānupaśāmyantīṃ kaphagranthivaduddharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.5"><label>ci.21.5</label> svedayedgrathitaṃ śaśvannāḍīsvedena
            buddhimān | sukhoṣṇair upanāhaiś ca susnigdhair upanāhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.6"><label>ci.21.6</label> kumbhīkāṃ pākamāpannāṃ
            bhindyācchuddhāṃ tu ropayet | tailena triphalālodhratindukāmrātakena tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.7"><label>ci.21.7</label> grāhayitvā jalaukobhiralajīṃ
            secayettataḥ | kaṣāyais teṣu siddhaṃ ca tailaṃ ropaṇamiṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.8"><label>ci.21.8</label> balātailena koṣṇena mṛditaṃ
            pariṣecayet | bhadhuraiḥ sarpiṣā snigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇair upanāhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.9"><label>ci.21.9</label> saṃmūḍhapiḍakāṃ kṣipraṃ
            jalaukobhirupācaret | bhittvā paryāgatāṃ cāpi lepayet kṣaudrasarpiṣā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.10"><label>ci.21.10</label> avamanthe gate pākaṃ bhinne
            tailaṃ vidhīyate | dhavāśvakarṇapattaṅgasallakītindukīkṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.11"><label>ci.21.11</label> kriyāṃ puṣkarikāyāṃ tu śītāṃ
            sarvāṃ prayojayet | jalaukobhirhareccāsṛk sarpiṣā cāvasecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.12"><label>ci.21.12</label> sparśahānyāṃ haredraktaṃ
            pradihyānmadhurair api | kṣīrekṣurasarpirbhir secayec ca suśītalaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.13"><label>ci.21.13</label> piḍakāmuttamākhyāṃ ca
            baḍiśenoddharedbhiṣak | uddhṛtya madhusaṃyuktaiḥ kaṣāyair avacūrṇayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.14"><label>ci.21.14</label> rasakriyā vidhātavyā likhite
            śataponake | pṛthakparṇyādisiddhaṃ ca deyaṃ tailamanantaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.15"><label>ci.21.15</label> kriyāṃ kuryād bhiṣak
            prājñastvakpākasya visarpavat | raktavidradhivac cāpi kriyā śoṇitaje 'rbude || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.16"><label>ci.21.16</label> kaṣāyakalkasarpīṃṣi tailaṃ cūrṇaṃ
            rasakriyām | śodhanaṃ ropaṇaṃ caiva vīkṣya vīkṣyāvacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.17"><label>ci.21.17</label> hitaṃ ca sarpiṣaḥ pānaṃ pathyaṃ
            cāpi cirecanam | hitaḥ śoṇitamokṣaś ca yac cāpi laghu bhojanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.21.18"><label>ci.21.18</label> arbudaṃ māṃsapākaṃ ca vidradhiṃ
            tilakālakam | pratyākhyāya prakurvīta bhiṣak samyak pratikriyām ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne śūkarogacikitsitaṃ
            nāmaikaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||21 ||</p>

        <div n="22" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>dvāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.1"><label>ci.22.1</label> athāto mukharogacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.2"><label>ci.22.2</label> yathovaca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.3"><label>ci.22.3</label> caturvidhena snehena
            madhūcchiṣṭayutena ca | vātaje 'bhyañjanaṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref>kuryānnāḍīsvedaṃ ca buddhimān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.4"><label>ci.22.4</label> vidadhyādoṣṭhakope tu sālvaṇaṃ
            copanāhane | mastiṣke caiva nasye ca tailaṃ vātaharaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.5"><label>ci.22.5</label> śrīveṣṭakaṃ sarjarasaṃ suradāru
            saguggulu | yaṣṭīmadhukacūrṇaṃ tu vidadhyāt pratisāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.6"><label>ci.22.6</label> pittaraktābhighātotthaṃ
            jalaukobhirupācaret | pittavidradhivac cāpi kriyāṃ kuryād aśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.7"><label>ci.22.7</label> śirovirecanaṃ dhūmaḥ svedaḥ kavala
            eva ca | hṛte rakte prayoktavyamoṣṭhakope kaphātmake || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.8"><label>ci.22.8</label> tryūṣaṇaṃ svarjikākṣāro yavakṣāro
            viḍaṃ tathā | kṣaudrayuktaṃ vidhātavyametac ca pratisāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.9"><label>ci.22.9</label> medoje svedite bhinne śodhite
            jvalano hitaḥ | priyaṅgutriphalālodhraṃ sakṣaudraṃ pratisāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.10"><label>ci.22.10</label> etadoṣṭhaprakopānāṃ sādhyānāṃ
            karma kīrtitam | dantamūlagatānāṃ tu rogāṇāṃ<ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref> karma vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.11"><label>ci.22.11</label> śītāde hṛtarakte tu toye
            nāgarasarṣapān | niṣkvāthya triphalāṃ mustaṃ gaṇḍūṣaḥ sarasāñjanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.12"><label>ci.22.12</label> priyaṅgavaś ca mustaṃ ca triphalā
            ca pralepanam | nasyaṃ ca triphalāsiddhaṃ madhukotpalapadmakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.13"><label>ci.22.13</label> dantapuppuṭake kāryaṃ taruṇe
            raktamokṣaṇam | sapañcalavaṇaḥ kṣāraḥ sakṣaudraḥ pratisāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.14"><label>ci.22.14</label> hitaḥ śirovirekaś ca nasyaṃ
            snigdhaṃ ca bhojanam | visrāvite dantaveṣṭe vraṇāṃs tu pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.15"><label>ci.22.15</label>
            rodhrapattaṅgayaṣṭyāhvalākṣācūrṇairmadhūttaraiḥ | gaṇḍūṣe kṣīriṇo yojyāḥ
            sakṣaudraghṛtaśarkarāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.16"><label>ci.22.16</label> kākolyādau daśakṣīrasiddhaṃ
            sarpiś ca nasyataḥ | śauṣire hṛtarakte tu rodhramustarasāñjanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.17"><label>ci.22.17</label> sakṣaudraiḥ śasyate lepo gaṇḍūṣe
            kṣīriṇo hitāḥ | <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>sārivotpalayaṣṭyāhvasāvarāgurucandanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.18"><label>ci.22.18</label> kṣīre daśaguṇe siddhaṃ
            sarpirnasye ca pūjitam | kriyāṃ paridare kuyācchītākoktāṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.19"><label>ci.22.19</label> saṃśodhyobhayataḥ kāryaṃ
            śiraścopakuśe tathā | kākodumbarikāgojīpatrairvisrāvayedasṛk || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.20"><label>ci.22.20</label> kṣaudrayuktaiś ca lavaṇaiḥ
            savyoṣaiḥ pratisārayet | pippalīḥ sarṣapāñ śvetānnāgaraṃ naiculaṃ phalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.21"><label>ci.22.21</label> sukhodakena saṃsṛjya kavalaṃ cāpi
            dhārayet | ghṛtaṃ madhurakaiḥ siddhaṃ hitaṃ kavalanasyayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.22"><label>ci.22.22</label> śastreṇa<ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref> dantavaidarbhe dantamūlāni
            śodhayet | tataḥ ksāraṃ prayuñjīta kriyāḥ sarvāś ca śītalāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.23"><label>ci.22.23</label> uddhṛtyādhikadantaṃ tu
            tato 'gnimavacārayet | kṛmidantakavac cāpi vidhiḥ kāryo vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.24"><label>ci.22.24</label> chittvā 'dhimāṃsaṃ
            sakṣaudrairebhiścūrṇair upācaret | vacātejovatīpāṭhāsvarjikāyāvaśūkajaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.25"><label>ci.22.25</label> kṣaudradvitīyāḥ pippalyaḥ
            kavalaścātra kīrtitaḥ | paṭolatriphalānimbakaṣāyaścātra dhāvane | hitaḥ
            śirovirekaś ca dhūmo vairecanaś ca yaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.26"><label>ci.22.26</label> sāmānyaṃ karma nāḍīnāṃ viśeṣaṃ
            cātra me śṛṇu | nāḍīvraṇaharaṃ karma dantanāḍīṣu kārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.27"><label>ci.22.27</label> yaṃ <ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref>dantam abhijāyeta nāḍī taṃ
            dantamuddharet | chittvā māṃsāni śastreṇa yadi noparijo bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.28"><label>ci.22.28</label> śodhayitvā dahec cāpi kṣāreṇa
            jvalanena vā | bhinattyupekṣite dante hanukāsthi gatirdhruvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.29"><label>ci.22.29</label> samūlaṃ daśanaṃ

              footnote marker">*</ref>samūle sthirabandhane || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.30"><label>ci.22.30</label> raktātiyogāt pūrvektā rogā ghorā
            bhavanti hi | kāṇaḥ saṃjāyate janturarditaṃ cāsya jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.31"><label>ci.22.31</label> calamapyuttaraṃ dantamato
            nāpaharedbhiṣak | dhāvane jātimadanasvādukaṇṭakakhādiram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.32"><label>ci.22.32</label> kaṣāyaṃ
            jātimadanakaṭukasvādukaṇṭakaiḥ | yaṣṭyāhvarodhramañjiṣṭhākhadiraiś cāpi yat
            kṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.33"><label>ci.22.33</label> tailaṃ saṃśodhanaṃ taddhi

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.34"><label>ci.22.34</label> snehānāṃ kavalāḥ koṣṇāḥ
            sarpiṣastraivṛtasya vā | niryūhāścānilaghnānāṃ dantaharṣapramardanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.35"><label>ci.22.35</label> snaihikaś ca hito dhūmo nasyaṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.36"><label>ci.22.36</label> śirobastirhitaś cāpi kramo
            yaścānilāpahaḥ | ahiṃsan dantamūlāni śarkarāmuddharedbhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.37"><label>ci.22.37</label> lākṣācūrṇairmadhuyutais tatastāḥ
            pratisārayet | dantaharṣakriyāṃ cāpi kuryānniravaśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.38"><label>ci.22.38</label> kapālikā kṛcchratamā tatrāpyeṣā
            kriyā hitā | jayedvisrāvaṇaiḥ svinnamacalaṃ kṛmidantakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.39"><label>ci.22.39</label> tathā 'vapīḍair vātaghnaiḥ
            snehagaṇḍūṣadhāraṇaiḥ | bhadradārvādivarṣābhūlepaiḥ snigdhaiś ca bhojanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.40"><label>ci.22.40</label> calamuddhṛtya<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> ca sthānaṃ vidahet suṣirasya
            ca | tato vidārīyaṣṭyāhvaśṛṅgāṭakakaserukaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.41"><label>ci.22.41</label> tailaṃ daśaguṇe kṣīre siddhaṃ
            nasye hitaṃ bhavet | hanomokṣe samuddiṣṭāṃ kuryāccārditavat kriyām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.42"><label>ci.22.42</label> phalānyamlāni śītāmbu rūkṣānnaṃ
            dantadhāvanam | tathā 'tikaṭhinān bhakṣyān dantarogī vivarjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.43"><label>ci.22.43</label> sādhyānāṃ dantarogāṇāṃ
            cikitsitamudīritam | jihvāgatānāṃ sādhyānāṃ karma vakṣyāmi siddhaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.44"><label>ci.22.44</label> auṣṭhaprakope 'nilaje yaduktaṃ
            prāk cikitsitam | kaṇṭakeṣv anilottheṣu tat kāryaṃ bhiṣajā bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.45"><label>ci.22.45</label> pittajeṣu vighṛṣṭeṣu niḥsṛte
            duṣṭaśoṇite | pratisāraṇagaṇḍūṣaṃ nasyaṃ ca madhuraṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.46"><label>ci.22.46</label> kaṇṭakeṣu kaphottheṣu
            likhiteṣv asṛjaḥ kṣaye | pippalyādirmadhuyutaḥ kāryas tu pratisāraṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.47"><label>ci.22.47</label> gṛhṇīyāt kavalāṃścāpi
            gaurasarṣapasaindhavaiḥ | paṭolanimbavārtākukṣārayūṣaiś ca bhojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.48"><label>ci.22.48</label> upajihvāṃ tu saṃlikhya kṣāreṇa
            pratisārayet | śirovirekagaṇḍūṣadhūmaiścainamupācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.49"><label>ci.22.49</label> jihvāgatānāṃ karmoktaṃ tālavyānāṃ
            pravakṣyate | aṅguṣṭhāṅgulisaṃdaṃśenākṛṣya galaśuṇḍikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.50"><label>ci.22.50</label> chedayenmaṇḍalāgreṇa jihvopari tu
            saṃsthitām | notkṛṣṭaṃ caiva hīnaṃ ca tribhāgaṃ chedayedbhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.51"><label>ci.22.51</label> atyādānāt sravedraktaṃ
            tannimittaṃ mriyeta ca | hīnacchedādbhavecchopho lālā nidrā bhramastamaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.52"><label>ci.22.52</label> tasmādvaidyaḥ prayatnena
            dṛṣṭakarmā viśāradaḥ | galaśuṇḍīṃ tu sañchidya kuryāt prāptamimaṃ kramam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.53"><label>ci.22.53</label>
            maricātiviṣāpāṭhāvacākuṣṭhakuṭannaṭaiḥ | kṣaudrayuktaiḥ salavaṇais tatastāṃ
            pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.54"><label>ci.22.54</label> vacāmativiṣāṃ pāṭhāṃ rāsnāṃ
            kaṭukarohiṇīm | niṣkvāthya picumandaṃ ca kavalaṃ tatra yojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.55"><label>ci.22.55</label>
            iṅgudīkiṇihīdantīsaralāsuradārubhiḥ | pañcāṅgīṃ kārayet piṣṭairvartiṃ
            gandhottarāṃ śubhām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.56"><label>ci.22.56</label> tato dhūmaṃ pibejjanturdvirahnaḥ
            kaphanāśanam | kṣārasiddheṣu mudgeṣu yūṣaścāpyaśane hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.57"><label>ci.22.57</label> tuṇḍikeryadhruṣe kūrme saṅghāte
            tālupuppuṭe | eṣa eva vidhiḥ kāryo viśeṣaḥ śastrakarmaṇi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.58"><label>ci.22.58</label> tālupāke tu kartavyaṃ vidhānaṃ
            pittanāśanam | snehasvedau tāluśoṣe vidhiścānilanāśanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.59"><label>ci.22.59</label> kīrtitaṃ tālujānāṃ tu kaṇṭhyānāṃ
            karma vakṣyate | sādhyānāṃ rohiṇīnāṃ tu hitaṃ śoṇitamokṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.60"><label>ci.22.60</label> chardanaṃ dhūmapānaṃ ca gaṇḍūṣo
            nasyakarma ca | vātikīṃ tu hṛte rakte lavaṇaiḥ pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.61"><label>ci.22.61</label> sukhoṣṇān snehagaṇḍūṣān
            dhārayeccāpyabhīkṣṇaśaḥ | pataṅgaśarkarākṣaudraiḥ paittikīṃ pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.62"><label>ci.22.62</label> drākṣāparūṣakakvātho hitaśca
            kavalagrahe | agāradhūmakaṭukaiḥ ślaiṣmikīṃ pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.63"><label>ci.22.63</label> śvetāviḍaṅgadantīṣu tailaṃ
            siddhaṃ sasaindhavam | nasyakarmaṇi yoktavyaṃ tathā kavaladhāraṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.64"><label>ci.22.64</label> pittavat sādhayedvaidyo rohiṇīṃ
            raktasaṃbhavām | visrāvya kaṇṭhaśālūkaṃ sādhayettuṇḍikerivat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.65"><label>ci.22.65</label> ekakālaṃ yavānnaṃ ca bhuñjīta
            snigdhamalpaśaḥ | upajihvikavac cāpi sādhayedadhijihvikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.66"><label>ci.22.66</label> ekavṛndaṃ tu visrāvya vidhiṃ
            śodhanamācaret | gilāyuś cāpi yo vyādhistaṃ ca śastreṇa sādhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.67"><label>ci.22.67</label> amarmasthaṃ supakvaṃ ca
            bhedayedgalavidradhim | vātāt sarvasaraṃ cūrṇairlavaṇaiḥ pratisārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.68"><label>ci.22.68</label> tailaṃ vātaharaiḥ siddhaṃ hitaṃ
            kavalanasyayoḥ | tato 'smai snaihikaṃ dhūmamimaṃ dadyādvicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.69"><label>ci.22.69</label> śālarājādanair
            aṇḍasāraiṅgudamadhūkajāḥ | majjāno gugguludhyāmamāṃsīkālānusārivāḥ |
            śrīsarjarasaśaileyamadhūcchiṣṭāni cāharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.70"><label>ci.22.70</label> tatsarvaṃ sukṛtaṃ cūrṇaṃ
            snehenāloḍya yuktitaḥ | ṭiṇḍūkavṛntaṃ sakṣaudraṃ matimāṃstena lepayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.71"><label>ci.22.71</label> eṣa sarvasare dhūmaḥ praśastaḥ
            snaihiko mataḥ | kaphaghno mārutaghnaś ca mukharogavināśanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.72"><label>ci.22.72</label> pittātmake sarvasare
            śuddhakāyasya dehinaḥ | sarvaḥ pittaharaḥ kāryo vidhirmadhuraśītalaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.73"><label>ci.22.73</label> pratisāraṇagaṇḍūṣau dhūmaḥ
            saṃśodhanāni ca | kaphātmake sarvasare vidhiṃ kuryāt kaphāpaham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.74"><label>ci.22.74</label> pibedativiṣāṃ pāṭhāṃ mustaṃ ca
            suradāru ca | rohiṇīṃ kaṭukākhyāṃ ca kuṭajasya phalāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.75"><label>ci.22.75</label> gavāṃ mūtreṇa manujo
            bhāgairdharaṇasaṃmitaiḥ | eṣa sarvān kaphakṛtān rogān yogo 'pakarṣati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.76"><label>ci.22.76</label>
            kṣīrekṣurasagomūtradadhimastvamlakāñjikaiḥ | vidadhyāt kavalān vīkṣya doṣaṃ
            tailaghṛtair api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.77"><label>ci.22.77</label> rogāṇāṃ mukhajātānāṃ sādhyānāṃ
            karma kīrtitam | asādhyā api vakṣyante rogā ye tatra kīrtitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.78"><label>ci.22.78</label> auṣṭhaprakope varjyāḥ
            syur māṃsaraktatridoṣajāḥ | dantamūleṣu varjyau tu triliṅgagatisauṣirau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.79"><label>ci.22.79</label> danteṣu ca na sidhyanti
            śyāvadālanabhañjanāḥ | jihvāgateṣv alāsas tu tālavyeṣv arbudaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.80"><label>ci.22.80</label> svaraghno valayo vṛndo
            vidāryalasa eva ca | galauṣṭho māṃsatānaś ca śataghnī rohiṇī ca yā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.22.81"><label>ci.22.81</label> asādhyāḥ kīrtitā hyete rogā nava
            daśaiva ca | teṣāṃ cāpi kriyāṃ vaidyaḥ pratyākhyāya samācaret ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne mukharogacikitsitaṃ nāma
            dvāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||22 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="23" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>trayoviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.1"><label>ci.23.1</label> athātaḥ śophānāṃ cikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.2"><label>ci.23.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.3"><label>ci.23.3</label> ṣaḍvidho 'vayavasamutthaḥ
            śopho 'bhihito lakṣaṇataḥ pratīkārataśca; sarvasaras tu pañcavidhaḥ, tadyathā
            vātapittaśleṣmasannipātaviṣanimittaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.4"><label>ci.23.4</label>
            tatrāpatarpitasyādhvagamanādatimātramabhyavaharato vā
            piṣṭānnaharitakaśākalavaṇāni kṣīṇasya vā 'timātramamlam upasevamānasya
            mṛtpakvaloṣṭakaṭaśarkarānūpaudakamāṃsasevanādajīrṇino vā
            grāmyadharmasevanādviruddhāhārasevanāt vā
            hastyaśvoṣṭrarathapadātisaṅkṣobhaṇādayo sitasya doṣā dhātūn pradūṣya
            śvayathumāpādayantyakhile śarīre || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.5"><label>ci.23.5</label> tatra vātaśvayathuraruṇaḥ kṛṣṇo vā
            mṛduranavasthitāstodādayaścātra vedanāviśeṣāḥ; pittaśvayathuḥ pītaḥ sarakto
            vā mṛduḥ śīghrānusāryūṣādayaścātra vedanāviśeṣāḥ; śleṣmaśvayathuḥ pāṇḍuḥ
            śuklo vā snigdhaḥ kaṭhinaḥ śīto mandānusārī, kaṇḍvādayaścātra vedanāviśeṣāḥ;
            sannipātaśvayathuḥ sarvavarṇavedanaḥ; viṣanimittastu
            garopayogādduṣṭatoyasevanāt prakuthitodakāvagāhanāt
            saviṣasattvadigdhacūrṇāvacūrṇanādvā saviṣamūtrapurīṣaśukraspṛṣṭānāṃ vā
            tṛṇakāṣṭhādīnāṃ saṃsparśanāt, sa tu mṛduḥ ksiprotthāno 'valambī calo 'calo vā
            dāhapākarāgaprāyaś ca bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.6"><label>ci.23.6</label> bhavanti cātra doṣāḥ
            śvayathumūrdhvaṃ hi kurvantyāmāśayasthitāḥ | pakvāśayasthā madhye ca
            varcaḥsthānagatāstvadhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.7"><label>ci.23.7</label> kṛtsnaṃ dehamanuprāptāḥ kuryuḥ
            sarvasaraṃ tathā | śvayathurmadhyadeśe yaḥ sa kaṣṭaḥ sarvagaś ca yaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.8"><label>ci.23.8</label> ardhāṅge 'riṣṭabhūtaś ca yaścordhvaṃ
            parisarpati | śvāsaḥ pipāsā daurbalyaṃ jvaraścchardirarocakaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.9"><label>ci.23.9</label> hikkātīsārakāsāś ca śūnaṃ
            saṅkṣapayanti hi | sāmānyato viśeṣāc ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi bheṣajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.10"><label>ci.23.10</label> śophinaḥ sarva eva
            parihareyuramlalavaṇadadhiguḍavasāpayastailaghṛtapiṣṭamayagurūṇi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.11"><label>ci.23.11</label> tatra vātaśvayathau
            traivṛtameraṇḍatailaṃ vā māsamardhamāsaṃ vā pāyayet,
            nyagrodhādikakaṣāyasiddhaṃ sarpiḥ pittaśvayathau, āragvadhādisiddhaṃ sarpiḥ
            śleṣmaśvayathau, sannipātaśvayathau snuhīkṣīrapātraṃ dvādaśabhiramlapātraiḥ
            pratisaṃsṛjya dantīdravantīpratīvāpaṃ sarpiḥ pācayitvā pāyayet,
            viṣanimitteṣu kalpeṣu pratīkāraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.12"><label>ci.23.12</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
            sāmānyacikitsitam upadekṣyāmaḥ tilvakaghṛtacaturthāni yānyuktānyudareṣu
            tato 'nyatamanupayujyamānaṃ śvayathumapahanti, mūtravartikriyāṃ vā seveta,
            navāyasaṃ vā 'haraharmadhunā,
            viḍaṅgātiviṣākuṭajaphalabhadradārunāgaramaricacūrṇaṃ vā dharaṇamuṣṇāmbunā,
            trikaṭukṣārāyaścūrṇāni vā triphalākaṣāyeṇa, mūtraṃ vā tulyakṣīraṃ, harītakīṃ
            vā tulyaguḍām upayuñjīta, devadāruśuṇṭhīṃ vā, gugguluṃ vā mūtreṇa
            varṣabhūkaṣāyānupānaṃ vā, tulyaguḍaṃ vā mūtreṇa varṣabhūkaṣāyānupānaṃ vā,
            tulyaguḍaṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ vā, varṣābhūkaṣāyaṃ mūlakalkaṃ vā saśṛṅgaveraṃ
            payo 'nupānamaharaharmāsaṃ, vyoṣavarṣābhūkaṣāyasiddhena vā sarpiṣā
            mudgolumbān bhakṣayet, pippalīpippalīmūlacavyacitrakamayūrakavarṣābhūsiddhaṃ
            vā kṣīraṃ pibet, sahauṣadhamuraṅgīmūlasiddhaṃ vā, trikaṭukair
            aṇḍaśyāmāmūlasiddhaṃ vā, varṣābhūśṛṅgaverasahādevadārusiddhaṃ vā,
            tathā 'lābubibhītakaphalakalkaṃ vā taṇḍulāmbunā;
            kṣīrapippalīmaricaśṛṅgaverānusiddhena ca mudgayūṣeṇālavaṇenālpasnehena
            bhojayedyavānnaṃ godhūmānnaṃ vā; vṛkṣakārkanaktamālanimbavarṣābhūkvāthaiśca
            pariṣekaḥ; sarṣapasuvarcalāsaindhavaśārṅgeṣṭābhiś ca pradehaḥ kāryaḥ;
            yathādoṣaṃ ca vamanavirecanāsthāpanāni tīkṣṇānyajasram upaseveta,
            snehasvedopanāhāṃśca; sirābhiścābhīkṣṇaṃ
            śoṇitamavasecayedanyatropadravaśophāditi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.23.13"><label>ci.23.13</label> bhavati cātra piṣṭānnamamlaṃ
            lavaṇāni madyaṃ mṛdaṃ divāsvapnamajāṅgalaṃ ca | striyo ghṛtaṃ tailapayogurūṇi
            śophaṃ jighāṃsuḥ parivarjayet tu ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne sothacikitsitaṃ nāma
            trayoviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||23 ||</p>
        </div>

          <head>caturviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.1"><label>ci.24.1</label> athāto 'nāgatābādhāpratiṣedhaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.2"><label>ci.24.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.3"><label>ci.24.3</label> utthāyotthāya satataṃ
            svasthenārogyamicchatā | dhīmatā yadanuṣṭheyaṃ tat sarvaṃ saṃpravakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.4"><label>ci.24.4</label> tatrādau <ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref>dantapavanaṃ
            dvādaśāṅgulamāyatam | kaniṣṭhikāparīṇāhamṛjvagranthitamavraṇam<ref
              rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.5"><label>ci.24.5</label> ayugmagranthi yac cāpi pratyagraṃ
            śastabhūmijam | avekṣyartuṃ ca doṣaṃ ca rasaṃ vīryaṃ ca yojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.6"><label>ci.24.6</label> kaṣāyaṃ madhuraṃ tiktaṃ kaṭukaṃ
            prātarutthitaḥ | nimbaś ca tiktake śreṣṭhaḥ kaṣāye khadiras tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.7"><label>ci.24.7</label> madhūko madhure śreṣṭhaḥ karañjaḥ
            kaṭuke tathā | kṣaudravyoṣatrivargāktaṃ satailaṃ saindhavena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.8"><label>ci.24.8</label> cūrṇena tejovatyāś ca dantānnityaṃ
            viśodhayet | ekaikaṃ ghrṣayeddantaṃ mṛdunā kūrcakena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.9"><label>ci.24.9</label> dantaśodhanacūrṇena
            dantamāṃsānyabādhayan | taddaurgandhyopadehau tu śleṣmāṇaṃ cāpakarṣati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.10"><label>ci.24.10</label>
            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>vaiśadyamannābhiruciṃ
            saumanasyaṃ karoti ca | na khādedgalatālvoṣṭhajihvārogasamudbhave || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.11"><label>ci.24.11</label>
            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>athāsyapāke śvāse ca
            kāsahikkāvamīṣu ca | durbalo 'jīrṇabhaktaś ca mūrcchārto madapīṣitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.12"><label>ci.24.12</label> śirorujārtastṛṣitaḥ śrāntaḥ
            pānaklamānvitaḥ | arditī karṇaśūlī ca dantarogī ca mānavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.13"><label>ci.24.13</label> jihvānirlekhanaṃ raupyaṃ
            sauvarṇaṃ vārkṣam eva ca | tanmalāpaharaṃ śastaṃ mṛdu ślakṣṇaṃ daśāṅgulam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.14"><label>ci.24.14</label> mukhavair
            asyadaurgandhyaśophajāḍyaharaṃ sukham | dantadārḍhyakaraṃ rucyaṃ
            snehagaṇḍūṣadhāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.15"><label>ci.24.15</label> kṣīravṛkṣakaṣāyair vā kṣīreṇa ca
            vimiśritaiḥ | <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>bhilloṭakakaṣāyeṇa tathaivāmalakasya vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.16"><label>ci.24.16</label> prakṣālayenmukhaṃ nentre svasthaḥ
            śītodakena vā | nīlikāṃ mukhaśoṣaṃ ca piḍakāṃ vyaṅgam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.17"><label>ci.24.17</label> raktapittakṛtān rogān sadya eva
            vināśayet | sukhaṃ laghu nirīkṣeta dṛḍhaṃ paśyati cakṣuṣā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.18"><label>ci.24.18</label> mataṃ srotoñjanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ
            viśuddhaṃ sindhusaṃbhavam | dāhakaṇḍūmalaghnaṃ ca dṛṣṭikledarujāpaham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.19"><label>ci.24.19</label> tejorūpāvahaṃ caiva sahate
            mārutātapau | na netrarogā jāyante tasmādañjanamācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.20"><label>ci.24.20</label> bhuktavāñchirasā snātaḥ
            śrāntaśchardanavāhanaiḥ | rātrau jāgaritaś cāpi nāñjyājjvarita eva ca || </l>
