            saṃbhramadattāni, (tānyapi) <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>makṣikābālopahatāni, nāprakṣālitapādo bhuñjīta na mūtroccārapīḍito
            na sandhyayornānupāśrito nātītakālaṃ hīnamatimātraṃ (noddhṛtasnehaṃ) ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.99"><label>ci.24.99</label> na bhuñjītoddhṛtasnehaṃ naṣṭaṃ
            paryuṣitaṃ payaḥ | na naktaṃ dadhi bhuñjīta na cāpyaghṛtaśarkaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.100"><label>ci.24.100</label> nāmudgayūṣaṃ nākṣaudraṃ noṣṇaṃ
            nāmalakairvinā | anyathā janayet kuṣṭhavisarpādīn gadān bahūn | nātmānamudake
            paśyenna nagnaḥ praviśejjalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.101"><label>ci.24.101</label>
            dyūtamadyātisevāpratibhutvasākṣitvasamāhvānagoṣṭhīvāditrāṇi na seveta,
            srajaṃ chatropānakau kanakamatītavāsāṃsi na cānyairdhṛtāni dhārayet,
            brāhmaṇamagniṃ gāṃ ca nocchiṣṭaḥ spṛśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.102"><label>ci.24.102</label> bhavanti cātra yasmin
            yasminnṛtau ye ye doṣāḥ kupyanti dehinām | teṣu teṣu pradātavyā rasāste te
            vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.103"><label>ci.24.103</label> varṣāsu na pibettoyaṃ
            pibeccharadi mātrayā | varṣasu caturo māsān mātrāvadudakaṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.104"><label>ci.24.104</label> uṣṇaṃ haime vasante ca kāmaṃ
            śrīṣme tu śītalam | hemante ca vasante ca sīdhvariṣṭau pibennaraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.105"><label>ci.24.105</label> śṛtaśītaṃ payo grīṣme
            prāvṛṭkāle rasaṃ pibet | yūṣaṃ varṣati, tasyānte prapicchītalaṃ jalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.106"><label>ci.24.106</label> svastha evamato 'nyastu
            doṣāhāragatānugaḥ | snehaṃ saindhavacūrṇena pippalībhiś ca saṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.107"><label>ci.24.107</label> pibedagnivivṛddhyarthaṃ na ca
            vegān vidhārayet | agnidīptikaraṃ nṝṇāṃ rogāṇāṃ śamanaṃ prati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.108"><label>ci.24.108</label> prāvṛṭśaradvasanteṣu samyak
            snehādimācaret | kaphe pracchardanaṃ pitte vireko bastirīrane || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.109"><label>ci.24.109</label> śasyate triṣv api sadā vyāyāmo
            doṣanāśanaḥ | bhuktaṃ viruddhamapyannaṃ vyāyāmānna praduṣyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.110"><label>ci.24.110</label> utsargamaithunahāraśodhane
            syāt tu tanmanāḥ | neccheddoṣacayāt<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
              >*</ref> prājñaḥ pīḍāṃ vā kāyamānasīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.111"><label>ci.24.111</label> atistrīsaṃprayogācca
            rakṣedātmānamātmavān | śūlakāsajvaraśvāsakārśyapāṇḍvāmayakṣayāḥ<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.112"><label>ci.24.112</label> ativyavājājjāyante
            rogāścākṣepakādayaḥ | āyuṣmanto mandajarā vapurvarṇabalānvitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.113"><label>ci.24.113</label> sthiropacitamāṃsāś ca bhavanti
            strīṣu saṃyatāḥ | tribhistribhirahobhirvā samīyāt pramadāṃ naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.114"><label>ci.24.114</label> sarveṣvṛtuṣu, gharmeṣu pakṣāt
            pakṣādvrajedbudhaḥ | rajasvalāmakāmāṃ ca malināmapriyāṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.115"><label>ci.24.115</label> varṇavṛddhāṃ vayovṛddhāṃ tathā
            vyādhiprapīḍitām | hīnāṅgīṃ garbhiṇīṃ dveṣyāṃ yonidoṣasamanvitām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.116"><label>ci.24.116</label> sagotrāṃ gurupatnīṃ ca tathā
            pravrajitām api | sandhyāparvasvagamyāṃ ca nopeyāt pramadāṃ naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.117"><label>ci.24.117</label> gosarge cārdharātre ca tathā
            madhyandineṣu ca | lajjāsamāvahe deśe vivṛte 'śuddha eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.118"><label>ci.24.118</label> kṣudhito vyādhitaścaiva
            kṣubdhacittaś ca mānavaḥ | vātaviṇmūtravegī ca pipāsaratidurbalaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.119"><label>ci.24.119</label> tiryagyonāvayonau ca
            prāptaśukravidhāraṇam | duṣṭayonau visargaṃ tu balavānapi varjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.120"><label>ci.24.120</label> retasaścātimātraṃ tu
            mūrdhāvaraṇam eva ca | sthitāvuttānaśayane viśeṣeṇaiva garhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.121"><label>ci.24.121</label> krīḍāyām api medhāvī hitārthī
            parivarjayet | rajasvalāṃ prāptavato narasyāniyatātmanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.122"><label>ci.24.122</label> dṛṣṭyāyustejasāṃ hāniradharmaś
            ca tato bhavet | liṅginīṃ gurupatnīṃ ca sagotrāmatha parvasu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.123"><label>ci.24.123</label> vṛddhāṃ ca sandhyayoścāpi
            gacchato jīvitakṣayaḥ | garbhiṇyā garbhapīḍā syād vyādhitāyāṃ balakṣayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.124"><label>ci.24.124</label> hīnāṅgīṃ malināṃ dveṣyāṃ kāmaṃ
            vandhyāmasaṃvṛte | deśe 'śuddhe ca śukrasya manasaś ca kṣayo bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.125"><label>ci.24.125</label> kṣudhitaḥ kṣubdhacittaśca
            madhyāhne tṛṣito 'balaḥ | sthitaś ca hāniṃ śukrasya vāyoḥ kopaṃ ca vindati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.126"><label>ci.24.126</label> atiprasaṅgādbhavati śoṣaḥ
            śukrakṣayāvahaḥ | vyādhitasya rujā plīhni mṛtyurmūrcchā ca jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.127"><label>ci.24.127</label> prayūṣasyardharātre ca
            vātapitte prakupyataḥ | tiryagyonāvayanau ca duṣṭayonau tathaiva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.128"><label>ci.24.128</label> upadaṃśas tathā vāyoḥ kopaḥ
            śukrasya ca kṣayaḥ | uccārite mūtrite ca <ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref>retasaś ca vidhāraṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.129"><label>ci.24.129</label> uttāne ca bhavecchīghraṃ
            śukrāśmaryās tu saṃbhavaḥ | sarvaṃ pariharettasmādetallokadvaye 'hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.130"><label>ci.24.130</label> śukraṃ copasthitaṃ mohānna
            sandhāryaṃ kathaṃcana | vayorūpaguṇopetāṃ tulyaśīlāṃ kulānvitām<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.131"><label>ci.24.131</label> abhikāmo 'bhikāmāṃ tu hṛṣṭo
            hṛṣṭāmalaṅkṛtām | seveta pramadāṃ yuktyā vājīkaraṇabṛṃhitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.132"><label>ci.24.132</label> bhakṣyāḥ saśarkarāḥ kṣīraṃ
            sasitaṃ rasa eva ca | snānaṃ savyajanaṃ svapno vyavāyānte hitāni tu<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.24.133"><label>ci.24.133</label> mukhamātraṃ samāsena
            sadvṛttasyaitadīritam | ārogyamāyurartho vā gāsadbhiḥ prāpyate <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>nṛbhiḥ ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne 'nāgatābādhacikitsitaṃ nāma
            caturviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||24 ||</p>
        </div>
        
        <div n="25" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>pañcaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.1"><label>ci.25.1</label> athāto miśrakacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.2"><label>ci.25.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.3"><label>ci.25.3</label> pālyāmayās tu visrāvyā ity uktaṃ
            prāṅgibodha tān | paripoṭas tathotpāta unmantho duḥkhavardhanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.4"><label>ci.25.4</label> pañcamaḥ parilehī ca karṇapālyāṃ
            gadāḥ smṛtāḥ | saukumāryāc cirotsṛṣṭe sahasā 'bhipravardhite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.5"><label>ci.25.5</label> karṇaśopho bhavet pālyāṃ sarujaḥ
            paripoṭavān | kṛṣṇāruṇanibhaḥ stabdhaḥ sa vātāt paripoṭakaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.6"><label>ci.25.6</label>
            gurvābharaṇasaṃyogāttāḍanād gharṣaṇādapi | śophaḥ pālyāṃ bhavecchyāvo
            dāhapākaruganvitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.7"><label>ci.25.7</label> rakto vā raktapittābhyāmutpātaḥ sa
            gado mataḥ | balādvardhayataḥ karṇaṃ pālyāṃ vāyuḥ prakupyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.8"><label>ci.25.8</label> gṛhītvā sakaphaṃ kuryācchophaṃ <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>tadvarṇavedanam | unmanthakaḥ
            sakaṇḍūko vikāraḥ kaphavātajaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.9"><label>ci.25.9</label> vardhamāne yadā karṇe
            kaṇḍūdāharuganvitaḥ | śopho bhavati pākaś ca tvakstho 'sau duḥkhavardhanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.10"><label>ci.25.10</label> kaphāsṛkkṛmayaḥ kuryuḥ sarṣapābhā
            vikāriṇīḥ | srāviṇīḥ piḍakāḥ pālyāṃ kaṇḍūdāharuganvitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.11"><label>ci.25.11</label> kaphāsṛkkṛmisaṃbhūtaḥ sa
            visarpannitastataḥ | lihyāt saśaṣkulīṃ pālīṃ parilehīti sa smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.12"><label>ci.25.12</label> pālyāmayā hyamī ghorā
            narasyāpratikāriṇaḥ | mithyāhāravihārasya pāliṃ hiṃsyurupekṣitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.13"><label>ci.25.13</label> tasmādāśu bhiṣak teṣu
            snehādikramamācaret | tathā 'bhyaṅgaparīṣekapradehāsṛgvimokṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.14"><label>ci.25.14</label> sāmānyato viśeṣācca
            vakṣyāmyabhyañjanaṃ prati | kharamañjariyaṣṭyāhvasaindhavāmaradārubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.15"><label>ci.25.15</label> supiṣṭaiḥ sāśvagandhaiśca
            mūlakāvalgujaiḥ phalaiḥ | sarpistailavasāmajjamadhūcchiṣṭāni pācayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.16"><label>ci.25.16</label> sakṣīrāṇyatha taiḥ pāliṃ
            pradihyāt paripoṭake | mañjiṣṭhātilayaṣṭyāhvasārivotpalapadmakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.17"><label>ci.25.17</label> sarodhraiḥ sakadambaiśca
            balājambvāmrapallavaiḥ | siddhaṃ dhānyāmlasaṃyuktaṃ tailamutpātanāśanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.18"><label>ci.25.18</label>
            tālapatryaśvagandhārkabākucīphalasaindhavaiḥ | tailaṃ kulīragodhābhyāṃ vasayā
            saha pācitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.19"><label>ci.25.19</label> saralālāṅgalībhyāṃ ca
            hitamunmanthanāśanam | tathā 'śmantakajambvāmrapatrakvāthena secanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.20"><label>ci.25.20</label>
            prapauṇḍarīkamadhukamañjiṣṭhārajanīdvayaiḥ | cūrṇair udvartanaiḥ pālīṃ
            tailāktāmavacūṇayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.21"><label>ci.25.21</label> lākṣāviḍaṅgakalkena tailaṃ
            paktvā 'vacārayet | svinnāṃ gomayapiṇḍena pradihyāt parilehike || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.22"><label>ci.25.22</label> piṣṭairviḍaṅgair athavā
            trivṛcchyāmārkasaṃyutaiḥ | karañjeṅgudibījair vā kuṭajāragvadhāyutaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.23"><label>ci.25.23</label> sarvair vā sārṣapaṃ tailaṃ siddhaṃ
            maricasaṃyutam | sanimbapatrair abhyaṅge madhūcchiṣṭānvitaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.24"><label>ci.25.24</label> pālīṣu vyādhiyuktāsu tanvīṣu
            kaṭhināsu ca | puṣṭyārthaṃ mārdavārthaṃ ca kuryād abhyañjanaṃ tvidam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.25"><label>ci.25.25</label> lopākānūpamajjānaṃ vasāṃ tailaṃ
            navaṃ ghṛtam | paceddaśaguṇaṃ kṣīramāvāpya madhuraṃ gaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.26"><label>ci.25.26</label> apāmārgāśvagandhe ca tathā
            lākṣārasaṃ śubham | tatsiddhaṃ paripūtaṃ ca svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.27"><label>ci.25.27</label> tenābhyañjyāt sadā pālīṃ
            susvinnāmtimarditām | etena pālyo vardhante nirujo nirupadravāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.28"><label>ci.25.28</label> mṛdvyaḥ puṣṭāḥ samāḥ snigdhā
            jāyante bhūṣaṇakṣamāḥ | nīlīdalaṃ bhṛṅgarajo 'rjunatvak piṇḍītakaṃ
            kṛṣṇamayorajaś ca | bījodbhavaṃ sāhacaraṃ ca puṣpaṃ pathyākṣadhātrīsahitaṃ
            vicūrṇya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.29"><label>ci.25.29</label> ekīkṛtaṃ sarvamidaṃ pramāya
            paṅkena tulyaṃ nalinībhavena | saṃyojya pakṣaṃ kalaśe nidhāya lauhe <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>ghaṭe sadmani sāpidhāne || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.30"><label>ci.25.30</label> anena tailaṃ <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>vipacedvimiśraṃ rasena
            bhṛṅgatriphalābhavena | āsannapāke ca parīkṣaṇārthaṃ patraṃ
            balākābhavamākṣipec ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.31"><label>ci.25.31</label> bhavedyadā tadbhramarāṅganīlaṃ
            tadā vipakvaṃ vinidhāya pātre | kṛṣṇāyase māsamavasthitaṃ tadabhyaṅgayogāt
            palitāni hanyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.32"><label>ci.25.32</label> sairīyajambvarjunakāśmarījaṃ
            puṣpaṃ tilānmārkavacūtabīje | punarnave kardamakaṇṭakāryau
            kāsīsapiṇḍītakabījasāram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.33"><label>ci.25.33</label> phalatrayaṃ loharajo 'ñjanaṃ ca
            yaṣṭyāhvayaṃ nīrajasārive ca | piṣṭvā 'tha sarvaṃ saha modayanty ā sārāmbhasā
            bījakasaṃbhavena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.34"><label>ci.25.34</label> sārāmbhasaḥ saptabhir eva paścāt
            prasthaiḥ samāloḍya daśāhaguptam | lauhe supātre vinidhāya tailamakṣodbhavaṃ
            tac ca pacet prayatnāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.35"><label>ci.25.35</label> pakvaṃ ca lauhe 'bhinave nidhāya
            nasyaṃ vidadhyāt pariśuddhakāyaḥ | abhyaṅgayogaiś ca niyujyamānaṃ bhuñjīta
            māṣān kṛśarāmatho vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.36"><label>ci.25.36</label> māsopariṣṭād ghanakuñjitāgrāḥ keśā
            bhavanti bhramarāñjanābhāḥ | keśās tathā 'nye khalatau bhaveyurjarā na cainaṃ
            sahasā 'bhyupaiti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.37"><label>ci.25.37</label> balaṃ paraṃ saṃbhavatīndiryāṇāṃ
            bhavec ca vaktraṃ valibhirvimuktam | nākāmine 'nārthini nākṛtāya naivāraye
            tailamidaṃ pradeyam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.38"><label>ci.25.38</label> lākṣā<ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref> rodhraṃ dve haridre śilāle
            kuṣṭhaṃ nāgaṃ gairikā varṇakāś ca | mañjiṣṭhogrā syāt surāṣṭrodbhavā ca
            pattaṅgaṃ vai rocanā cāñjanaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.39"><label>ci.25.39</label> hemāṅgatvak pāṇḍupatraṃ vaṭasya
            kālīyaṃ syāt padmakaṃ padmamadhyam | raktaṃ śvetaṃ candanaṃ pāradaṃ ca
            kākolyādiḥ kṣīrapiṣṭaś ca vargaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.40"><label>ci.25.40</label> medo majjā sikthakaṃ goghṛtaṃ ca
            dugdhaṃ kvāthaḥ kṣīriṇāṃ ca drumāṇām | etat sarvaṃ pakvamaikadhyatastu
            vaktrābhyaṅge sarpiruktaṃ pradhānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.41"><label>ci.25.41</label> hanyād vyaṅgaṃ nīlikāṃ
            cātivṛddhāṃ vaktre jātāḥ sphoṭikāś cāpi kāścit | padmākāraṃ nirvalīkaṃ ca
            vaktraṃ kuryād etat pīnagaṇḍaṃ manojñam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.42"><label>ci.25.42</label> rājñāmetadyoṣitāṃ cāpi nityaṃ
            kuryād vaidyastatsamānāṃ nṛṇāṃ ca | kuṣṭhaghnaṃ vai sarpiretat pradhānaṃ
            yeṣāṃ pāde santi vaipādikāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.25.43"><label>ci.25.43</label> harīkakīcūrṇamariṣṭapatraṃ
            cūtatvacaṃ dāḍimapuṣpavṛntam | patraṃ ca dadyānmadayantikāyā lepo 'ṅgarāgo
            naradevayogyaḥ ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne miśrakacikitsitaṃ nāma
            pañcaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||25 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="26" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.1"><label>ci.26.1</label> athātaḥ kṣīṇabalīyaṃ
            vājīkaraṇacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.2"><label>ci.26.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.3"><label>ci.26.3</label> kalyasyodagravayaso
            vājīkaraṇasevinaḥ | sarveṣvṛtuṣvaharaharvyavāyo na nivāritaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.4"><label>ci.26.4</label> sthavirāṇāṃ riraṃsūnāṃ strīṇāṃ
            vāllabhyamicchatām | yoṣitprasaṅgāt kṣīṇānāṃ klībānāmalparetasām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.5"><label>ci.26.5</label> vilāsināmarthavatāṃ
            rūpayauvanaśālinām | nṛṇāṃ ca bahubhāryāṇāṃ yogā vājīkarā hitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.6"><label>ci.26.6</label> sevamāno
            yadaucityādvājīvātyarhtavegavān | nārīstarpayate tena vājīkaraṇamucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.7"><label>ci.26.7</label> bhojanāni vicitrāṇi pānāni
            vividhāni ca | vācaḥ śrotrānugāminyastvacaḥ sparśasukhās tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.8"><label>ci.26.8</label> yāminī sendutilakā kāminī
            navayauvanā | gītaṃ śrotramanohāri tāmbūlaṃ madirāḥ srajaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.9"><label>ci.26.9</label> gandhā manojñā rūpāṇi
            citrāṇyupavanāni ca | manasaścāpratīghāto vājīkurvanti mānavam |
            tais tair bhāvair ahṛdyais tu riraṃsormanasi kṣate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.10"><label>ci.26.10</label> dveṣyastrīsaṃprayogāc ca klaibyaṃ
            tanmānasaṃ smṛtam | kaṭukāmloṣṇalavaṇair atimātropasevitaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.11"><label>ci.26.11</label> saumyadhātukṣayo dṛṣṭaḥ klaibyaṃ
            tadaparaṃ smṛtam | ativyavāyaśīlo yo na ca vājīkriyārataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.12"><label>ci.26.12</label> dhvajabhaṅgamavāpnoti
            tacchukrakṣayahetukam | mahatā meḍhrarogeṇa marmacchedena vā punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.13"><label>ci.26.13</label> klaibyametaccaturthaṃ syānnṝṇāṃ
            puṃstvopaghātajam | janmaprabhṛti yaḥ klībaḥ klaibyaṃ tat sahajaṃ smṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.14"><label>ci.26.14</label> balinaḥ kṣubdhamanaso nirodhād
            brahmacaryataḥ | ṣaṣṭhaṃ klaibyaṃ mataṃ tat tu kharaśukranimittajam<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.15"><label>ci.26.15</label> asādhyaṃ sahajaṃ klaibyaṃ
            marmacchedāc ca yadbhavet | sādhyānāmitareṣāṃ tu kāryo hetuviparyayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.16"><label>ci.26.16</label> vidhirvājīkaro yas tu taṃ
            pravakṣyāmyataḥ param | tilamāṣavidārīṇāṃ śālīnāṃ cūrṇam eva vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.17"><label>ci.26.17</label> pauṇḍrakekṣurasairārdraṃ marditaṃ
            saindhavānvitam | varāhamedasā yuktāṃ ghṛtenotkārikāṃ pacet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.18"><label>ci.26.18</label> tāṃ bhakṣayitvā <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>puruṣo gacchet tu pramadāśatam |
            bastāṇḍasiddhe payasi bhāvitānasakṛttilān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.19"><label>ci.26.19</label> śiśumāravasāpakvāḥ
            śaṣkulyastistailaiḥ kṛtāḥ | yaḥ svādet sa pumān gacchet strīṇāṃ
            śatamapūrvavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.20"><label>ci.26.20</label> pippalīlavaṇopete bastāṇḍe

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.21"><label>ci.26.21</label> pippalīmāṣaśālīnāṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.22"><label>ci.26.22</label> tāṃ bhakṣayitvā pītvā tu

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.23"><label>ci.26.23</label> vidāryāḥ sukṛtaṃ cūrṇaṃ

              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.24"><label>ci.26.24</label> evamāmalakaṃ cūrṇaṃ svarasenaiva

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.25"><label>ci.26.25</label> etenāśītivarṣo 'pi yuveva

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.26"><label>ci.26.26</label> śiśumārasya vā khādette tu

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.27"><label>ci.26.27</label> mahiṣarṣabhabastānāṃ

              marker">*</ref> payasā naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.30"><label>ci.26.30</label> avalihya payaḥ pītvā tena vājī

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.34"><label>ci.26.34</label> uccaṭācūrṇaṃ peyamevaṃ

              footnote marker">*</ref> pibennaraḥ || </l>

            hṛṣyati sarvarātram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.36"><label>ci.26.36</label> māṣān vidārīm api soccaṭāṃ ca

            kuliṅgavaddhṛṣyati sarvarātram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.37"><label>ci.26.37</label> gṛṣṭīnāṃ vṛddhavatsānāṃ
            māṣaparṇabhṛtāṃ gavām | yat kṣīraṃ tat praśaṃsanti balakāmeṣu jantuṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.38"><label>ci.26.38</label> kṣīramāṃsagaṇāḥ sarve kākolyādiś
            ca pūjitaḥ | vājīkaraṇahetorhi tasmāttut tu prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.26.39"><label>ci.26.39</label> ete vājīkarā yogāḥ
            prītyapatyabalapradāḥ | sevyā viśuddhopacitadehaiḥ kālādyapekṣayā ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ kṣīṇabalīyavājīkaraṇacikitsitaṃ nāma

        <div n="27" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>saptaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.1"><label>ci.27.1</label> athātaḥ sarvopaghātaśamanīyaṃ<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> rasāyanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.2"><label>ci.27.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.3"><label>ci.27.3</label> pūrve vayasi madhye vā manuṣyasya
            rasāyanam | prayuñjīta bhiṣak prājñaḥ snigdhaśuddhatanoḥ sadā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.4"><label>ci.27.4</label> nāviśuddhaśarīrasya yukto rāsāyano
            vidhiḥ | na bhāti vāsasi kliṣṭe raṅgayoga ivāhitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.5"><label>ci.27.5</label> śarīrasyopaghātā ye doṣajā
            mānasās tathā | upadiṣṭāḥ pradeśeṣu teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi vāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.6"><label>ci.27.6</label> śītodakaṃ payaḥ kṣaudraṃ
            sarpirityekaśo dviśaḥ | triśaḥ samastamathavā prāk pītaṃ sthāpayedvayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.7"><label>ci.27.7</label> tatra viḍaṅgataṇḍulacūrṇamāhṛtya
            yaṣṭīmadhukamadhuyuktaṃ yathābalaṃ śītatoyenopayuñjīta śītatoyaṃ
            cānupibedevamaharaharmāsaṃ, tadeva madhuyuktaṃ bhallātakakvāthena vā,
            madhudrākṣākvāthayuktaṃ vā, madhvāmalakarasābhyāṃ vā, guḍūcīkvāthena vā,
            evam ete pañ ca prayogā bhavanti; jīrṇe mudgāmalakayūṣeṇālavaṇenālpasnehena
            ghṛtavantamodanamaśnīyāt; ete svalvarśāṃsi kṣapayanti, kṛmīnupaghnanti,
            grahaṇadhāraṇaśaktiṃ janayanti, māse māse ca prayoge varṣaśataṃ
            varṣaśatamāyuṣo 'bhivṛddhir bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.8"><label>ci.27.8</label> viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṃ droṇaṃ
            piṣṭapacane <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>piṣṭavadupasvedya
            vigatakaṣāyaṃ svinnamavatārya dṛṣadi piṣṭamāyase dṛḍhe kumbhe
            madhūdakottaraṃ prāvṛṣi bhasmarāśāvantargṛhe caturo māsānnidadhyāt,
            varṣāvigame coddhṛtyopasaṃskṛtaśarīraḥ sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā
            prātaḥprātaryathābalam upayuñjīta, jīrṇe mudgāmalakayūṣeṇālavaṇena<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> ghṛtavantamodanamaśnīyāt,
            pāṃśuśayyāyāṃ śayīta, tasya māsādūrdhvaṃ sarvāṅgebhyaḥ kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti,
            tānaṇutailenābhyaktasya vaṃśavidalenāpaharet, dvitīye pipīlikāstṛtīye
            yūkāstathaivāpaharet, caturthe dantanakharomāṇyavaśīryante; pañcame
            praśastaguṇalakṣaṇāni jāyante, amānuṣaṃ cādityaprakāśaṃ vapuradhigacchati,
            dūrācchravaṇāni darśanā nicāsya bhavanti, rajastamasī cāpohya
            sattvamadhitiṣṭhati, śrutanigādyapūrvotpādī gajabalo 'śvajavaḥ punaryuvā 'ṣṭau
            varṣaśatānyāyuravāpnoti; tasyāṇutailamabhyaṅgārthe, candanam upalepanārthe,
            bhallātakavidhānavadāhāraḥ parihāraś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.9"><label>ci.27.9</label> kāśmaryāṇāṃ niṣkulīkṛtānāmeṣa eva
            kalpaḥ pāṃśuśayyābhojanavarjaṃ; atra hi payasā śṛtena bhoktavyaṃ,
            samānamanyat pūrveṇāśiṣaś ca | śoṇitapittanimitteṣu vikāreṣveteṣām upayogaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.10"><label>ci.27.10</label> yathoktamāgāraṃ praviśya
            balāmūlārdhapalaṃ palaṃ vā payasā++āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana
            ityāhāraḥ, evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayujya dvādaśa varṣāṇi vayastiṣṭhati; evaṃ
            divasaśatam upayujya varṣaśataṃ vayastiṣṭhati |
            evam evātibalānāgabalāvidārīśatāvarīṇām upayogaḥ | viśeṣatastvatibalāmudakena,
            nāgabalācūrṇaṃ madhunā, vidārīcūrṇaṃ kṣīreṇa, śatāvarīmapyevaṃ, pūrveṇānyat
            samānamāśiṣaś ca samāḥ | etāstvauṣadhayo balakāmānāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ
            raktapittopasṛṣṭānāṃ śoṇitaṃ chardayatāṃ viricyamānānāṃ copadiśyante || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.11"><label>ci.27.11</label> vārāhīmūlatulācūrṇaṃ kṛtvā tato
            mātrāṃ madhuyuktāṃ payasā++āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ,
            pratibedho 'tra <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>pūrvavat;
            prayogamimam upasevamāno varṣaśatamāyuravāpnoti strīṣu cākṣayatām, etenaiva
            cūrṇena payo 'vacūrṇya śṛtaśītam abhimathyājyamutpādya madhuyutam upayuñjīta
            sāyaṃprātarekakālaṃ vā, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ, evaṃ
            māsam upayujya <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>varṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.12"><label>ci.27.12</label> cakṣuḥkāmaḥ prāṇakāmo vā
            bījakasārāgnimanthamūlaṃ niṣkvāthya māṣaprasthaṃ sādhayet, tasmin sidhyati
            citrakamūlānāmakṣamātraṃ kalkaṃ dadyād āmalakarasacaturthabhāgaṃ, tataḥ
            svinnamavatārya sahasrasṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā śītībhūtaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ
            saṃsṛjyopayuñjīta yathābalaṃ, yathāsātmyaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ pariharan bhakṣayet |
            jīrṇe mudgāmalakayūṣeṇālavaṇena ghṛtavantamodanamaśnīyāt payasā vā
            māsatrayam; evamābhyāṃ prayogābhyāṃ cakṣuḥ <ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref>sauparṇaṃ bhavatyanalpabalaḥ
            strīṣu cākṣayo varṣaśatāyurbhavatīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.27.13"><label>ci.27.13</label> bhavati cātra payasā saha
            siddhāni naraḥ śaṇaphalāni yaḥ | bhakṣayet payasā sārdhaṃ vayastasya na
            śīryate ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne sarvopaghātaśamanīyaṃ
            rasāyanacikitsitaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||27 ||</p>

        <div n="28" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>aṣṭaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.1"><label>ci.28.1</label> athāto <ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref>medhāyuṣkāmīyaṃ
              rasāyanacikitsitaṃ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.2"><label>ci.28.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvanatariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.3"><label>ci.28.3</label> medhāyuḥkāmaḥ
            śvetāvalgujaphalānyātapapariśuṣkāṇyādāya sūkṣmacūrṇāni kṛtvā guḍena
            sahāloḍya snehakumbhe saptarātraṃ dhānyarāśau nidadhyāt, saptarātrāduddhṛtya
            hṛtadoṣasya yathābalaṃ piṇḍaṃ prayacched anudite sūrye, uṣṇodakaṃ cānupibet;
            bhallātakavidhānavaccāgārapraveśaḥ, jīrṇauṣadhaścāparāhṇe himābhiradbhiḥ
            pariṣiktagātraḥ śālīnāṃ ṣaṣṭikānāṃ ca payasā śarkarāmadhureṇaudanamaśnīyāt;
            evaṃ ṣaṇmāsānupayujya vigatapāpmā balavarṇopetaḥ śrutanigādī smṛtimānarogo
            varṣaśatāyur bhavati | kuṣṭhinaṃ pāṇḍurogiṇamudariṇaṃ vā kṛṣṇāyā
            gormūtreṇāloḍyārdhapalikaṃ piṇḍaṃ vigatalauhitye savitari pāyayet, parāhṇe
            cālavaṇenāmalakayūṣeṇa sarpiṣmantamodanamaśnīyāt, evaṃ māsam upayujya
            smṛtimānarogo varṣaśatāyur bhavati | eṣaevopayogaścitrakamūlānāṃ rajanyāśca;
            citrakamūle viśeṣo dvipalikaṃ piṇḍaṃ paraṃ pramāṇaṃ, śeṣaṃ pūrvavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.4"><label>ci.28.4</label> hṛtadoṣa eva pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto
            yathākramamāgāraṃ praviśya maṇḍūkaparṇīsvarasamādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ
            kṛtvā yathābalaṃ payasā++āloḍya pibet payo 'nupānaṃ vā, tasyāṃ jīrṇāyāṃ
            yavānnaṃ payasopayuñjīta; tilair vā saha bhakṣayettrīn māsān payo 'nupānaṃ,
            jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ; evam upayuñjāno brahmavarcasī śrutanigādī
            bhavati varṣaśatamāyuravāpnoti | trirātropoṣitaś ca trirātramenāṃ bhakṣayet,
            trirātrādūrdhvaṃ payaḥ sarpiriti copayuñjīta | bilvamātraṃ piṇḍaṃ vā
            payasā++āloḍya pibet, evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayujya medhāvī
            varṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.5"><label>ci.28.5</label> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya
            pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto brāhmīsvarasamādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā
            yathābalampayuñjīta, jīrṇauṣadhaścāparāhṇe yavāgūmalavaṇaṃ pibet,
            kṣīrasātmyo vā payasā bhuñjīta, evaṃ saptarātram upayujya brahmavarcasī
            medhāvī bhavati, dvitīyaṃ saptarātram upayujya granthamīpsitamutpādayati
            naṣṭaṃ cāsya prādurbhavati, tṛtīyaṃ saptarātram upayujya dviruccāritaṃ
            śatamapyavadhārayati, evam ekaviṃśatirātram upayujyālakṣmīrapakrāmati;
            mūrtimatī cainaṃ vāgdevyanupraviśati, sarvāścainaṃ śrutaya upatiṣṭhanti,
            śrutadharaḥ pañcavarṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.6"><label>ci.28.6</label> brāhmīsvarasaprasthadvaye
            ghṛtaprasthaṃ viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṃ kuḍavaṃ dve dve pale vacāmṛtayordvādaśa
            harītakyāmalakabibhītakāni ślakṣṇapiṣṭānyāvāpyaikadhyaṃ sādhayitvā
            svanuguptaṃ nidadhyāt, tataḥ pūrvavidhānena mātrāṃ yathābalam upayuñjīta,
            jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ, pūrvavaccātra parīhāraḥ,
            etenordhvamadhastiryak kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, alakṣmīrapakrāmati, puṣkaravarṇaḥ
            sthiravayāḥ śrutanigādī trivarṣaśatāyurbhavati; etadeva
            kuṣṭhaviṣamajvarāpasmāronmādaviṣabhūtagraheṣv anyeṣu ca mahāvyādhiṣu
            saṃśodhanamādiśanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.7"><label>ci.28.7</label> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya
            haimavatyā vacāyāḥ piṇḍamāmalakamātram abhihutaṃ payasā++āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe
            payaḥ sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ, evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayuñjīta, tato 'sya śrotraṃ
            vivriyate, dvirabhyāsāt smṛtimān bhavati, trirabhyāsācchrutamādatte,
            caturdvādaśarātram upayujya sarvaṃ tarati kilbiṣaṃ, tārkṣyadarśanamutpadyate,
            śatāyuś ca bhavati | dve dve pale itarasyā vacāyā viṣkvāthya pibet payasā,
            samānaṃ bhojanaṃ, samāḥ pūrveṇāśiṣaś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.8"><label>ci.28.8</label> vacāśatapākaṃ vā
            sarpirdroṇam upayujya pañcavarṣaśatāyurbhavati,
            galagaṇḍāpacīślīpadasvaramedāṃścāpahantīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.9"><label>ci.28.9</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi
            āyuṣkāmarasāyanam | mantrauṣadhasamāyuktaṃ saṃvatsaraphalapradam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.10"><label>ci.28.10</label> bilvasya cūrṇaṃ puṣye tu hutaṃ
            vārān sahasraśaḥ | śrīsūktena naraḥ kalye sasuvarṇaṃ dine dine || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.11"><label>ci.28.11</label> sarpirmdhuyutaṃ
            lihyādalakṣmīnāśanaṃ param | tvacaṃ vihāya bilvasya mūlakvāthaṃ dine dine || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.12"><label>ci.28.12</label> prāśnīyāt payasā sārdhaṃ snātvā
            hutvā samāhitaḥ | daśasāhassramāyuṣyaṃ smṛtaṃ yuktarathaṃ bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.13"><label>ci.28.13</label> hutvā bisānāṃ kvāthaṃ tu
            madhulājaiś ca saṃyutam | amoghaṃ śatasāhasraṃ yuktaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.14"><label>ci.28.14</label> suvarṇaṃ padmabījāni madhu lājāḥ
            priyaṅgavaḥ | gavyena payasā pītamalakṣmīṃ pratibedhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.15"><label>ci.28.15</label> nīlotpaladalakvātho gavyena
            payasā śṛtaḥ | sasuvarṇastilaiḥ sārdhamalakṣmīnāśanaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.16"><label>ci.28.16</label> gavyaṃ payaḥ suvarṇaṃ ca
            madhūcchiṣṭaṃ ca mākṣikam | pītaṃ śatasahasrābhihutaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.17"><label>ci.28.17</label> vacāghṛtasuvarṇaṃ ca
            bilvacūrṇam iti trayam | medhyamāyuṣyamārogyapuṣṭisaubhāgyavardhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.18"><label>ci.28.18</label> vāsāmūlatulākvāthe tailamāvāpya
            sādhitam | hutvā sahasramaśnīyānmedhyamāyuṣyamucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.19"><label>ci.28.19</label> yāvakāṃstāvakān khādedabhibhūya
            yavāṃs tathā | pippalīmadhusaṃyuktān śikṣā caraṇavadbhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.20"><label>ci.28.20</label> madhvāmalakacūrṇāni suvarṇamiti
            ca trayam | prāśyāriṣṭagṛhīto 'pi mucyate prāṇasaṃśayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.21"><label>ci.28.21</label> śatāvarīghṛtaṃ samyagupayuktaṃ
            dine dine | sakṣaudraṃ sasuvarṇaṃ ca narendraṃ sthāpayedvaśe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.22"><label>ci.28.22</label> gocandanā mohanikā madhukaṃ
            mākṣikaṃ madhu | suvarṇam iti saṃyogaḥ peyaḥ saubhāgyamicchatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.23"><label>ci.28.23</label>
            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>padmanīlotpalakvāthe
            yaṣṭīmadhukasaṃyute | sarpirāsāditaṃ gavyaṃ sasuvarṇaṃ sadā paibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.24"><label>ci.28.24</label> payaścānupibet siddhaṃ teṣāmeva
            samudbhave | alakṣmīghnaṃ sadā++āyuṣyaṃ rājyāya subhagāya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.25"><label>ci.28.25</label> yatra nodīrito mantro yogeṣveteṣu
            sādhane | śabditā tatra sarvatra gāyatrī tripadā bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.26"><label>ci.28.26</label> pāpmānaṃ nāśayantyetā
            dadyuścauṣadhayaḥ śriyam | kuryurnāgabalaṃ cāpi manuṣyamamaropamam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.27"><label>ci.28.27</label> satatādhyayanaṃ vādaḥ
            paratantrāvalokanam | tadvidyācāryasevā ca buddhimedhākaro guṇaḥ(gaṇaḥ) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.28.28"><label>ci.28.28</label> āyuṣyaṃ bhojanaṃ jīrṇe vegānāṃ
            cāvidhāraṇam | brahmacaryamahiṃsā ca sāhasānāṃ ca varjanam ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne medhāyuṣkāmīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ
            nāmāṣṭāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||28 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="29" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>ekonatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.1"><label>ci.29.1</label> athātaḥ
            svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.2"><label>ci.29.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.3"><label>ci.29.3</label> brahmādayo 'sṛjan pūrvamamṛtaṃ
            somasaṃjñitam | jarāmṛtyuvināśāya vidhānaṃ tasya vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.4"><label>ci.29.4</label> eka eva khalu bhagavān somaḥ
            sthānanāmākṛtivīryaviśeṣaiścaturviṃśatidhā bhidyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.5"><label>ci.29.5</label> aṃśumān muñjavāṃścaiva candramā
            rajataprabhaḥ | dūrvāsomaḥ kanīyāṃś ca śvetākṣaḥ kanakaprabhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.6"><label>ci.29.6</label> pratānavāṃstālavṛntaḥ
            karavīro 'ṃśavānapi | svayaṃprabho mahāsomo yaś cāpi garuḍāhṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.7"><label>ci.29.7</label> gāyatrastraiṣṭubhaḥ pāṅkto jāgataḥ
            śākvaras tathā | agniṣṭomo raivataś ca yathokta iti saṃjñitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.8"><label>ci.29.8</label> gāyatryā tripadā yukto
            yaścoḍupatirucyate | ete somāḥ samākhyātā vedoktairnām abhiḥ śubhaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.9"><label>ci.29.9</label> sarveṣām eva caiteṣāmeko
            vidhirupāsane | sarve tulyaguṇāścaiva vidhānaṃ teṣu vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.10"><label>ci.29.10</label> ato 'nyatamaṃ somam upayuyukṣuḥ
            sarvopakaraṇaparicārakopetaḥ praśaste deśe trivṛtamāgāraṃ kārayitvā
            hṛtadoṣaḥ pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhaktaḥ praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu
            aṃśumantamādāyādhvarakalpenāhṛtam abhiṣutam abhihutaṃ cāntarāgāre
            kṛtamaṅgalasvastivācanaḥ somakandaṃ suvarṇasūcyā vidārya payo gṛhṇīyāt
            sauvarṇe (<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>rājate vā)
            pātre 'ñjalimātraṃ, tataḥ sakṛdevopayuñjīta nāsvādayan, tata upaspṛśya
            śeṣamapsvavasādya yamaniyamābhyāmātmānaṃ saṃyojya vāgyato 'bhyantarataḥ
            suhṛdbhirupāsyamāno viharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.11"><label>ci.29.11</label> rasāyanaṃ pītavāṃs tu nivāte
            tanmanāḥ śuciḥ | āsīta tiṣṭhet krāmec ca na kathaṃcana saṃviśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.12"><label>ci.29.12</label> sāyaṃ vā bhuktavānupaśrutaśāntiḥ
            kuśaśayyāyāṃ kṛṣṇājinottarāyāṃ suhṛdbhirupāsyamānaḥ śayīta, tṛṣito vā
            śītodakamātrāṃ pibet (<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>aśanāyito vā kṣīraṃ); tataḥ prātarutthāyopaśrutaśāntiḥ kṛtamaṅgalo
            gāṃ spṛṣṭvā tatahaivāsīta, tasya jīrṇe some chardirutpadyate, tataḥ
            śoṇitāktaṃ kṛmivyāmiśraṃ charditavate sāyaṃ śṛtaśītaṃ kṣīraṃ vitaret;
            tatastṛtīye 'hani kṛmivyāmiśramatisāryate, sa
            tenāniṣṭapratigrahabhuktaprabhṛtibhirviśeṣairvinirmuktaḥ śuddhatanurbhavati,
            tataḥ sāyaṃ snātāya pūrvavadeva kṣīraṃ vitaret, kṣaumavastrāstṛtāyāṃ cainaṃ
            śayyāyāṃ śāyayet; tataścaturthe 'hani tasya śvayathurutpadyate, tataḥ
            sarvāṅgebhyaḥ kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, tadahaś ca <ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref>śayyāyāṃ pāṃśubhiravakīryamāṇaḥ
            śayīta, tataḥ sāyaṃ pūrvavadeva kṣīraṃ vitaret; evaṃ
            pañcamaṣaṣṭhayordivasayorvarteta, kevalamubhayakālamasmai kṣīraṃ vitaret;
            tataḥ saptame 'hani nirmāṃsastvagasthibhūtaḥ kevalaṃ
            somaparigrahādevocchvasiti, tadahaś ca kṣīreṇa sukhoṣṇena pariṣicya
            tilamadhukacandanānuliptadehaṃ payaḥ pāyayet; tato 'ṣṭame 'hani prātareva
            kṣīrapariṣiktaṃ candanapradigdhāgātraṃ payaḥ pāyayitvā pāṃśuśayyāṃ
            samutsṛjya kṣaumavastrāstṛtāyāṃ śayyāyāṃ śāyayet, tato 'sya māṃsamāpyāyyate,
            tvak cāvadalati, dantanakharomāṇi cāsya patanti; tasya navamadivasāt
            prabhṛtyaṇutailābhyaṅgaḥ somavalkakaṣāyapariṣekaḥ; tato daśame 'hanyetadeva
            vitaret, tato 'sya tvak sthiratām upaiti; evam ekādaśadvādaśayorvarteta;
            tatastrayodaśāt prabhṛti somavalkakaṣāyapariṣekaḥ, evamāṣoḍaśādvarteta;
            tataḥ saptadaśāṣṭādaśayordivasayordaśanā jāyante śikhariṇaḥ
            snigdhavajravaidūryasphaṭikaprakāśāḥ samāḥ sthirāḥ sahiṣṇavaḥ, tadā prabhṛti
            cānavaiḥ śālitaṇḍulaiḥ kṣīrayavāgūm upaseveta yāvat pañcaviṃśatiriti;
            tato 'smai dadyācchālyodanaṃ mṛdūbhayakālaṃ payasā, tato 'sya nakhā jāyante
            vidrumendragopakataruṇādityaprakāśāḥ, sthirāḥ snigdhā lakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ keśāś
            ca sūkṣmā jāyante, tvak ca nīlotpalātasīpuṣpavaidūryaprakāśā; ūrdhvaṃ ca
            māsāt keśān vāpayet, vāpayitvā cośīracandanakṛṣṇatilakalkaiḥ śiraḥ pradihyāt
            payasā vā snāpayet; tato 'syānantaraṃ saptarātrāt keśā jāyante
            bhramarāñjananibhāḥ kuñcitāḥ sthirāḥ snigdhāḥ; tatastrirātrāt<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>
            prathamāvasathaparisarānniṣkramya muhūrtaṃ sthitvā punarevāntaḥ praviśet,
            tato 'sya balātailamabhyaṅgārthe 'vacāryaṃ, yavapiṣṭamudvartanārthe, sukhoṣṇaṃ
            ca payaḥ pariṣekārthe, ajakarṇakaṣāyamutsādanārthe, sośīraṃ kūpodakaṃ
            snānārthe, candanamanulepārthe, āmalakarasavimiśrāścāsya yūṣasūpavikalpāḥ,
            kṣīramadhukasiddhaṃ ca kṛṣṇatilamavacāraṇārthe, evaṃ daśarātraṃ;
            tato 'nyaddaśarātraṃ dvitīye parisare varteta; tatastṛtīye parisare
            sthirīkurvannātmānamanyaddaśarātramāsīta, kiñcidātapapavanān vā seveta,
            punaścāntaḥ praviśet, na cātmānamādarśe 'psu vā nirīkṣeta rūpaśālitvāt;
            tato 'nyaddaśarātraṃ krodhādīn <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
              >*</ref>pariharet, evaṃ sarveṣām upayogavikalpaḥ | viśeṣatastu
            vallīpratānakṣupakādayaḥ somā brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyairbhakṣayitavyāḥ | teṣāṃ
            tu pramāṇamardhacatuṣkamuṣṭayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.13"><label>ci.29.13</label> aṃśumantaṃ sauvarṇe
            pātre 'bhiṣuṇuyāt, candramasaṃ rājate;
            tāvupayujyāṣṭaguṇamaiśvaryamavāpyeśānaṃ devamanupraviśati, śeṣāṃstu
            tāmramaye mṛnmaye vā rohite vā carmaṇi vitate; śūdravarjaṃ tribhirvarṇaiḥ
            somā upayoktavyāḥ | tataścaturthe māse paurṇamāsyāṃ śucau deśe
            brāhmaṇānarcayitvā kṛtamaṅgalo niṣkramya yathoktaṃ vrajediti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.14"><label>ci.29.14</label> oṣadhīnāṃ patiṃ somam upayujya
            vicakṣaṇaḥ | daśavarṣasahasrāṇi navāṃ dhārayate tanum || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.15"><label>ci.29.15</label> nāgnirna toyaṃ na viṣaṃ na
            śastraṃ nāstram eva ca | tasyālamāyuḥkṣapaṇe samarthāni bhavanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.16"><label>ci.29.16</label> bhadrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇāṃ
            prasrutānāmanekadhā | kuñjarāṇāṃ sahasrasya balaṃ samadhigacchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.17"><label>ci.29.17</label> kṣīrodaṃ śakrasadanamuttarāṃś ca
            kurūnapi | yatrecchati sa gantuṃ vā tatrāpratihatā gatiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.18"><label>ci.29.18</label> kandarpa iva rūpeṇa kāntyā candra
            ivāparaḥ | prahlādayati bhūtānāṃ manāṃsi sa mahādyutiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.19"><label>ci.29.19</label> sāṅgopāṅgāṃś ca nikhilān vedān
            vindati tattvataḥ | caratyamoghasaṅkalpo devavaccākhilaṃ jagat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.20"><label>ci.29.20</label> sarveṣām eva somānāṃ patrāṇi daśa
            pañ ca ca | tāni śukle ca kṛṣṇe ca jāyante nipatanti ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.21"><label>ci.29.21</label> ekaikaṃ jāyate patraṃ
            somasyāharahastadā | śuklasya paurṇamāsyāṃ tu bhavet pañcadaśacchadaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.22"><label>ci.29.22</label> śīryate patramekaikaṃ divase
            divase punaḥ | kṛṣṇapakṣakṣaye cāpi latā bhavati kevalā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.23"><label>ci.29.23</label> aṃśumānājyagandhas tu kandavān
            rajataprabhaḥ | kadalyākārakandas tu muñjavāṃllaśunacchadaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.24"><label>ci.29.24</label> candramāḥ kanakābhāso jale carati
            sarvadā | garuḍāhṛtanāmā ca śvetākṣaś cāpi pāṇḍurau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.25"><label>ci.29.25</label> sarpanirmokasadṛśau tau
            vṛkṣāgrāvalambinau | <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>tathā 'nye
            maṇḍalaiścitraiścitritā iva bhānti te || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.26"><label>ci.29.26</label> sarva eva tu vijñeyāḥ somāḥ
            pañcadaśacchadāḥ | kṣīrakandalatāvantaḥ patrairnānāvidhaiḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.27"><label>ci.29.27</label> himavatyarbude sahye mahendre
            malaye tathā | śrīparvate devagirau girau devasahe tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.28"><label>ci.29.28</label> pāriyātre ca vindhye ca devasunde
            hrade tathā | uttareṇa vitastāyāḥ pravṛddhā ye mahīdharāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.29"><label>ci.29.29</label> haṣṭhavat plavate tatra candramāḥ
            somasattamaḥ | tasyoddeśeṣu cāpyanti muñjavānaṃśumānapi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.30"><label>ci.29.30</label> tasyoddeśeṣu cāpyasti
            muñjavānaṃśumānapi | kāśmīreṣu saro divyaṃ nāmnā kṣudrakamānasam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.31"><label>ci.29.31</label> gāyatrastraiṣṭubhaḥ pāṅkto
            jāgataḥ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>śākvaras tathā | atra
            santyapare cāpi somāḥ somasamaprabhāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.32"><label>ci.29.32</label> yaiścātra mandabhāgyais te
            bhiṣajaścāpamānitāḥ | na tān paśyantyadharmiṣṭhāḥ kṛtaghnāś cāpi mānavāḥ |
            bheṣajadveṣiṇaś cāpi brāhmaṇadveṣiṇas tathā ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
            svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ rasāyanacikitsitaṃ nāmaikonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
             ||29 ||</p>

        <div n="30" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>triṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.1"><label>ci.30.1</label> athāto nivṛttasantāpīyaṃ <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>rasāyanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.2"><label>ci.30.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.30.5"><label>ci.30.5</label> athauṣadhīvyākhyāsyāmaḥ
            tatrājagarī, śvetakāpotī, kṛṣṇakāpotī, gonasī, vārāhī, kanyā, chatrā,
            aticchatrā, kareṇuḥ, ajā, cakrakā, ādityaparṇī, brahmasuvarcalā, śrāvaṇī,

            mahauṣadhayo vyākhyātāḥ | tāsāṃ somavat kriyāśīḥstutayaḥ śāstre 'bhihitāḥ |
            tāsāmāgāre 'bhihutānāṃ yāḥ kṣīravatyastāsāṃ kṣīrakuḍavaṃ <ref

            bhakṣayitavyā, gonasyajagarīkṛṣṇakāpotīnāṃ sanakhamuṣṭiṃ khaṇḍaśaḥ
            kalpayitvā kṣīreṇa vipācya parisrāvyābhighāritam abhihutaṃ ca
            sakṛdevopayuñjīta, cakrakāyāḥ payaḥ sakṛdeva, brahmasuvarcalā
            saptarātram upayoktavyā bhakṣyakalpena, śeṣāṇāṃ pañ ca pañ ca palāni
            kṣīrāḍhakakvathitāni prasthe 'vaśiṣṭe 'vatārya parisrāvya sakṛdevopayuñjīta |
            somavadāhāravihārau vyākhyātau, kevalaṃ navanītamabhyaṅgārthe, śeṣaṃ
            somavadānirgamāditi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.1"><label>ci.31.1</label> athātaḥ snehopayaugikacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.2"><label>ci.31.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.3"><label>ci.31.3</label> snehasāro 'yaṃ puruṣaḥ, prāṇāśca
            snehabhūyiṣṭāḥ snehasādhyāś ca bhavanti | sneho hi
            pānānuvāsanamastiṣkaśirovastyuttarabastinasyakarṇapūraṇagātrābhyaṅgabhojaneṣūpayojyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.4"><label>ci.31.4</label> tatra dviyoniścaturvikalpo 'bhihitaḥ
            snehaḥ snehaguṇāś ca | tatra jaṅgamebhyo gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ pradhānaṃ,
            sthāvarebhyastilatailaṃ pradhānam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.5"><label>ci.31.5</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ yathāprayojanaṃ <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>yathāpradhānaṃ ca
            sthāvarasnehānupadekṣyāmaḥ tatra tilvakair
            aṇḍakośāmradantīdravantīsaptalāśaṅkhinīpalāśaviṣāṇikāgavākṣīkampillakaśampākanīlinīsnehā
            virecayanti, jīmūtakakuṭajakṛtavedhanekṣvākudhāmārgavamadanasnehā vāmayanti,
            viḍaṅgakharamañjarīmadhuśigrusūryavallīpīlusiddhārthakajyotiṣmatīsnehāḥ śiro
            virecayanti, karañjapūtīkakṛtamālamātuluṅgeṅgudīkirātatiktakasnehā
            duṣṭavraṇeṣūpayujyante, tuvarakakapitthakampillakabhallātakapaṭolasnehā
            mahāvyādhiṣu, trapusair vārukakarkārukatumbīkūṣmāṇḍasnehā mūtrasaṅgeṣu,
            kapotavaṅkāvalgujaharītakīsnehāḥ śarkarāśmarīṣu,
            kusumbhasarṣapātasīpicumardātimuktakabhāṇḍīkaṭutumbīkaṭabhīsnehāḥ prameheṣu,
            tālanārikelapanasamocapriyālabilvamadhūkaśleṣmātakāmrātakaphalasnehāḥ
            pittasaṃsṛṣṭe vāyau, bibhītakabhallātakapiṇḍītakasnehāḥ kṛṣṇīkaraṇe,
            śravaṇakaṅgukaṭuṇṭukasnehāḥ pāṇḍūkaraṇe, saralapītadāruśiṃśapāgurusārasnehā
            dadrukuṣṭhakiṭimeṣu, sarva eva snehā vātam upaghnanti, tailaguṇāś ca samāsena
            vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.6"><label>ci.31.6</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
            kaṣāyasnehapākakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ | tatra kecidāhuḥ tvakpatraphalamūlādīnāṃ
            bhāgastaccaturguṇaṃ jalaṃ caturbhāgāvaśeṣaṃ niṣkvāthyāpaharedityeṣa
            kaṣāyapākakalpaḥ; snehaprasṛteṣu ṣaṭsu caturguṇaṃ dravamāvapya
            caturaścākṣasamān <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>bheṣajapiṇḍānityeṣa snehapākakalpaḥ | etat tu na samyak; kasmāt
            āgamāsiddhatvāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.7"><label>ci.31.7</label> palakuḍavādīnāmato mānaṃ tu
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ tatra dvādaśa dhānyamāṣā madhyamāḥ suvarṇamāṣakaḥ, te ṣoḍaśa
            suvarṇam; athavā madhyamaniṣpāvā ekonaviṃśatirdharaṇaṃ, tāvyardhatṛtīyāni
            karṣaḥ; tataścordhvaṃ caturguṇam abhivardhayantaḥ palakuḍavaprasthāḍhakadroṇā
            ity abhiniṣpadyante, tulā punaḥ palaśataṃ, tāḥ punarviṃśatirbhāraḥ;
            śuṣkāṇāmidaṃ mānam, <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>ārdradravāṇāṃ ca dviguṇam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.8"><label>ci.31.8</label> tatrānyatamaparimāṇasaṃmitānāṃ
            yathāyogaṃ tvakpatraphalamūlādīnāmātapapariśoṣitānāṃ chedyāni
            khaṇḍaśaśchedayitvā bhedyānyaṇuśo bhedayitvā 'vakuṭyāṣṭaguṇena ṣoḍaśaguṇena
            vā 'mbhasā 'bhiṣicyasthālyāṃ caturbhāgāvaśiṣṭaṃ kvāthayitvā 'paharedityeṣa
            kaṣāyayākakalpaḥ | snehāccaturbhāgāvaśiṣṭaṃ kvāthayitvā 'paharedityeṣa
            kaṣāyapākakalpaḥ | snehāccaturguṇo dravaḥ, snehacaturthaṃśo bheṣajakalkaḥ,
            tadaikadhyaṃ saṃṛjya vipacedityeṣa snehapākakalpaḥ | athavā tatrodakadroṇe
            tvakpatraphalamūlādīnāṃ tulāmāvāpya caturbhāgāvaśiṣṭaṃ
            niṣkvāthyāpaharedityeṣa kaṣāyapākakalpaḥ; snehakuḍave bheṣajapalaṃ piṣṭaṃ
            kalkaṃ caturguṇaṃ dravamāvāpya vipacedityeṣa snehapākakalpaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.9"><label>ci.31.9</label> bhavataścātra snehabheṣajatoyānāṃ
