            tṛṇamūrcchonmādakārakaḥ | śīte vātakaphārtasya gauravāruciśūlakṛt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.24"><label>ci.31.24</label> snehapītasya cettṛṣṇā
            pibeduṣṇodakaṃ naraḥ | evaṃ cānupaśāmyantyāṃ snehamuṣṇāmbunā vamet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.25"><label>ci.31.25</label> dihyācchītaiḥ śiraḥ śītaṃ toyaṃ
            cāpyavagāhayet | yā mātrā parijīryeta caturbhāgagate 'hani || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.26"><label>ci.31.26</label> sā mātrā dīpayatyagnimalpadoṣe ca
            pūjitā | yā mātrā parijīryeta tathā 'rdhadivase gate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.27"><label>ci.31.27</label> sā vṛṣyā bṛṃhaṇī yā ca madhyadoṣe
            ca pūjitā | yā mātrā parijīryeta caturbhāgāvaśeṣite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.28"><label>ci.31.28</label> snehanīyā ca sā mātrā bahudoṣe ca
            pūjitā | yā mātrā parijīryet tu tathā pariṇate 'hani || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.29"><label>ci.31.29</label> glānimūrcchāmadān hitvā sā mātrā
            pūjitā bhavet | ahorātrādasaṃduṣṭā yā mātrā parijīryati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.30"><label>ci.31.30</label> sā tu
            kuṣṭhavoṣonmādagrahāpasmāranāśinī | yathāgni prathamāṃ mātrāṃ pāyayeta
            vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.31"><label>ci.31.31</label> pīto hyatibahuḥ sneho janayet
            prāṇasaṃśayam | mithyācārādbahutvādvā yasya sneho na jīryati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.32"><label>ci.31.32</label> viṣṭabhya cāpi jīryettaṃ
            vāriṇoṣṇena vāmayet | tataḥ snehaṃ punardadyāllaghukoṣṭhāya dehine |
            jīrṇājīrṇaviśaṅkāyāṃ snehasyoṣṇodakaṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.33"><label>ci.31.33</label> tenodgāro bhavecchuddho bhaktaṃ
            rucis tathā | syuḥ pacyamāne tṛḍdāhabhramasādāratiklamāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.34"><label>ci.31.34</label> pariṣicyādbhiruṣṇābhirjīrṇasnehaṃ
            tato naram | yavāgūṃ pāyayeccoṣṇāṃ kāmaṃ klinnālpataṇḍulām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.35"><label>ci.31.35</label> deyau yūṣarasau vā 'pi sugandhī
            snehavarjitau | kṛtau vā 'tyalpasarpiṣkau vilepī vā<ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref> vidhīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.36"><label>ci.31.36</label> pibettryahaṃ caturahaṃ pañcāhaṃ
            ṣaḍahaṃ tathā | saptarātrāt paraṃ snehaḥ sātmyībhavati sevitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.37"><label>ci.31.37</label> sukumāraṃ kṛśaṃ vṛddhaṃ śiśuṃ
            snehadviṣaṃ tathā | tṛṣṇārtamuṣṇakāle ca saha bhaktena pāyayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.38"><label>ci.31.38</label> pippalyo lavaṇaṃ snehāścatvāro
            dadhimastukaḥ | pītamaikadhyametaddhi sadyaḥsnehanamucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.39"><label>ci.31.39</label> bhṛṣṭā māṃsarase snigdhā yavāgūḥ
            sūpakalpitā | <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>prakṣudrā
            pīyamānā tu sadyaḥsnehanamucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.40"><label>ci.31.40</label> sarpiṣmatī payaḥsiddhā yavāgūḥ
            svalpataṇḍulā | sasvoṣṇā sevyamānā tu sadyaḥsnehanamucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.41"><label>ci.31.41</label> pippalyo lavaṇaṃ sarpistilapiṣṭaṃ
            varāhajā | vasā ca pītamaikadhyaṃ sadyaḥsnehanamucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.42"><label>ci.31.42</label> śarkarācūrṇasaṃsṛṣṭe dohanasthe
            ghṛte tu gām | dugdhvā kṣīraṃ pibedrūkṣaḥ sadyaḥsnehanamucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.43"><label>ci.31.43</label> yavakolakulatthānāṃ kvātho
            māgadhikānvitaḥ | payo dadhi surā ceti ghṛtamapyaṣṭamaṃ bhavet<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.44"><label>ci.31.44</label> siddhametairghṛtaṃ pītaṃ
            sadyaḥsnehanam uttamam | rājñe rājasamebhyo vā deyametadghṛtottamam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.45"><label>ci.31.45</label> balahīneṣu vṛddheṣu
            mṛdvagnistrīhatātmasu | alpadoṣeṣu yojyāḥ syurye yogāḥ samyagīritāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.46"><label>ci.31.46</label> vivarjayet snehapānamajīrṇī
              taruṇajvarī<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> |
            durbalo 'rocakī sthūlo mūrcchārto madapīḍitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.47"><label>ci.31.47</label> chardyarditaḥ pipāsārtaḥ śrāntaḥ
            pānaklamānvitaḥ | dattabastirviriktaś ca vānto yaś cāpi mānavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.48"><label>ci.31.48</label> akāle durdine caiva na ca snehaṃ
            pibennaraḥ | akāle ca prasūtā strī snehapānaṃ vivarjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.49"><label>ci.31.49</label> snehapānādbhavantyeṣāṃ nṝṇāṃ
            nānāvidhā gadāḥ | gadā vā kṛcchratāṃ yānti na sidhyantyathavā punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.50"><label>ci.31.50</label> garbhāśaye 'vaśeṣāḥ syū
            raktakledamalāstataḥ | snehaṃ jahyānniṣeveta pācanaṃ rūkṣam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.51"><label>ci.31.51</label> daśarātrāttataḥ snehaṃ
            yathāvadavacārayet | purīṣaṃ grathitaṃ rūkṣaṃ kṛcchrādannaṃ vipacyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.52"><label>ci.31.52</label> uro vidahate vāyuḥ koṣṭhād upari
            dhāvati | durvarṇo durbalaścaiva rūkṣo bhavati mānavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.53"><label>ci.31.53</label> susnigdhā tvagviṭśaithilyaṃ
            dīpto 'gnir mṛdugātratā | glānir lāghavam aṅgānām adhastāt snehadarśanam |
            samyaksnigdhasya liṅgāni snehodvegas tathaiva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.54"><label>ci.31.54</label> bhaktadveṣo mukhasrāvo gudadāhaḥ
            pravāhikā | purīṣātipravṛttiś ca bhṛśasnigdhasya lakṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.55"><label>ci.31.55</label> rūkṣasya snehanaṃ snehair
            atisnigdhasya rūkṣaṇam | śyāmākakoradūṣānnatakrapiṇyākaśaktubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.56"><label>ci.31.56</label> dīptāntaragniḥ pariśuddhakoṣṭhaḥ
            pratyagradhāturbalavarṇayuktaḥ | dṛḍhendriyo mandajaraḥ śatāyuḥ
              snehopasevī<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> puruṣo
            bhavet tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.31.57"><label>ci.31.57</label> sneho hito
            durbalahnidehasandhukṣaṇe vyādhinipīḍitasya | balānvitau bhojanadoṣajātaiḥ
            pramardituṃ tau sahasā na sādhyau ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne snehopayaugikacikitsitaṃ
            nāmaikatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||31 ||</p>
        </div>
        
        
        <div n="32" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>dvātriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.1"><label>ci.32.1</label> athātaḥ svedāvacāraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.2"><label>ci.32.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.3"><label>ci.32.3</label> caturvidhaḥ svedaḥ tadyathā
            tāpasveda, ūṣmasveda, upanāhasvedo, dravasveda iti atra
            sarvasvedavikalpāvarodhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.4"><label>ci.32.4</label> tatra tāpasvedaḥ
            pāṇikāṃsyakandukakapālavālukāvastraiḥ prayujyate, śayānasya cāṅgatāpo
            bahuśaḥ khādirāṅgārairiti<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.5"><label>ci.32.5</label> ūṣmasvedastu
            kapālapāṣāśeṣṭakālohapiṇḍānagnivarṇānadbhirāsiñcedamladravyair vā,
            tairārdrālaktakapariveṣṭitair aṅgapradeśaṃ<ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref> svedayet |
            māṃsarasapayodadhisnehadhānyāmlavātaharapatrabhaṅgakvāthapūrṇāṃ vā
            kumbhīmanutaptāṃ prāvṛtyoṣmāṇaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | pārśvacchidreṇa vā
            kumbhenādhomukhena tasyā mukham abhisandhāya tasmiñchidrehastiśuṇḍākārāṃ
            nāḍīṃ praṇidhāya taṃ svedayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.6"><label>ci.32.6</label> sukhopaviṣṭaṃ svabhyaktaṃ
            guruprāvaraṇāvṛtam | hastiśuṇḍikayā nāḍyā svedayedvātarogiṇam | sukhā
            sarvāṅgagā hyeṣā na ca kliśnāti mānavam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.7"><label>ci.32.7</label> vyāmārdhamātrā trirvakrā
            hastihastasamākṛtiḥ | svedanārthe hitā nāḍī kailiñjī hastiśuṇḍikā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.8"><label>ci.32.8</label> puruṣāyāmamātrāṃ ca bhūmimutkīrya
            khādiraiḥ | kāṣṭhairdagdhvā tathā 'bhyukṣya kṣīradhānyāmlavāribhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.9"><label>ci.32.9</label> patrabhaṅgair avacchādya śayānaṃ
            svedayettataḥ | pūrvavat svedayeddagdhvā bhasmāpohyāpi vā śilām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.10"><label>ci.32.10</label> pūrvavat kuṭīṃ vā caturdvārāṃ
            kṛtvā tasyām upaviṣṭasyāntaścaturdvāre 'ṅgārānupasandhāya taṃ svedayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.11"><label>ci.32.11</label>
            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>kośadhānyāni vā
            samyagupasvedyāstīrya kiliñje 'nyasmin vā tatpratirūpake śayānaṃ prāvṛtya
            svedayet; evaṃ pāṃśugośakṛttuṣabusapalāloṣm abhiḥ svedayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.12"><label>ci.32.12</label> upanāhasvedastu
            vātaharamūlakalkair amlapiṣṭairlavaṇapragāḍhaiḥ susnigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇaiḥ
            pradihya svedayet | evaṃ kākolyādibhirelādibhiḥ
            surasādibhistilātasīsarṣapakalkaiḥ kṛśarāpāyasotkārikābhirveśavāraiḥ
            sālvaṇair vā tanuvastrāvanaddhaiḥ svedayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.13"><label>ci.32.13</label> dravasvedastu
            vātaharadravyakvāthapūrṇe koṣṇakaṭāhe<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
              >*</ref> droṇyāṃ vā 'vagāhya svedayet, evaṃ
            payomāṃsarasayūṣatailadhānyāmlaghṛtavasāmūtreṣv avagāheta; etaireva <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>sukhoṣṇaiḥ kaṣāyaiśca
            pariṣiñcediti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.14"><label>ci.32.14</label> tatra tāpoṣmasvedau viśeṣataḥ
            śleṣmaghnau, upanāhasvedo vātaghnaḥ, anyatarasmin pittasaṃsṛṣṭe dravasveda
            iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.15"><label>ci.32.15</label> kaphamedonvite vāyau
            nivātātapaguruprāvaraṇaniyuddhādhvavyāyāmabhāraharaṇāmarṣaiḥ
            svedamutpādayediti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.16"><label>ci.32.16</label> bhavanti cātra caturvidho
            yo 'bhihito dvidhā svedaḥ prayujyate | sarvasminneva dehe tu dehasyāvayave
            tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.17"><label>ci.32.17</label> yeṣāṃ nasyaṃ vidhātavyaṃ
            bastiścaiva hi dehinām | śodhanīyāś ca ye kecit pūrvaṃ svedyās tu te matāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.18"><label>ci.32.18</label> paścāt svedyā hṛte śalye
            mūḍhagarbhā 'nupadravā | samyak prajātā kāle yā paścāt svedyā vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.19"><label>ci.32.19</label> svedyaḥ pūrvaṃ ca paścācca
            bhagandaryarśasas tathā | aśmaryā cāturo jantuḥ śeṣāñchāstre pracakṣmahe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.20"><label>ci.32.20</label> nānabhyakte nāpi cāsnigdhadehe
            svedo yojyaḥ svedavidbhiḥ kathañcit | dṛṣṭaṃ loke kāṣṭhamasnigdhamāśu
            gacchedbhaṅgaṃ svedayogairgṛhītam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.21"><label>ci.32.21</label> snehaklinnā dhātusaṃsthāś ca doṣāḥ
            svasthānasthā ye ca mārgeṣu līnāḥ | samyak svedairyojitais te dravatvaṃ
            prāptāḥ koṣṭhaṃ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>śodhanairyāntyaśeṣam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.22"><label>ci.32.22</label> agnerdīptiṃ mārdavaṃ tvakprasādaṃ
            bhaktaśraddhāṃ srotasāṃ nirmalatvam | kuryāt svedo hanti nidrāṃ satandrāṃ
            sandhīn stabdhāṃśceṣṭayedāśu yuktaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.23"><label>ci.32.23</label> svedāsrāvo vyādhihānirlaghutvaṃ
            śītārthitvaṃ mārdavaṃ cāturasya | samyaksvinne lakṣaṇaṃ
            prāhuretanmithyāsvinne vyatyayenaitadeva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.24"><label>ci.32.24</label> svinne 'tyarthaṃ sandhipīḍā
            vidāhaḥ sphoṭotpattiḥ pittaraktaprakopaḥ | mūrcchā bhrāntirdāhatṛṣṇe klamaśca
            kuryāttūrṇaṃ tatra śītaṃ vidhānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.25"><label>ci.32.25</label> pāṇḍurmehī pittaraktī kṣayārtaḥ
            kṣāmo 'jīrṇī <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>codarārto
            viṣārtaḥ | tṛḍcchardyārto garbhiṇī pītamadyo <ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref>naite svedyā yaś ca martyo<ref
              rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref>atisārī | svedādeṣāṃ yānti
            dehā vināśaṃ nosādhyatvaṃ yānti caiṣāṃ vikārāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.26"><label>ci.32.26</label> svedaiḥ sādhyo
            durbalo 'jīrṇabhaktaḥ syātāṃ ceddvau svedanīyau tatastau | eteṣāṃ svedasādhyā
            ye vyādhayasteṣu buddhimān | mṛdūn svedān prayuñjīta tathā hṛnmuṣkadṛṣṭiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.27"><label>ci.32.27</label> sarvān svedānnivāte ca
            jīrṇānnasyāvacārayet | snehābhyaktaśarīrasya śītairācchādya cakṣuṣī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.28"><label>ci.32.28</label> svidyamānasya ca muhurhṛdayaṃ
            śītalaiḥ spṛśet | samyaksvinnaṃ vimṛditaṃ snātamuṣṇāmbubhiḥ śanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.32.29"><label>ci.32.29</label> svabhyaktaṃ prāvṛtāṅgaṃ ca
            nivātaśaraṇasthitam | bhojayedanabhiṣyandi sarvaṃ cācāram ādiśet ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne svedāvacāraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ
            nāma dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||32 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="33" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>trayastriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.1"><label>ci.33.1</label> athāto
            vamanavirecanasādhyopadravacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.2"><label>ci.33.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.3"><label>ci.33.3</label> doṣāḥ kṣīṇā bṛṃhayitavyāḥ, kupitāḥ
            praśamayitavyāḥ, vṛddhā nirhartavyāḥ, samāḥ paripālyā iti siddhāntaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.4"><label>ci.33.4</label> prādhānyena vamanavirecane vartate
            nirharaṇe doṣāṇām | tasmāttayorvidhānamucyamānam upadhāraya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.5"><label>ci.33.5</label> athāturaṃ snigdhaṃ
            svinnam abhiṣyandibhirāhārair anavabaddhadoṣamavalokya śvo vamanaṃ
            pāyayitā 'smīti saṃbhojayettīkṣṇāgniṃ balavantaṃ bahudoṣaṃ mahāvyādhiparītaṃ
            vamanasātmyaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.6"><label>ci.33.6</label> bhavati cātra peśalairvividhair
            annairdoṣānutkleśya dehinaḥ | snigdhasvinnāya vamanaṃ dattaṃ samyak
            pravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.7"><label>ci.33.7</label> athāparedyuḥ pūrvāhṇe sādhāraṇe
            kāle vamanadravyakaṣāyakalkacūrṇasnehānām anyatamasya mātrāṃ pāyayitvā
            vāmayedyathāyogaṃ koṣṭhaviśeṣamavekṣya; asātmyabībhatsadurgandhadurdarśanāni
            ca vamanāni vidadhyāt, ato viparītāni virecanāni; tatra sukumāraṃ kṛśaṃ
            bālaṃ vṛddhaṃ bhīruṃ vā vamanasādhyeṣu vikāreṣu
            kṣīradadhitakrayavāgūnāmanyatamamākaṇṭhaṃ pāyayet, pītauṣadhaṃ ca
            pāṇibhiragnitaptaiḥ pratāpyamānaṃ muhūrtamupekṣeta; tasya ca
            svedaprādurbhāveṇa śithilatāmāpannaṃ svebhyaḥ sthānebhyaḥ pracalitaṃ
            kukṣimanusṛtaṃ jānīyāt, tataḥ pravṛttahṛllāsaṃ jñātvā
            jānumātrāsanopaviṣṭamāptairlalāṭe pṛṣṭhe pārśvayoḥ kaṇṭhe ca pāṇibhiḥ
            suparigṛhītamaṅgulīgandharvahastotpalanālānām anyatamena kaṇṭham abhispṛśantaṃ
            vāmayettāvadyāvat samyagvāntaliṅgānīti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.8"><label>ci.33.8</label> bhavataścātra kaphaprasekaṃ
            hṛdyāviśuddhiṃ kaṇḍūṃ ca duścharditaliṅgamāhuḥ | pittātiyogaṃ ca cisaṃjñatāṃ
            ca hṛtkaṇṭhapīḍām api cātivānte || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.9"><label>ci.33.9</label> pitte kaphasyānu sukhaṃ pravṛtte
            śuddheṣu hṛtkaṇṭhaśiraḥsu cāpi | laghau ca dehe kaphasaṃsrave ca sthite
            suvāntaṃ puruṣaṃ vyavasyet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.10"><label>ci.33.10</label> samyagvāntaṃ cainam abhisamīkṣya
            snehanavirecanaśamanānāṃ dhūmānām anyatamaṃ sāmarthyataḥ
            pāyayitvā++ācārikam ādiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.11"><label>ci.33.11</label> bhavanti cātra tato 'parāhṇe
            śuciśuddhadehamuṣṇābhiraddbhiḥ pariṣiktagātram | kulatthamudgāḍhakijāṅgalānāṃ
            yūṣai rasair vā 'pyupabhojayet tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.12"><label>ci.33.12</label>
            kāsopalepasvarabhedanidrātandrāsyadaurgandhyaviṣopasargāḥ |
            kaphaprasekagrahaṇīpradoṣā na santi jantorvamataḥ kadācit || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.13"><label>ci.33.13</label> chinne tarau puṣpaphalaprarohā
            yathā vināśaṃ sahasā vrajanti | tathā hṛte śleṣmaṇi śodhanena tajjā vikārāḥ
            praśamaṃ prayānti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.14"><label>ci.33.14</label> na
              vāmayettaimirikordhvavātagulmodaraplīhakṛmiśramārtān<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> |
            sthūlakṣatakṣīṇakṛśātivṛddhamūtrāturān kevalavātarogān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.15"><label>ci.33.15</label>
            svaropaghātādhyayanaprasaktaduśchardiduḥkoṣṭhatṛḍārtabālām |
            ūrdhvāsrapittikṣudhitātirūkṣagarbhiṇyudāvartirūhitāṃś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.16"><label>ci.33.16</label> avamyavamanādrogāḥ kṛcchratāṃ
            yānti dehinām | asādhyatāṃ vā gacchanti naite vāmyāstataḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.17"><label>ci.33.17</label> ete 'pyajīrṇavyathitā vāmyā ye ca
            viṣāturāḥ | atīva colbaṇakaphāste ca syur madhukāmbunā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.18"><label>ci.33.18</label> vāmyāstu
            viṣaśoṣastanyadoṣamandāgnyunmādāpasmāraślīpadārbudavidārikāmedomehagarajvarārucyapacyāmātīsārahṛdrogacittavibhramavisarpavidradhyajīrṇamukhaprasekahṛllāsaśvāsakāsapīnasapūtīnāsakaṇṭhauṣṭhavaktrapākakarṇasrāvādhijihvopajihvikāgalaśuṇḍikādhaḥśoṇitapittinaḥ
            kaphasthānajeṣu vikāreṣv anye ca kaphavyādhiparītā iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.19"><label>ci.33.19</label> virecanam api snigdhasvinnāya
            vāntāya ca deyam; avāntasya hi samyagviriktasyāpi sato 'dhaḥ srastaḥ śleṣmā
            grahaṇīṃ chādayati, gauravamāpādayati, pravāhikāṃ vā janayati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.20"><label>ci.33.20</label> athāturaṃ śvo virecanaṃ
            pāyayitā 'smīti pūrvāhṇe laghu bhojayet, phalāmlamuṣṇodakaṃ cainamanupāyayet |
            athāpare 'hani vigataśleṣmadhātumāturopakramaṇīyādavekṣyāturamathāsmai
            auṣadhamātrāṃ pātuṃ prayacchet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.21"><label>ci.33.21</label> tatra mṛduḥ, krūro, madhyama iti
            trividhaḥ koṣṭho bhavati | tatra bahupitto mṛduḥ, sa dugdhenāpi viricyate;
            bahuvātaśleṣmā krūraḥ, sa durvirecyaḥ; samadoṣo madhyamaḥ, sa sādhāraṇa iti |
            tatra mṛdau mātrā mṛdvī, tīkṣṇā krūre, madhye madhyā kartavyeti | pītauṣadhaś
            ca tanmanāḥ śayyābhyāśe virecyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.22"><label>ci.33.22</label> virecanaṃ pītavāṃs tu na vegān
            dhārayedbudhaḥ | nivātaśāyī śītāmbu na spṛśenna pravāhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.23"><label>ci.33.23</label> yathā ca vamane
            prasekauṣadhakaphapittānilāḥ krameṇa gacchanti, evaṃ virecane
            mūtrapurīṣapittauṣadhakaphā iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.24"><label>ci.33.24</label> bhavanti cātra hṛtkukṣyaśuddhiḥ
            paridāhakaṇḍūviṇmūtrasaṅgāś ca na sadvirikte | mūrcchāgudabhraṃśakaphātiyogāḥ
            śūlodgamaścātiviriktaliṅgam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.25"><label>ci.33.25</label> gateṣu doṣeṣu kaphānviteṣu
              nābhyā<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> laghutve manasaś
            ca tuṣṭau | gate 'nile cāpyanulomabhāvaṃ samyagviriktaṃ manujaṃ vyavasyet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.26"><label>ci.33.26</label> mandāgnimakṣīṇamasadviriktaṃ na
            pāyayetāhani tatra peyām | kṣīṇaṃ tṛṣārtaṃ suvirecitaṃ ca tanvīṃ sukhoṣṇāṃ
            laghu pāyayec ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.27"><label>ci.33.27</label> buddheḥ prasādaṃ balamindiryāṇāṃ
            dhātusthiratvaṃ balamagnidīptim | cirāc ca pākaṃ vayasaḥ karoti virecanaṃ
            samyagupāsyamānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.28"><label>ci.33.28</label> yathaudakānāmudake 'panīte
            carasthirāṇāṃ bhavati praṇāśaḥ | pitte hṛte tvevam upadravāṇāṃ pittātmakānāṃ
            bhavati praṇāśaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.29"><label>ci.33.29</label>
            mandāgnyatisnehitabālavṛddhasthūlāḥ kṣatakṣīṇabhayopataptāḥ |
            śrāntastṛṣārto 'parijīrṇabhakto garbhiṇyadho gacchati yasya cāsṛk || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.30"><label>ci.33.30</label> navapraviśyāyamadātyayī ca
            navajravī yā ca navaprasūtā | śalyārditāścāpyavirecanīyāḥ snehādibhirye
            tvanupaskṛtāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.31"><label>ci.33.31</label> virecanairyānti narā
            vināśamajñaprayuktair avirecanīyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.32"><label>ci.33.32</label> virecyās tu
            jvaragarārucyarśo 'rbudodaragranthividradhipāṇḍurogāpasmārahṛdrogavātaraktabhagandaracchardiyonirogavisarpagulmapakvāśayarugvibandhavisūcikālasakamūtrāghātakuṣṭhavisphoṭakapramehānāhaplīhaśophavṛddhiśastrakṣatakṣārāgnidagdhaduṣṭavraṇākṣipākakācatimirābhiṣyandaśiraḥkarṇākṣināsāsyagudameḍhradāhordhvaraktapittakṛmikoṣṭhinaḥ
            pittasthānajeṣv anyeṣu ca vikāreṣv anye ca paittikavyādhiparītā iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.33"><label>ci.33.33</label>
            saratvasaukṣmyataikṣṇyauṣṇyavikāśitvairvirecanam | vamanaṃ tu hareddoṣaṃ
            prakṛtyā gatamanyathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.34"><label>ci.33.34</label> yātyadho doṣamādāya pacyamānaṃ
            virecanam | guṇotkarṣāhvrajatyūrdhvamapakvaṃ vamanaṃ punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.35"><label>ci.33.35</label> mṛdukoṣṭhasya dīptāgneratitīkṣṇaṃ
            virecanam | na samyaṅnirhareddoṣānativegapradhāvitam<ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.36"><label>ci.33.36</label> pītaṃ yadauṣadhaṃ
            prātarbhuktapākasame kṣaṇe | paktiṃ gacchati doṣāṃś ca nirharettat
            praśasyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.37"><label>ci.33.37</label> durbalasya calān doṣānalpānalpān
            punaḥ punaḥ | haret prabhūtānakpāṃs tu śamayet pracyutānapi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.38"><label>ci.33.38</label> hareddoṣāṃścalān pakvān balino
            durbalasya vā | calā hyupekṣitā doṣāḥ kleśayeyuściraṃ naram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.39"><label>ci.33.39</label> mandāgniṃ krūrakoṣṭhaṃ ca
            sakṣāralavaṇairghṛtaiḥ | sandhukṣitāgniṃ snigdhaṃ ca svinnaṃ caiva
            virecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.40"><label>ci.33.40</label> snigdhasvinnasya
            bhaiṣajyairdoṣastūtkleśito balāt | nilīyate na mārgeṣu snigdhe bhāṇḍa
            ivodakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.41"><label>ci.33.41</label> na cātisnehapītas tu pibet
            snehavirecanam | doṣāḥ pracalitāḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
              >*</ref> sthānādbhūyaḥ śliṣyanti vartmasu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.42"><label>ci.33.42</label>
            viṣābhighātapiḍakāśophapāṇḍuvisarpiṇaḥ | nātisnigdhā viśodhyāḥ syustathā
            kuṣṭhipramehiṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.43"><label>ci.33.43</label> virūkṣya snehasātmyaṃ tu bhūyaḥ
            saṃsnehya śodhayet | tena doṣā hṛtāstasya bhavanti balavardhanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.44"><label>ci.33.44</label> prāgapītaṃ naraṃ śodhyaṃ
            pāyayetauṣadhaṃ mṛdu | tato vijñātakoṣṭhasya kāryaṃ saṃśodhanaṃ punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.45"><label>ci.33.45</label> sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaphalaṃ
            hṛdyamalpamātraṃ mahāguṇam | vyāpatsvalpātyayaṃ cāpi pibennṛpatirauṣadham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.46"><label>ci.33.46</label> snehasvedāvanabhyasya yastu
            saṃśodhanaṃ pibet | dāru śuṣkamivānāme dehastasya viśīryate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.47"><label>ci.33.47</label> snehasvedapracalitā rasaiḥ
            snigdhair udīritāḥ | doṣāḥ koṣṭhagatā jantoḥ sukhā hartuṃ viśodhanaiḥ ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
            vamanavirecanasādhyopadravacikitsitaṃ nāma trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||33 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="34" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>catustriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.1"><label>ci.34.1</label> athāto
            vamanavirecanavyāpaccikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.2"><label>ci.34.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.3"><label>ci.34.3</label> vaidyāturanimittaṃ vamanaṃ
            virecanaṃ ca pañcadaśadhā vyāpadyate | tatra vamanasyādho gatirūrdhvaṃ
            virecanasyeti pṛthak; sāmānyamubhayoḥ sāvaśeṣaudhatvaṃ, jīrṇauṣadhatvaṃ,
            hīnadoṣāpahṛtatvaṃ, vātaśūlam, ayogo, atiyogo, jīvādānam, ādhmānaṃ,
            parikartikā, parisrāvaḥ, pravāhikā, hṛdayopasaraṇaṃ, vibandha, aṅgapragraha
            iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.4"><label>ci.34.4</label> tatra
            bubhukṣāpīḍitasyātitīkṣṇāgnermṛdukoṣṭhasya cāvatiṣṭhamānaṃ durvamasya vā
            guṇasāmānyabhāvādvamanamadho gacchati, tatrepsitānavāptirdoṣotkleśaśca<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>; tamāśu snehayitvā
            bhūyastīkṣṇatarair vāmayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.5"><label>ci.34.5</label>
            apariśuddhāmāśayasyotkliṣṭaśleṣmaṇaḥ saśeṣānnasya vā 'hṛdyamatiprabhūtaṃ vā
            virecanaṃ pītamūrdhvaṃ gacchati, tatrepsitānavāptirdoṣokleśaśca<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>;
            tatrāśuddhāmāśayamulbaṇaśleṣmāṇamāśu vāmayitvā bhūyastīkṣṇatarairvirecayet,
            āmānvaye tvāmavat saṃvidhānam, ahṛdye 'tiprabhūte ca hṛdyaṃ pramāṇayuktaṃ ca;
            ata ūrdhvamuttiṣṭhatyauṣadhe na tṛtīyaṃ pāyayet, tatastvenaṃ
            madhughṛtaphāṇitayuktairlehairvirecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.6"><label>ci.34.6</label>
            doṣavigrathitamalpamauṣadhamavasthitamūrdhvabhāgikamadhobhāgikaṃ vā na
            sraṃsayati doṣān, tatra tṛṣṇā pārśvaśūlaṃ chardirmūrcchā parvabhedo
            hṛllāso 'ratirudgārāviśuddhiś ca bhavati; tamuṣṇābhiradbhirāśu
            vāmayedūrdhvabhāgike, adhobhāgike 'pi ca
            sāvaśeṣauṣadhamatipradhāvitadoṣamatibalamasamyagviriktalakṣaṇamapyevaṃ
            vāmayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.7"><label>ci.34.7</label>
            krūrakoṣṭhasyātitīkṣṇāgneralpamauṣadhamalpaguṇaṃ vā bhaktavat pākam upaiti,
            tatra samudīrṇā doṣā yathākālamanirhrīyamāṇā vyādhivibhramaṃ balavibhraṃśaṃ
            cāpādayanti, tamanalpamamandamauṣadhaṃ ca pāyayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.8"><label>ci.34.8</label> asnigdhasvinnenālpaguṇaṃ vā
            bheṣajam upayuktamalpān doṣān hanti; tatra vamane doṣaśeṣo gauravamutkleśaṃ
            hṛdayāviśuddhiṃ vyādhivṛddhiṃ ca karoti, tatra taṃ yathāyogaṃ pāyayitvā
            vāmayeddṛḍhataraṃ; virecane tu gudaparikartanamādhmānaṃ
            śirogauravamaniḥsaraṇaṃ vā vāyorvyādhivṛddhiṃ ca karoti; tam upapādya bhūyaḥ
            snehasvedābhyāṃ virecayeddṛḍhataraṃ, dṛḍhaṃ bahupracalitadoṣaṃ vā tṛtīye
            divase 'lpaguṇaṃ ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.9"><label>ci.34.9</label> asnigdhasvinnena
            rūkṣauṣadham upayuktamabrahmacāriṇā vā vāyuṃ kopayati, tatra vāyuḥ prakupitaḥ
            pārśvapṛṣṭhaśroṇimanyāmarmaśūlaṃ mūrcchāṃ bhramaṃ madaṃ saṃjñānāśaṃ ca
            karoti, taṃ vātaśūlamityācakṣate; tamabhyajya dhāvyasvedena svedayitvā
            yaṣṭīmadhukavipakvena tailenānuvāsayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.10"><label>ci.34.10</label>
            snehasvedābhyāmavibhāvitaśarīreṇālpamauṣadhamalpaguṇaṃ vā pītamūrdhvamadho
            vā nābhyeti doṣāṃścotkleśya taiḥ saha balakṣayamāpādayati, tatrādhmānaṃ
            hṛdayagrahastṛṣṇā mūrcchā dāhaś ca bhavati, tamayogamityācakṣate; tamāśu
            vāmayenmadanaphalalavaṇāmbubhirvirecayettīkṣṇataraiḥ kaṣāyaiś ca | durvāntasya
            tu samutkliṣṭādoṣā vyāpya śarīraṃ
            kaṇḍūśvayathukuṣṭhapiḍakājvarāṅgamardanistodanāni kurvanti,
            tatastānaśeṣānmadauṣadhenāpaharet | asnigdhasvinnasya durviriktasyādhonābheḥ
            stabdhapūrṇodaratā śūlaṃ vātapurīṣasaṅgaḥ kaṇḍūmaṇḍalaprādurbhāvo vā
            bhavati, tamāsthāpya punaḥ saṃsrehya virecayettīkṣṇena | nātipravartamāne
            tiṣṭhati vā duṣṭasaṃśodhane tatsantejanārthamuṣṇodakaṃ pāyayet, pāṇitāpaiśca
            pārśvodaram upasvedayet, tataḥ pravartante doṣāḥ | anupravṛtte cālpadoṣe
            jīrṇauṣadhaṃ bahudoṣamahaḥśeṣaṃ daśarātrādūrdhvam upasaṃskṛtadehaṃ
            snehasvedābhyāṃ bhūyaḥ śodhayet | durvirecyamāsthāpya punaḥ saṃsnehya
            virecayet | hrībhayalobhairvegāghātaśīlāḥ prāyaśaḥ striyo rājasamīpasthā
            vaṇijaḥ śrotriyāś ca bhavanti, tasmādete durvirecyāḥ, bahuvātatvāt; ata eva
            tānatisnigdhān svedopapannāñ śodhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.11"><label>ci.34.11</label>
            sngidhasvinnasyātimātramatimṛdukoṣṭhasya vā 'titīkṣṇamadhikaṃ vā
            dattamauṣadhamatiyogaṃ kuryāt | tatra vamanātiyoge
            pittātipravṛttirbalavisraṃso vātakopaś ca balavān bhavati, taṃ
            ghṛtenābhyajyāvagāhya śītāsvapsu śarkarāmadhumiśrairlehair upacaredyathāsvaṃ;
            virecanātiyoge kaphasyātipravṛttiruttarakālaṃ ca saraktasya, tatrāpi
            balavisraṃso vātakopaś ca balavān bhavati, <ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref>tamatiśītāmbubhiḥ
            pariṣicyāvagāhya vā śītais taṇḍulāmbubhirmadhumiśraiśchardayet, picchābastiṃ
            cāsmai dadyāt, kṣīrasarpiṣā cainamanuvāsayet, priyaṅgvādiṃ cāsmai
            taṇḍulāmbunā pātuṃ prayacchet, kṣīrarasayoścānyatareṇa bhojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.12"><label>ci.34.12</label> tasiminneva vamanātiyoge
            pravṛddhe śoṇitaṃ ṣṭhīvati chardayati vā, tatra
            jihvāniḥsaraṇamapasaraṇamakṣṇorvyāvṛttirhanusaṃhananaṃ tṛṣṇā hikkā jvaro
            vaisaṃjñyamityaupadravā bhavanti; tamajāsṛkcandanośīrāñjanalājacūrṇaiḥ
            saśarkarodakairmanthaṃ pāyayet, phalarasair vā saghṛtakṣaudraśarkaraiḥ
            śuṅgābhirvā vaṭādīnāṃ peyāṃ siddhāṃ sakṣaudrāṃ varcogrāhibhirvā, payasā
            jāṅgalarasena vā bhojayet, atisrutaśoṇitavidhānenopacaret; jihvāmatisarpitāṃ
            kaṭukalavaṇacūrṇapraghṛṣṭāṃ tiladrākṣāpraliptāṃ vā 'ntaḥ pīḍayet, antaḥ
            praviṣṭāyāmamlamanye tasya purastāt khādayeyuḥ; vyāvṛtte cākṣiṇī
            ghṛtābhyakte pīḍayet, tṛṣṇādiṣu ca yathāsvaṃ pratikurvīta, visaṃjñe
            veṇuvīṇāgītasvanaṃ śrāvayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.13"><label>ci.34.13</label> virecanātiyoge ca sacandrakaṃ
            salilamadhaḥ sravati tato māṃsadhāvanaprakāśamuttarakālaṃ jīvaśoṇitaṃ ca,
            tato gudaniḥsaraṇaṃ vepathurvamanātiyogopadravāścāsya bhavanti; tamapi
            niḥsrutaśoṇitavidhānenopacaret, niḥsarpitagudasya gudamabhyajya
            parisvedyāntaḥ pīḍayet kṣudrarogacikitsitaṃ vā vīkṣeta, vepathau
            vātavyādhividhānaṃ kurvīta, jihvāniḥsaraṇādiṣūktaḥ pratīkāraḥ, atipravṛtte
            vā jīvaśoṇite kāśmarīphalabadarīdūrvośīraiḥ śṛtena payasā
            ghṛtamaṇḍāñjanayuktena suśītenāsthāpayet,
            nyagrodhādikaṣāyekṣurasaghṛtaśoṇitasaṃsṛṣṭaiścainaṃ bastibhirupācaret,
            śoṇitaṣṭhīvane raktapittaraktātīsārakriyāścāsya vidhadhyāt, nyagrodhādiṃ
            cāsya vidadhyāt pānabhojaneṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.14"><label>ci.34.14</label> jīvaśoṇitaraktapittayośca
            jijñāsārthaṃ tasmin picuṃ plotaṃ vā kṣipet, yadyuṣṇodakaprakṣālitamapi
            vastraṃ rañjayati tajjīvaśoṇitamavagantavyaṃ; sabhaktaṃ ca śune
            dadyācchaktusaṃmiśraṃ vā, sa yadyupabhuñjīta tajjīvaśoṇitamavagantavyam;
            anyathā raktapittam iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.15"><label>ci.34.15</label> saśeṣānnena bahudoṣeṇa
            rūkṣeṇānilaprāyakoṣṭhenānuṣṇamasnigdhaṃ vā pītamauṣadhamādhmāpayati,
            tatrānilamūtrapurīṣasaṅgaḥ samunnaddhodaratā pārśvabhaṅgo
            gudabastinistodanaṃ bhaktāruciś ca bhavati, taṃ cādhmānamityācakṣate;
            tam upasvedyānāhavartidīpanabastikriyābhirupacaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.16"><label>ci.34.16</label> kṣāmeṇātimṛdukoṣṭhena mandāgninā
            rūkṣeṇa vā 'titīkṣṇoṣṇātilavaṇamatirūkṣaṃ vā pītamauṣadhaṃ pittānilau
            pradūṣya parikartikāmāpādayati, tatra gudanābhimeḍhrebastiśiraḥsu sadāhaṃ
            parikartanamanilasaṅgo vāyuviṣṭambho bhaktāruciś ca bhavati; tatra
            picchābastiryaṣṭīmadhukakṛṣṇatilakalkamadhughṛtayuktaḥ, śītāmbupariṣiktaṃ
            cainaṃ payasā bhuktavantaṃ ghṛtamaṇḍena yaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena tailena
            vā 'nuvāsayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.17"><label>ci.34.17</label> krūrakoṣṭhasyātiprabhūtadopasya
            mṛdvauṣadhamavacāritaṃ samutkliśya doṣānna niḥśeṣānapaharati, tataste doṣāḥ
            parisrāvamāpādayanti, tatra daurbalyodaraviṣṭambhārucigātrasadanāni
            bhavanti, savedanau cāsya pittaśleṣmāṇau parisravataḥ, taṃ
            parisrāvamityācakṣate;
            tamajakarṇadhavatiniśapalāśabalākaṣāyairmadhusaṃyuktairāsthāpayet,
            upaśāntadoṣaṃ snigdhaṃ ca bhūyaḥ saṃśodhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.18"><label>ci.34.18</label> atirūkṣe 'tisnigdhe vā <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>bheṣajamavacāritamaprāptaṃ
            vātavarca udīrayati vegāghātena vā, tadā pravāhikā bhavati; tatra savātaṃ
            sadāhaṃ saśūlaṃ guru picchilaṃ śvetaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ saraktaṃ vā bhṛśaṃ pravāhamāṇaḥ
            kapham upaviśati; tāṃ parisrāvavidhānenopacaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.19"><label>ci.34.19</label> yastūrdhvamadho vā bheṣajavegaṃ
            pravṛttamajñatvādvinihanti tasyopasaraṇaṃ hṛdi kurvanti doṣāḥ, tatra
            pradhānamarmasantāpādvedanābhiratyarthaṃ pīḍyamāno dantān kiṭakiṭāyate <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>udgatākṣo jihvāṃ svādati
            pratāmyatyacetāś ca bhavati, taṃ parivarjayanti mūrkhāḥ; tamabhyajya
            dhānyasvedena svedayet, yaṣṭimadhukasiddhena ca tailenānuvāsayet,
            śirovirecanaṃ cāsmai tīkṣṇaṃ vidadhyāt, tato yaṣṭimadhukamiśreṇa
            taṇḍulāmbunā chardayet, yathādoṣocchrāyeṇa cainaṃ bastibhirupācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.20"><label>ci.34.20</label> yastūrdhvamadho vā pravṛttadoṣaḥ
            śītāgāramudakamanilamanyadvā seveta, tasya doṣāḥ srotaḥsvavalīyamānā <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>ghānībhāvamāpannā
            vātamūtraśakṛdgrahamāpādya vibadhyante<ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref>, tasyāṭopo dāho jvaro vedanāś ca
            tīvrā bhavanti; tamāśu vāmayitvā prāptakālāṃ kriyāṃ kurvīta; adhobhāge
            tvadhobhāgadoṣaharadravyaṃ saindhavāmlamūtrasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ virecanāya pāyayet,
            āsthāpanamanuvāsanaṃ ca yathādoṣaṃ vidadhyāt, yathādoṣamāhārakramaṃ ca;
            ubhayatobhāge tūpadravaviśeṣān yathāsvaṃ pratikurvīta || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.21"><label>ci.34.21</label> yā tu virecane gudaparikartikā
            tadvamane kaṇṭhakṣaṇanaṃ, yadadhaḥ parisravaṇaṃ sa ūrdhvabhāge
            śleṣmaprasekaḥ, yā tvadhāḥ pravāhikā sā tūrdhvaṃ śuṣkodgārā iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.34.22"><label>ci.34.22</label> bhavati cātra yāstvetā vyāpadaḥ
            proktā daśa pañ ca ca tattvataḥ | etā virekātiyogaduryogāyogajāḥ smṛtāḥ ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
            vamanavirecanavyāpaccikitsitaṃ nāma catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||34 ||</p>
        </div>
        <div n="35" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>pañcatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.1"><label>ci.35.1</label> athāto
            netrabastipramāṇapravibhāgacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.2"><label>ci.35.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.3"><label>ci.35.3</label> tatra snehādīnāṃ karmaṇāṃ
            bastikarma pradhānatamamāhurācāryāḥ | kasmāt anekakarmakaratvādbasteḥ; iha
            khalu bastirnānāvidhadravyasaṃyogāddoṣāṇāṃ saṃśodhanasaṃśamanasaṃgrahaṇāni
            karoti, kṣīṇaśukraṃ vājīkaroti, kṛśaṃ bṛṃhayati, sthūlaṃ karśayati, cakṣuḥ
            prīṇayati, valīpalitamapahanti, vayaḥ sthāpayati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.4"><label>ci.35.4</label> śarīropacayaṃ varṇaṃ
            balamārogyamāyuṣaḥ | kurute parivṛddhiṃ ca bastiḥ samyagupāsitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.5"><label>ci.35.5</label> tathā
              jvarātīsāratimirapratiśyāyaśirorogādhimanthārditākṣepakapakṣāghātaikāṅgasarvāṅgarogādhmānodarayoniśūlaśarkarāśūlavṛddhyupadaṃśānāhamūtrakṛcchragulmavātaśoṇitavātamūtrapurīṣodāvartaśukrārtavastanyanāśahṛddhanumanyāgrahaśarkarāśmarīmūḍhagarbhaprabhṛtiṣu<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> cāsyartham upayujyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.6"><label>ci.35.6</label> bhavati cātra bastirvāte ca pitte
            ca kaphe rakte ca śasyate | saṃsarge sannipāte ca bastireva hitaḥ sadā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.7"><label>ci.35.7</label> tatra
            sāṃvatsarikāṣṭadviraṣṭavarṣāṇāṃ ṣaḍaṣṭadaśāṅgulapramāṇāni
            kaniṣṭhikānāmikāmadhyamāṅgulipariṇāhānyagre 'dhyardhāṅguladvyaṅgulārdhatṛtīyāṅgulasanniviṣṭakarṇikāni
            kaṅkaśyenabarhiṇapakṣanāḍītulyapraveśāni mudgamāṣakalāyamātrasrotāṃsi
            vidadhyānnetrāṇi | teṣu cāsthāpanadravyapramāṇamāturahastasaṃmitena prasṛtena
            saṃmitau prasṛtau dvau catvāro 'ṣṭau ca vidheyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.8"><label>ci.35.8</label> varṣāntareṣu<ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref> netrāṇāṃ bastimānasya caiva
            hi | vayobalaśarīrāṇi samīkṣyotkarṣayedvidhim<ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.9"><label>ci.35.9</label> pañcaviṃśaterūrdhvaṃ dvādaśāṅgulaṃ,
            mūle 'ṅguṣṭhodaraparīṇāham, agre kaniṣṭhikodaraparīṇāham, agre
            tryaṅgulasanniviṣṭakarṇikaṃ, gṛdhrapakṣanāḍīṃtulyapraveśaṃ,
            kolāsthimātrachidraṃ, klinnakalāyamātrachidramityeke; sarvāṇi mūle
            bastinibandhanārthaṃ dvikarṇikāni | āsthāpanadravyapraṇāṇaṃ tu vihitaṃ
            dvādaśaprasṛtāḥ | saptatestūrdhvaṃ netrapramāṇametadeva, dravyapramāṇaṃ tu
            dviraṣṭavarṣavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.10"><label>ci.35.10</label> mṛdurbastiḥ prayoktavyo
            viśeṣādbālavṛddhayoḥ | tayostīkṣṇaḥ prayuktas tu bastirhiṃsyād balāyuṣī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.11"><label>ci.35.11</label> (<ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref>vraṇanetramaṣṭāṅgulaṃ
            mudgavāhisrotaḥ; vraṇamavekṣya yathāsvaṃ snehakaṣāye vidadhīta ||) </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.12"><label>ci.35.12</label> tatra netrāṇi
            suvarṇarajatatāmrāyorītidantaśṛṅgamaṇitarusāramayāni ślakṣṇāni dṛḍhāni
            gopucchākṛtīnyṛjūni guṭikāmukhāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.13"><label>ci.35.13</label> bastayaś ca <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>bandhyā mṛdavo nātivahalā
            dṛḍhāḥ pramāṇavanto gomahiṣavarāhājorabhrāṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.14"><label>ci.35.14</label> netrālābhe hitā nāḍī
            nalavaṃśāsthisaṃbhavā | bastyalābhe hitaṃ carma sūkṣmaṃ vā tāntavaṃ ghanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.15"><label>ci.35.15</label> bastiṃ nirupadigdhaṃ tu śuddhaṃ
            suparimārjitam | mṛdvanuddhatahīnaṃ ca muhuḥ snehavimarditam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.16"><label>ci.35.16</label> netrāmūle pratiṣṭhāpya nyubjaṃ tu
            vivṛtānanam | baddhvā lohena taptena carmasrotasi nirdahet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.17"><label>ci.35.17</label> parivartya tato bastiṃ baddhvā
            guptaṃ nidhāpayet | āsthāpanaṃ ca tailaṃ ca yathāvattena dāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.18"><label>ci.35.18</label> tatra dvividho bastiḥ nairūhikaḥ,
            snaihikaś ca | āsthāpanaṃ, nirūha ityanarthāntaraṃ; tasya vikalpo
            mādhutailikaḥ; tasya prayāyaśabdo yāpano, yuktarathaḥ, siddhabastiriti | sa
            doṣanirharaṇāccharīranīrohaṇādvā nirūhaḥ, bayaḥsthāpanādāyuḥsthāpanādvā
            āsthāpanam | mādhutailikavidhānaṃ ca nirūhopakramacikitsite vakṣyāmaḥ |
              yathāpramāṇaguṇavihitaḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>
            snehabastivikalpo 'nuvāsanaḥ pādāva(pādāpa)kṛṣṭaḥ | anuvasannapi na
            duṣyatyanudivasaṃ vā dīyata ityanuvāsanaḥ | tasyāpi vikalpo+<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>ardhārdhamātrāvakṛṣṭo 'parihāryo mātrābastiriti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.19"><label>ci.35.19</label> nirūhaḥ śodhano lekhī snaihiko
            bṛṃhaṇo mataḥ | nirūhaśodhitānmārgān samyak sneho 'nugacchati |
            apetasarvadoṣāsu nāḍīṣviva vahajjalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.20"><label>ci.35.20</label> sarvadoṣaharaścāsau śarīrasya ca
            jīvanaḥ | tasmādviśuddhadehasya snehabastirvidhīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.21"><label>ci.35.21</label>
            tatronmādabhayaśokapipāsārocakājīrṇārśaḥpāṇḍurogabhramamadamūrcchācchardikuṣṭhamehodarasthaulyaśvāsakāsakaṇṭhaśoṣaśophopasṛṣṭakṣatakṣīṇacatustrimāsagarbhiṇīdurbalāgnyasahā

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.22"><label>ci.35.22</label> udarī ca pramehī ca kuṣṭhī
            sthūlaś ca mānavaḥ | avaśyaṃ sthāpanīyāste nānuvāsyāḥ kathañcana || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.23"><label>ci.35.23</label> asādhyatā vikārāṇāṃ
            syād eṣāmanuvāsanāt | asādhyatve 'pi bhūyiṣṭhaṃ gātrāṇāṃ sadanaṃ bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.24"><label>ci.35.24</label> pakvāśaye tathā śroṇyāṃ
            nābhyadhastāc ca sarvataḥ | samyakpraṇihito bastiḥ sthāneṣveteṣu tiṣṭhati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.25"><label>ci.35.25</label> pakvāśayādbastivīryaṃ
            khairdehamanusarpati | vṛkṣamūle niṣiktānāmapāṃ vīryamiva drumam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.26"><label>ci.35.26</label> sa cāpi sahasā bastiḥ kevalaḥ
            samalo 'pi vā | pratyeti vīryaṃ tvanilair apānādyairvinīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.27"><label>ci.35.27</label> vīryeṇa bastirādatte
            doṣānāpādamastakāt(n) | pakvāśayastho 'mbarago bhūmerarko rasāniva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.28"><label>ci.35.28</label> sa kaṭīpṛṣṭhakoṣṭhasthān
            vīryeṇāloḍya saṃcayān | utkhātamūlān harati doṣāṇāṃ sādhuyojitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.29"><label>ci.35.29</label> doṣatrayasya yasmāc ca prakope
            vāyurīśvaraḥ | tasmāttasyātivṛddhasya śarīram abhinighnataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.30"><label>ci.35.30</label> vāyorviṣahate vegaṃ nānyā
            basterṛte kriyā | pavanāviddhatoyasya velā vegamivodadheḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.31"><label>ci.35.31</label> śarīropacayaṃ varṇaṃ
            balamārogyamāyuṣaḥ | kurute parivṛddhiṃ ca bastiḥ samyagupāsitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.32"><label>ci.35.32</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ vyāpado vakṣyāmaḥ |
            tatra netraṃ vicalitaṃ, vivartitaṃ, pārśvāvapīḍitam, atyutkṣiptam,
            avasannaṃ, tiryakprakṣiptam iti ṣaṭ praṇidhānadoṣāḥ; atisthūlaṃ, karkaśam,
            avanataṃ, <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>aṇubhinnaṃ,
            sannikṛṣṭaviprakṛṣṭakarṇikaṃ, sūkṣmāticchidram, atidīrgham, <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>atihrasvam, asrimadityekādaśa
            netradoṣāḥ; bahalatā, alpatā, <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
              >*</ref>sacchidratā, prastīrṇatā, durbaddhateti pañ ca bastidoṣāḥ;
            atipīḍitatā, śithilapīḍitatā, bhūyo bhūyo 'vapīḍanaṃ, kālātikrama iti
            catvāraḥ pīḍanadoṣāḥ; āmatā, hīnatā, atimātratā, atiśītatā, atyuṣṇatā,
            atitīkṣṇatā, atimṛdutā, atisnigdhatā, atirūkṣatā, atisāndratā, atidravatā,
            ityekādaśa dravyadoṣāḥ;
            avākśīrṣocchīrṣanyubjottānasaṅkucitadehasthitadakṣiṇapārśvaśāyinaḥ
            pradānam iti sapta śayyādoṣāḥ; evam etāścatuścatvāriṃśadvyāpado
            vaidyanimittāḥ | āturanimittāḥ pañcadaśa āturopadravacikitsite vakṣyante |
            snehastvaṣṭabhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ pratihato na pratyāgacchati tribhirdoṣaiḥ,
            aśanābhibhūto, malavyāmiśro, dūrānupraviṣṭo, asvinnasya, anuṣṇo,
            alpambhuktavato, alpaś ceti vaidyāturanimittā bhavanti | ayogastūbhayoḥ,
            ādhmānaṃ, parikartikā, parisrāvaḥ, pravāhikā, hṛdayopasaraṇam, aṅgapragraho,
            atiyogo, jīvādānam iti nava vyāpado vaidyanimittā bhavanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.35.33"><label>ci.35.33</label> bhavati cātra ṣaṭsaptatiḥ
            samāsena vyāpadaḥ parikīrtitāḥ | tāsāṃ vakṣyāmi vijñānaṃ siddhiṃ ca
            tadanantaram ||</l>

            netrabastipramāṇapravibhāgacikitstitaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||35 ||</p>

          <head>ṣaṭtriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.1"><label>ci.36.1</label> athāto netrabastivyāpaccikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.2"><label>ci.36.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.3"><label>ci.36.3</label> atha netre vicalite tathā caiva
            vivartite | gude kṣataṃ rujā vā syāttatra sadyaḥkṣatakriyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.4"><label>ci.36.4</label> atyutkṣipte 'vasanne ca netre pāyau
            bhavedrujā | vidhiratrāpi pittaghnaḥ kāryaḥ snehaiś ca secanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.5"><label>ci.36.5</label> tiryakpraṇihite netre tathā
            pārśvāvapīḍite | mukhasyāvaraṇādbastirna samyak pratipadyate | ṛju netraṃ
            vidheyaṃ syāttatra samyagvijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.6"><label>ci.36.6</label> atisthūle karkaśe ca
              netre 'strimati<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> gharṣaṇāt |
            gude bhavet kṣataṃ ruk ca sādhanaṃ tasya pūrvavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.7"><label>ci.36.7</label>
            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>āsannakarṇike netre
            bhinne 'ṇau vā 'pyapārthakaḥ | avaseko bhavedbastestasmāddoṣān vivarjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.8"><label>ci.36.8</label> prakṛṣṭakarṇike raktaṃ
            gudamarmaprapīḍanāt | kṣaratyatrāpi pittaghno vidhirbastiś ca picchilaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.9"><label>ci.36.9</label> hrasve tvaṇusrotasi ca kleśo bastiś
            ca pūrvavat | pratyāgacchaṃstataḥ kuryād rogān bastivighātajān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.10"><label>ci.36.10</label> dīrghe mahāsrotasi ca
            jñeyamatyavapīḍavat | prastīrṇe bahale cāpi bastau durbaddhadoṣavat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.11"><label>ci.36.11</label> bastāvalpe 'lpatā vā 'pi
            dravyasyālpā guṇā matāḥ | durbaddhe <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
              >*</ref>cāṇubhinne ca vijñeyaṃ bhinnanetravat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.12"><label>ci.36.12</label> atiprapīḍito bastiḥ
              prayātyāmāśayaṃ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> tataḥ |
            vāterito nāsikābhyāṃ mukhato vā prapadyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.13"><label>ci.36.13</label> tatra tūrṇaṃ galāpīḍaṃ
            kuryāccāpyavadhūnanam | śiraḥkāyavirekau ca tīkṣṇau sekāṃś ca śītalān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.14"><label>ci.36.14</label> śanaiḥ prapīḍito bastiḥ
            pakvādhānaṃ ca gacchati | na ca saṃpādayatyarthaṃ tasmādyuktaṃ prapīḍayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.15"><label>ci.36.15</label> bhūyo bhūyo 'vapīḍena vāyurantaḥ
            prapīḍyate | tenādhmānaṃ rujaścogrā yathāsvaṃ tatra bastayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.16"><label>ci.36.16</label> kālātikramaṇāt kleśo
            vyādhiścābhipravardhate | tatra vyādhibalaghnaṃ tu bhūyo bastiṃ nidhāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.17"><label>ci.36.17</label> godopadehaśophau tu sneho 'pakvaḥ
            karoti hi | tatra saṃśodhano bastirhitaṃ cāpi virecanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.18"><label>ci.36.18</label> hīnamātrāvubhau bastī
            nātikāryakarau matau | atimātrau tathā++ānāhaklamātīsārakārakau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.19"><label>ci.36.19</label> mūrcchāṃ <ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref>dāhamatīsāraṃ pittaṃ
            cātyuṣṇatīkṣṇakau | mṛduśītāvubhau vātavibandhādhmānakārakau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.20"><label>ci.36.20</label> tatra hīnādiṣu hitaḥ pratyanīkaḥ
            kriyāvidhiḥ | gudabastyupadehaṃ tu kuryāt sāndro nirūhaṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.21"><label>ci.36.21</label> pravāhikāṃ vā
            janayettanuralpaguṇāvahaḥ | tatra sāndre tanuṃ bastiṃ tanau sāndraṃ ca
            dāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.22"><label>ci.36.22</label> snigdho 'tijāḍyakṛdrūkṣaḥ
            stambhādhmānakṛducyate | bastiṃ rūkṣamatisnigdhe snigdhaṃ rūkṣe ca dāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.23"><label>ci.36.23</label> atipīḍitavaddoṣān viddhi<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> cāpyavaśīrṣake | ucchīrṣake
            samunnāhaṃ bastiḥ kuryāc ca mehanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.24"><label>ci.36.24</label> tatrottaro hito bastiḥ
              susvinnasya<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> sukhāvahaḥ |
            nyubjasya bastirnāpnoti pakvādhānaṃ vimārgagaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.25"><label>ci.36.25</label> hṛdgudaṃ bādhate cātra vāyuḥ
            koṣṭhamathāpi ca | uttānasyāvṛte mārge bastirnāntaḥ prapadyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.26"><label>ci.36.26</label> netrasaṃvejanabhrānto vāyuścāntaḥ
            prakupyati | dehe saṅkucite dattaḥ sakthnorapyubhayos tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.27"><label>ci.36.27</label> na samyaganilāviṣṭo bastiḥ
            pratyeti dehinaḥ | sthitasya bastirdattas tu kṣipramāyātyavāṅmukhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.28"><label>ci.36.28</label> na cāśayaṃ tarpayati
            tasmānnārthakaro hi saḥ | nāpnoti bastirdattas tu kṛtsnaṃ pakvāśayaṃ punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.29"><label>ci.36.29</label> dakṣiṇāśritapārśvasya
            vāmapārśvānugo yataḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> |
            nyubjādīnāṃ pradānaṃ ca basternaiva praśasyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.30"><label>ci.36.30</label>
            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>paścād anilakopo 'tra yathāsvaṃ
            tatra kārayet | vyāpadaḥ snehabastes tu vakṣyante <ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref>taccikitsite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.31"><label>ci.36.31</label> ayogādyās tu vakṣyāmi vyāpadaḥ
            sacikitsitāḥ | anuṣṇo 'lpauṣadho hīno bastirnaiti prayojitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.32"><label>ci.36.32</label> viṣṭambhādhmānaśūlaiś ca tamayogaṃ
            pracakṣate | tatra tīkṣṇo hito bastistīkṣṇaṃ cāpi virecanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.33"><label>ci.36.33</label> saśeṣānne 'thavā bhukte bahudoṣe
            ca yojitaḥ | atyāśitasyātibahurbastirmandoṣṇa eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.34"><label>ci.36.34</label> anuṣṇalavaṇasneho
            hyatimātro 'thavā punaḥ | tathā bahupurīṣaṃ ca kṣipramādhmāpayennaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.35"><label>ci.36.35</label> hṛtkaṭīpārśvapṛṣṭheṣu śūlaṃ
            tatrātidāruṇam | tatra tīkṣṇataro bastirhitaṃ cāpyanuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.36"><label>ci.36.36</label> atitīkṣṇotilavaṇo rūkṣo bastiḥ
            prayojitaḥ | sapittaṃ kopayedvāyuṃ kuryāc ca parikartikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.37"><label>ci.36.37</label> nābhibastigudaṃ tatra
            chinattīvātidehinaḥ | picchābastirhitastasya snehaś ca madhuraiḥ śṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.38"><label>ci.36.38</label> atyamlalavaṇastīkṣṇaḥ parisrāvāya
            kalpate | daurbalyamaṅgasādaś ca jāyate tatra dehinaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.39"><label>ci.36.39</label> parisravettataḥ pittaṃ dāhaṃ
            sañjanayedgude | picchābastirhitas tatra bastiḥ kṣīraghṛtena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.40"><label>ci.36.40</label> pravāhikā bhavettīkṣṇānnirūhāt
            sānuvāsanāt | sadāhaśūlaṃ kṛcchreṇa kaphāsṛgupaveśyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.41"><label>ci.36.41</label> picchābastirhitas tatra payasā
            caiva bhojanam | sarpirmadhurakaiḥ siddhaṃ tailaṃ cāpyanuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.42"><label>ci.36.42</label> atitīkṣṇo nirūho vā savāte
            cānuvāsanaḥ | hṛdayasyopasaraṇaṃ kurute vā savāte cānuvāsanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.43"><label>ci.36.43</label> doṣais tatra rujastāstā mado
            mūrcchā 'ṅgagauravam | sarvadoṣaharaṃ bastiṃ śodhanaṃ tatra dāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.44"><label>ci.36.44</label> rūksasya bahuvātasya tathā
            duḥśāyitasya ca | bastiraṅgagrahaṃ kuryād rūkso mṛdvalpabheṣajaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.45"><label>ci.36.45</label> tatrāṅgasādaḥ prastambho
            jṛmbhodveṣṭanavepakāḥ | parvabhedaś ca tatreṣṭāḥ svedābhyañjanabastayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.46"><label>ci.36.46</label>
            atyuṣṇatīkṣṇo 'tibahurdatto 'tisveditasya ca | alpadoṣasya vā bastiratiyogāya
            kalpate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.47"><label>ci.36.47</label> virecanātiyogena samānaṃ tasya
            lakṣaṇam | picchābastiprayogaś ca tatra śītaḥ sukhāvahaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.48"><label>ci.36.48</label> atiyogāt paraṃ yatra jīvādānaṃ
            viriktavat | deyas tatra hitaścāpsu picchābastiḥ saśoṇitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.49"><label>ci.36.49</label> navaitā vyāpado yās tu nirūhaṃ
            pratyudāhṛtāḥ | snehabastiṣv api hi tā vijñeyāḥ kuśalairiha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.50"><label>ci.36.50</label> ity uktā vyāpadaḥ sarvāḥ
            salakṣaṇacikitsitāḥ | bhiṣajā ca tathā kāryaṃ yathaitā na bhavanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.36.51"><label>ci.36.51</label> paksādvireko vāntasya <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>tataś cāpi nirūhaṇam | sadyo
            nirūḍho 'nuvāsyaḥ saptarātrādvirecitaḥ ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne netrabastivyāpaccikitsitaṃ
            nāma ṣaṭtriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||36 ||</p>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.1"><label>ci.37.1</label> athāto 'nuvāsanottarabasticikitsitaṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.3"><label>ci.37.3</label> virecanāt saptarātre gate
            jātabalāya vai | kṛtānnāyānuvāsyāya samyagdeyo 'nuvāsanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.4"><label>ci.37.4</label> yathāvayo nirūhāṇāṃ yā mātrāḥ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.5"><label>ci.37.5</label> utsṛṣṭānilaviṇmūtre nare bastiṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.6"><label>ci.37.6</label> snehavastirvidheyas tu nāviśuddhasya

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.43"><label>ci.37.43</label> aśuddham api vātena
            kevalenātipīḍitam | ahorātrasya kāleṣu sarveṣvevānuvāsayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.44"><label>ci.37.44</label> rūkṣasya bahūvātasya dvau
            trīnapyanuvāsanān | dattvā snigdhatanuṃ jñātvā tataḥ paścānnirūhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.45"><label>ci.37.45</label> asnigdham api vātena
            kevalenātipīḍitam | snehapragāḍhairmatimānnirūhaiḥ samupācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.46"><label>ci.37.46</label> atha samyaṅgirūḍhaṃ tu
            vātādiṣvanuvāsayet | bilvayaṣṭyāhvamadanaphalatailairyathākramam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.47"><label>ci.37.47</label> rātrau bastiṃ na dadyāttu
            doṣotkleśo hi rātrijaḥ | snehavīryayutaḥ kuryādādhmānaṃ gauravaṃ jvaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.48"><label>ci.37.48</label> ahni sthānasthite doṣe vahnau
            cānnarasānvite | sphuṭasrotomukhe dehe snehaujaḥ parisarpati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.49"><label>ci.37.49</label> pitte 'dhike kaphe kṣīṇe rūkṣe
            vātarugardite | nare rātrau tu dātavyaṃ kāle coṣṇe 'nuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.50"><label>ci.37.50</label> uṣṇe pittādhike vā 'pi divā
            dāhādayo gadāḥ | saṃbhavanti <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>yatastasmāt pradoṣe yojayedbhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.51"><label>ci.37.51</label> śīte vasante ca divā
            grīṣmaprāvṛṅghanātyaye | snehyo dinānte pānoktān doṣān parijihīrṣatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.52"><label>ci.37.52</label> ahorātrasya kāleṣu
            sarveṣvevānilādhikam | tīvrāyāṃ ruji jīrṇānnaṃ bhojayitvā 'nuvāsayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.53"><label>ci.37.53</label> na cābhuktavataḥ snehaḥ
            praṇidheyaḥ kathañcana | śuddhatvāc chūnyakoṣṭhasya sneha ūrdhvaṃ samutpatet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.54"><label>ci.37.54</label> sadā 'nuvāsayeccāpi
            bhojayitvā++ārdrapāṇinam | jvaraṃ vidagdhabhuktasya kuryāt snehaḥ
            prayojitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.55"><label>ci.37.55</label> na cātisnigdhamaśanaṃ
            bhojayitvā 'nuvāsayet | madaṃ mūrcchāṃ ca janayed dvidhā snehaḥ prayojitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.56"><label>ci.37.56</label> rūkṣaṃ bhuktavato hyannaṃ balaṃ
            varṇaṃ ca hāpayet | yuktasnehamato jantuṃ bhojayitvā 'nuvāsayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.57"><label>ci.37.57</label> yūṣakṣīrarasais tasmādyathāvyādhi
            samīkṣya vā | yathocitāt pādahīnaṃ bhojayitvā 'nuvāsayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.58"><label>ci.37.58</label> athānuvāsyaṃ
            svabhyaktamuṣṇāmbusveditaṃ śanaiḥ | bhojayitvā yathāśāstraṃ kṛtacaṅkramṇaṃ
            tataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.59"><label>ci.37.59</label> visṛjya ca śakṛnmūtraṃ yojayet
            snehabastinā | praṇidhānavidhānaṃ tu nirūhe saṃpravakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.60"><label>ci.37.60</label> tataḥ praṇihitasneha uttāno
            vākśataṃ bhavet | prasāritaiḥ sarvagātrais tathā vīryaṃ visarpati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.61"><label>ci.37.61</label> tāḍayettalayorenaṃ trīṃstrīn
            vārāñchanaiḥ śanaiḥ | sphicoścainaṃ tataḥ śayyāṃ trīn vārānutkṣipettataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.62"><label>ci.37.62</label> evaṃ praṇihite bastau
            mandāyāso 'tha mandavāk | svāstīrṇe śayane kāmamāsītācārike rataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.63"><label>ci.37.63</label> sa tu saindhavacūrṇena <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>śatāhvena ca yojitaḥ | deyaḥ
            sukhoṣṇaś ca tathā nireti sahasā sukham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.64"><label>ci.37.64</label> yasyānuvāsano dattaḥ
            sakṛdanvakṣamāvrajet | atyauṣṇyādatitaikṣṇyādvā vāyunā vā prapīḍitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.65"><label>ci.37.65</label> savāto 'dhikamātro vā gurutvādvā
            sabheṣajaḥ | tasyānyo 'lpataro deyo na hi snihyatyatiṣṭhati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.66"><label>ci.37.66</label> viṣṭabdhānilaviṇmūtraḥ
              snehahīne 'nuvāsane<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> |
            dāhaklamapravāhārtikaraścātyanuvāsanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.67"><label>ci.37.67</label> sānilaḥ sapurīṣaś ca snehaḥ
            pratyeti yasya tu | oṣacoṣau vinā śīghraṃ sa samyaganuvāsitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.68"><label>ci.37.68</label> jīrṇānnamatha sāyāhne snehe
            pratyāgate punaḥ | laghvannaṃ bhojayet kāmaṃ dīptāgnis tu naro yadi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.69"><label>ci.37.69</label> prātaruṣṇodakaṃ <ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>deyaṃ dhānyanāgarasādhitam |
            tenāsya dīpyate vahnirbhaktākāṅkṣā ca jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.70"><label>ci.37.70</label> snehabastikrameṣvevaṃ
            vidhimāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ | anena vidhinā ṣaḍ vā sapta vā 'ṣṭau navaiva vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.71"><label>ci.37.71</label> vidheyā bastayasteṣāmantarā tu
            nirūhaṇam | dattas tu prathamo bastiḥ snehayedbastivaṅkṣaṇau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.72"><label>ci.37.72</label> samyagdatto dvitīyastu
            mūrdhasthamanilaṃ jayet | janayedbalavarṇau ca tṛtīyas tu prayojitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.73"><label>ci.37.73</label> rasaṃ caturtho raktaṃ tu pañcamaḥ
            snehayettathā | ṣaṣṭhas tu snehayenmāṃsaṃ medaḥ saptama eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.74"><label>ci.37.74</label> aṣṭamo navamaścāsthi majjānaṃ ca
            yathākramam | evaṃ śukragatān doṣān dviguṇaḥ sādhu sādhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.75"><label>ci.37.75</label> aṣṭādaśāṣṭādaśakān bastīnāṃ yo
            niṣevate | yathokena vidhānena parihārakrameṇa ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.76"><label>ci.37.76</label> sa kuñjarabalo 'śvasya
            javais tulyo 'maraprabhaḥ | vītapāpmā śrutadharaḥ sahasrāyurnaro bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.77"><label>ci.37.77</label> snehabastiṃ nirūhaṃ vā
            naikamevātiśīlayet | snehādagnivadhotkleśau nirūhāt pavanādbhayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.78"><label>ci.37.78</label> tasmānnirūḍho 'nuvāsyo
            nirūhyaścānuvāsitaḥ | naivaṃ pittakaphotkleśau syātāṃ na pavanādbhayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.79"><label>ci.37.79</label> rūkṣāya bahuvātāya snehavastiṃ
            dine dine | dadyādvaidyastato 'nyeṣāmagnyābādhabhayāttryahāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.80"><label>ci.37.80</label> sneho 'lpamātro rūkṣāṇāṃ
            dīrghakālamanatyayaḥ | tathā nirūhaḥ snigdhānāmalpamātraḥ praśasyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.81"><label>ci.37.81</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi vyāpadaḥ
            snehabastijāḥ | balavanto yadā doṣāḥ koṣṭhe syuranilādayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.82"><label>ci.37.82</label> alpavīryaṃ tadā sneham abhibhūya
            pṛthagvidhān | kurvantyupadravān snehaḥ sa cāpi na nivartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.83"><label>ci.37.83</label> tatra vātābhibhūte tu snehe
            mukhakaṣāyatā | jṛmbhā vātarujastāstā vepathurviṣamajvaraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.84"><label>ci.37.84</label> pittābhibhūte snehe tu mukhasya
            kaṭutā bhavet | <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>dāhastṛṣṇā
            jvaraḥ svedo netramūtrāṅgapītatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.85"><label>ci.37.85</label> śleṣmābhibhūte snehe tu praseko
            madhurāsyatā | gauravaṃ chardirucchvāsaḥ kṛcchrācchītajvaro 'ruciḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.86"><label>ci.37.86</label> tatra doṣābhibhūte tu snehe
            bastiṃ nidhāpayet | yathāsvaṃ doṣaśamanānyupayojyāni yāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.87"><label>ci.37.87</label> atyāśite 'nnābhibhavāt sneho naiti
            yadā tadā | gururāmāśayaḥ śūlaṃ vāyoścāpratisaṃcaraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.88"><label>ci.37.88</label> hṛtpīḍā mukhavair asyṃa śvāso
            mūrcchā bhramo 'ruciḥ | tatrāpatarpaṇasyānte dīpano vidhiriṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.89"><label>ci.37.89</label> aśuddhasya malonmiśraḥ sneho
            naiti yadā punaḥ | tadā 'ṅgasadanādhmāne śvāsaḥ śūlaṃ ca jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.90"><label>ci.37.90</label> pakvāśayagurutvaṃ ca tatra
            dadyān nirūhaṇam | tīkṣṇaṃ tīkṣṇauṣadhaireva siddhaṃ cāpyanuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.91"><label>ci.37.91</label> śuddhasya dūrānusṛte snehe
            snehasya darśanam | gātreṣu sarvendriyāṇām upalepo 'vasādanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.92"><label>ci.37.92</label> snehagandhi mukhaṃ cāpi
            kāsaśvāsāvarocakaḥ | atipīḍitavattatra siddhirāsthāpanaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.93"><label>ci.37.93</label> asvinnasyāviśuddhasya sneho 'lpaḥ
            saṃprayojitaḥ | śīto mṛduś ca nābhyeti tato mandaṃ <ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref>pravāhate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.94"><label>ci.37.94</label> vibandhagauravādhmānaśūlāḥ
            pakvāśayaṃ prati | tatrāsthāpanam evāśu prayojyaṃ sānuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.95"><label>ci.37.95</label> alpaṃ bhuktavato 'lpo hi sneho
            mandaguṇas tathā | datto naiti klamotkleśau bhṛśaṃ cāratimāvahet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.96"><label>ci.37.96</label> tatrāpyāsthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ
            śodhanīyena bastinā | (anvāsanaṃ ca snehena śodhanīyena śasyate<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.97"><label>ci.37.97</label> ahorātrādapi snehaḥ
            pratyāgacchanna duṣyati | kuryād bastiguṇāṃś cāpi jīrṇastvalpaguṇo bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.98"><label>ci.37.98</label> yasya nopadravaṃ kuryāt
            snehabastiraniḥsṛtaḥ | sarvo 'lpo vā++āvṛto raukṣyādupekṣyaḥ sa vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.99"><label>ci.37.99</label> anāyāntaṃ tvahorātrāt snehaṃ
            saṃśodhanairharet | snehabastāvanāyāte nānyaḥ sneho vidhīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.100"><label>ci.37.100</label> ity uktā vyāpadaḥ sarvā
            salakṣaṇacikitsitāḥ | basteruttarasaṃjñasya vidhiṃ vakṣyāmyataḥ param || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.101"><label>ci.37.101</label> caturdaśāṅgulaṃ
            netramāturāṅgulasaṃmitam | <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>mālatīpuṣpavṛntāgraṃ chidraṃ sarṣapanirgamam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.102"><label>ci.37.102</label> snehapramāṇaṃ paramaṃ
            prakuñcaścātra kīrtitaḥ | pañcaviṃśādadho mātrāṃ vidadhyādbuddhikalpitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.103"><label>ci.37.103</label> niviṣṭakarṇikaṃ madhye nārīṇāṃ
            caturaṅgule | mūtrasrotaḥparīṇāhaṃ mudgavāhi daśāṅgulam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.104"><label>ci.37.104</label> meḍhrāyāmasamaṃ kecidicchanti
            khalu tadvidaḥ | tāsāmapatyamārge tu nidadhyāccaturaṅgulam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.105"><label>ci.37.105</label> dvyaṅgulaṃ mūtramārge tu
            kanyānāṃ tvekamaṅgulam | vidheyaṃ cāṅgulaṃ tāsāṃ vidhivadvakṣyate yathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.106"><label>ci.37.106</label> snehasya prasṛtaṃ cātra
            svāṅgulīmūlasaṃmitam | deyaṃ pramāṇaṃ paramamarvāg buddhivikalpitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.107"><label>ci.37.107</label> aurabhraḥ śaukaro vā 'pi
            bastirājaś ca pūjitaḥ | tadalābhe prayuñjīta galacarma tu pakṣiṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.108"><label>ci.37.108</label> (tasyālābhe dṛteḥ pādo
            mṛducarma tato 'pi vā<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>) |
            athāturam upasnigdhaṃ svinnaṃ praśithilāśayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.109"><label>ci.37.109</label> yavāgūṃ saghṛtakṣīrāṃ
            pītavantaṃ yathābalam | niṣaṇṇamājānusame pīṭhe sopāśraye samam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.110"><label>ci.37.110</label> svabhyaktabastimūrdhānaṃ
            tailenoṣṇena mānavam | tataḥ samaṃ sthāpayitvā nālamasya praharṣitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.111"><label>ci.37.111</label> pūrvaṃ śalākayā 'nviṣya tato
            netramanantaram | śanaiḥ śanairghṛtābhyaktaṃ vidadhyādaṅgulāni ṣaṭ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.112"><label>ci.37.112</label> meḍhrayāmasamaṃ kecidicchanti
            praṇidhānakam | tato 'vapīḍayedbastiṃ śanairnetraṃ ca nirharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.113"><label>ci.37.113</label> tataḥ pratyāgatasnehamaparāhṇe
            vicakṣaṇaḥ | bhojayet payasā <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>mātrāṃ yūṣeṇātha rasena vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.114"><label>ci.37.114</label> anena vidhinā
            dadyādbastīṃstrīṃścaturo 'pi vā | ūrdhvajānvai striyai dadyāduttānāyai
            vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.115"><label>ci.37.115</label> samyak prapīḍayedyoniṃ dadyāt
            sumṛdupīḍitam | trikarṇikena netreṇa dadyādyonimukhaṃ prati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.116"><label>ci.37.116</label> garbhāśayaviśuddhyarthaṃ
            snehena dviguṇena tu | <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>kvāthapramāṇaṃ prasṛtaṃ striyā dviprasṛtaṃ bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.117"><label>ci.37.117</label> kanyetarasyāḥ
            kanyāyāstadvadbastipramāṇakam | apratyāgacchati bhiṣag bastāvuttarasaṃjñite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.118"><label>ci.37.118</label> bhūyo bastiṃ nidadhyāttu
            saṃyuktaṃ śodhanairgaṇaiḥ | gude vartiṃ nidadhyādvā śodhanadravyasaṃbhṛtām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.119"><label>ci.37.119</label> praveśayedvā matimān
            bastidvāramathaiṣaṇīm | pīḍayedvā 'pyadho nābherbalenottaramuṣṭinā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.120"><label>ci.37.120</label> āragvadhasya patrais tu
            nirguṇḍyāḥ svarasena ca | kuryād gomūtrapiṣṭeṣu vartīrvā 'pi sasaindhavāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.121"><label>ci.37.121</label> mudgailāsarṣapasamāḥ
            pravibhajya vayāṃsi tu | basterāgamanārthāya tā nidadhyāchalākayā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.122"><label>ci.37.122</label>
            āgāradhūmabṛhatīpippalīphalasaindhavaiḥ | kṛtā vā śuktagomūtrasurāpiṣṭaiḥ
            sanāgaraiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.123"><label>ci.37.123</label> anuvāsanasiddhiṃ ca vīkṣya
            karma prayojayet | śarkarāmadhumiśreṇa śītena madhukāmbunā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.124"><label>ci.37.124</label> dahyamāne tadā bastau
            dadyādbastiṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ | kṣīravṛkṣakaṣāyeṇa payasā śītalena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.125"><label>ci.37.125</label> śukraṃ duṣṭaṃ śoṇitaṃ
            cāṅganānāṃ puṣpodrekaṃ tasya nāṇaṃ ca kaṣṭam | mūtrāghātānmūtradoṣān
            pravṛddhān yonivyādhiṃ saṃsthitiṃ cāparāyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.126"><label>ci.37.126</label> śukrotsekaṃ śarkarāmaśmarīṃ ca
            śūlaṃ bastau vaṅkṣaṇe mehane ca | ghorānanyān bastijāṃś cāpi rogān hitvā
            mehānuttaro hanti bastiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.37.127"><label>ci.37.127</label> samyagdattasya liṅgāni vyāpadaḥ
            krama eva ca | basteruttarasaṃjñasya samānaṃ snehabastinā ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ
            cikitsāsthāne 'nuvāsanottarabasticikitsitaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||37 ||
          </p>

        <div n="38" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>aṣṭatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.38.1"><label>ci.38.1</label> athāto nirūhakramacikitsitaṃ
            vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.38.2"><label>ci.38.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.38.3"><label>ci.38.3</label> athānuvāsitamāsthāpayet;
            svabhyaktasvinnaśarīramutsṛṣṭabahirvegamavāte śucau veśmani madhyāhne
            pratatāyāṃ śayyāyāmadhaḥsuparigrahāyāṃ
            śroṇipradeśaprativyūḍhāyāmanupadhānāyāṃ
            vāmapārśvaśāyinamākuñcitadakṣiṇasakthimitaraprasāritasakthiṃ sumanasaṃ
            jīrṇānnaṃ vāgyataṃ suniṣaṇṇadehaṃ viditvā, tato vāmapādasyopari netraṃ
            kṛtvetarapādāṅguṣṭhāṅgulibhyāṃ karṇikām upari niṣpīḍya,
            savyapāṇikaniṣṭhikānāmikābhyāṃ bastermukhārdhaṃ saṅkocya,
            madhyamāpradeśinyaṅguṣṭhair ardhaṃ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
              >*</ref> tu vivṛtāsyaṃ kṛtvā, bastāvauṣadhaṃ prakṣipya,
            dakṣiṇahastāṅguṣṭhena pradeśinīmadhyamābhyāṃ
              cānusiktamanāyatamabudbudamasaṅkucitamavātamauṣadhāsannam upasaṃgṛhya<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>, punarupari taditareṇa
            gṛhītvā dakṣiṇenāvasiñcet, tataḥ sūtreṇaivauṣadhānte dvistrirvā++āveṣṭya
            badhnīyāt, atha dakṣiṇenottānena pāṇinā bastiṃ gṛhītvā
            vāmahastamadhyamāṅgulipradeśinībhyāṃ netram upasaṃgṛhyāṅguṣṭena netradvāraṃ
            pidhāya, ghṛtābhyaktāgranetraṃ ghṛtāktamupādāya prayacched anupṛṣṭhavaṃśaṃ
            samamunmukhamākarṇikaṃ netraṃ praṇidhatsveti brūyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.38.4"><label>ci.38.4</label> bastiṃ savye kare kṛtvā
            dakṣiṇenāvapīḍayet | ekenaivāvapīḍena na drutaṃ na vilambitam || </l>

            vārāhamāhiṣaurabhrabaiḍālaiṇeyakaukkuṭam | <ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref>sadyaskamasṛgājaṃ vā deyaṃ
            picchilabastiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.38.88"><label>ci.38.88</label> eteṣv eva ca yogeṣu snehāḥ siddhāḥ

          <l xml:id="SS.4.38.91"><label>ci.38.91</label> evaṃ kālaṃ balaṃ doṣaṃ vikāraṃ ca

          <l xml:id="SS.4.38.92"><label>ci.38.92</label> dadyādutkleśanaṃ pūrvaṃ madhye

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne āturopadravacikitsitaṃ
