        <div n="40" type="adhyāyaḥ">
          <head>catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.1"><label>ci.40.1</label> athāto
            dhūmanasyakavalagrahacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.2"><label>ci.40.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.3"><label>ci.40.3</label> dhūmaḥ pañcavidho bhavati tadyathā
            prāyogikaḥ, snaihiko, vairenikaḥ, kāsaghno, vāmanīyaś ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.4"><label>ci.40.4</label> tatrailādinā kuṣṭhatagaravarjyena
            ślakṣṇapiṣṭena dvādaśāṅgulaṃ śarakāṇḍamaṅgulipariṇāhaṃ kṣaumeṇāṣṭāṅgulaṃ
            veṣṭayitvā lepayedeṣā vartiḥ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>prāyogike, snehaphalasāramadhūcchiṣṭasarjarasagugguluprabhṛtibhiḥ
            snehamiśraiḥ snaihike, śirovirecanadravyairvairecane,
            bṛhatīkaṇṭakārikātrikaṭukāsamardahiṅgviṅgudītvaṅmanaḥśilācchinnaruhākarkaṭaśṛṅgīprabhṛtibhiḥ
            kāsaharaiś ca kāsaghne,
            snāyucarmakhuraśṛṅgakarkaṭakāsthiśuṣkamatsyavallūrakṛmiprabhṛtibhirvāmanīyaiśca
            vāmanīye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.5"><label>ci.40.5</label> tatra
            bastinetradravyairdhūmanetradravyāṇi vyākhyātāni bhavanti | dhūmanetraṃ tu
            kaniṣṭhikāpariṇāhamagre kalāyamātrasroto mūle 'ṅguṣṭhapariṇāhaṃ
            dhūmavartipraveśasroto 'ṅgulānyaṣṭacatvāriṃśat prāyogike, dvātriṃśat snehane,
            caturviṃśatirvairecane, ṣoḍaśāṅgulaṃ kāsaghne vāmanīye ca | ete 'pi
            kolāsthimātracchidre bhavataḥ | vraṇanetramaṣṭāṅgulaṃ vraṇadhūpanārthaṃ
            kalāyaparimaṇḍalaṃ kulatthavāhisrota iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.6"><label>ci.40.6</label> atha sukhopaviṣṭaḥ sumanā
            ṛjvadhodṛṣṭiratandritaḥ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
            >*</ref>snehāktadīpatāgrāṃ vartiṃ netrasrotasi praṇidhāya dhūmaṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.7"><label>ci.40.7</label> mukhena taṃ pibet pūrvaṃ
            nāsikābhyāṃ tataḥ pibet | mukhapītaṃ mukhenaiva vamet pītaṃ ca nāsayā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.8"><label>ci.40.8</label> mukhena dhūmamādāya nāsikābhyāṃ na
            nirharet | tena hi pratilomena dṛṣṭis tatra nihanyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.9"><label>ci.40.9</label> viśeṣatas tu prāyogikaṃ
            ghrāṇenādadīta, snaihikaṃ mukhanāsābhyāṃ, nāsikayā vairecanikaṃ,
            mukhenaivetarau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.10"><label>ci.40.10</label> tatra prāyogike vartiṃ
            vyapagataśarakāṇḍāṃ nivātātapaśuṣkāmaṅgāreṣv avadīpya netramūlasrotasi
            prayujyadhūmamāhareti brūyāt; evaṃ snehanaṃ vairecanikaṃ ca kuryād iti |
              itarayorvyapetadhūmāṅgāre<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>
            sthire samāhite śarāve prakṣipya vartiṃ mūlacchidreṇānyena śarāveṇa pidhāya
            tasmin chidre netramūlaṃ saṃyojya dhūmamāseveta, praśānte dhūme
            vartimavaśiṣṭāṃ prakṣipya punarapi dhūmaṃ pāyayedādoṣaviśuddheḥ; eṣa
            dhūmapānopāyavidhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.11"><label>ci.40.11</label> tatra
            śokaśramabhayāmarṣauṣṇyaviṣaraktapittamadamūrcchādāhapipāsāpāṇḍurogatāluśoṣacchardiśiro 'bhighātodgārāpatarpitatimirapramehodarādhmānordhvavātārtā
            bālavṛddhadurbalaviriktāsthāpitajāgaritagarbhiṇīrūkṣakṣīṇakṣatoraskamadhughṛtad adhidugdhamatsyamadyayavāgūpītālpakaphāśca
            na dhūmamāseveran || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.12"><label>ci.40.12</label> akālapītaḥ kurute bhramaṃ
            mūrcchāṃ śirorujam | ghrāṇaśrotrākṣijihvānām upaghātaṃ ca dāruṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.13"><label>ci.40.13</label> ādyās tu trayo dhūmā dvādaśasu
            kāleṣūpādeyāḥ | tadyathā
            kṣutadantaprakṣālananasyasnānabhojanadivāsvapnamaithunacchardimūtroccārahasitaruṣitaśastrakarmānteṣv iti |
            tatra vibhāgo mūtroccārakṣavathuhasitaruṣitamaithunānteṣu snaihikaḥ,
            snānacchardivāsvapnānteṣu vairecanikaḥ, dantaprakṣālanasya
            snānabhojanaśastrakarmānteṣu prāyogika iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.14"><label>ci.40.14</label> tatra snaihiko vātaṃ śamayati,
            snehād upalepāc ca; vairecanaḥ śleṣmāṇamutkleśyāpakarṣati,
            raukṣyāttaikṣṇyādauṣṇyādvaiśadyācca; prāyogikaḥ
            śleṣmāṇamutkleśayatyutkliṣṭaṃ cāpakarṣati śamayati vātaṃ sādhāraṇatvāt
            pūrvābhyām iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.15"><label>ci.40.15</label> bhavati cātra naro dhūmopayogācca
            prasannendriyavāṅmanāḥ | dṛḍhakeśadvijaśmaśruḥ sugandhiviśadānanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.16"><label>ci.40.16</label> tathā
            kāsaśvāsārocakāsyopalepasvarabhedamukhāsrāvakṣavathuvamathukrathatandrānidrāhanumanyāstambhāḥ
            pīnasaśirorogakarṇākṣiśūlā vātakaphanimittāścāsya mukharogā na bhavanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.17"><label>ci.40.17</label> tasya yogāyogātiyogā vijñātavyāḥ |
            tatra yogo rogapraśamanaḥ, ayogo rogāpraśamanaḥ,
              tālugalaśoṣaparidāhapipāsāmūrcchābhramamadakarṇakṣveḍadṛṣṭināsārogadaurbalyānyatiyogo<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> janayati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.18"><label>ci.40.18</label> prāyogikaṃ
            trīṃstrīnucchvāsānādadīta mukhanāsikābhyāṃ ca paryāyāṃstrīṃścaturo veti,
            snaihikaṃ yāvadaśrupravṛttiḥ, vairecanikamādoṣadarśanāt,
            tilataṇḍulayavāgūpītena pātavyo vāmanīyaḥ, grāsāntareṣu kāsaghna iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.19"><label>ci.40.19</label> vraṇadhūmaṃ śarāvasaṃpuṭopanītena
            netreṇa vraṇamānayet, dhūmapānādvedanopaśamo vraṇavaiśadyamāsrāvopaśamaś ca
            bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.20"><label>ci.40.20</label> vidhireṣa samāsena
            dhūmasyābhihito mayā | nasyasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ niravaśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.21"><label>ci.40.21</label> auṣadhamauṣadhasiddho vā sneho
            nāsikābhyāṃ dīyata iti nasyam | taddvividhaṃ śirovirecanaṃ, snehanaṃ ca |
            taddvividham api pañcadhā | tadyathā nasyaṃ, śirovirecanaṃ, pratimarśo,
            avapīḍaḥ, pradhamanaṃ ca | teṣu nasyaṃ pradhānaṃ śirovirecanaṃ ca;
            nasyavikalpaḥ pratimarśaḥ, śirovirecanavikalpo 'vapīḍaḥ pradhamanaṃ ca; tato
            nasyaśabdaḥ pañcadhā niyamitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.22"><label>ci.40.22</label> tatra yaḥ snehanārthaṃ
            śūnyaśirasāṃ grīvāskandhorasāṃ ca balajananārthaṃ dṛṣṭiprasādajananārthaṃ vā
            sneho vidhīyate tasmin vaiśeṣiko nasyaśabdaḥ | tat tu deyaṃ vātābhibhūte
            śirasi
            dantakeśaśmaśruprapātadāruṇakarṇaśūlakarṇakṣveḍatimirasvaropaghātanāsārogāsyaśoṣāvabāhukākālajavalīpalitaprādurbhāvadāruṇaprabodheṣu
            vātapaittikeṣu mukharogeṣv anyeṣu ca vātapittaharadravyasiddhena sneheneti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.23"><label>ci.40.23</label> śirovirecanaṃ
            śleṣmaṇā 'bhivyāptatālukaṇṭhaśirasāmarocakaśirogauravaśūlapīnasārdhāvabhedakakṛmipratiśyāyāpasmāragandhājñāneṣv anyeṣu
            cordhvajatrugateṣu kaphajeṣu vikāreṣu śirovirecanadravyais tatsiddhena vā
            sneheneti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.24"><label>ci.40.24</label>
            tatraitaddvividhamapyabhuktavato 'nnakāle pūrvāhṇe śleṣmarogiṇāṃ, madhyāhne
            pittarogiṇāṃ, aparāhṇe vātarogiṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.25"><label>ci.40.25</label> atha puruṣāya śirovirecanīyāya
            tyaktamūtrapurīṣāya bhuktavate vyabhre kāle dantakāṣṭhadhūmapānābhyāṃ
            viśuddhavaktrasrotase pāṇitāpaparisvinnamṛditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśāya
            vātātaparajohīne veśmanyuttānaśāyine prasāritakaracaraṇāya kiñcit
            pravilambitaśirase vastrācchāditanetrāya
            vāmahastapradeśinyagronnāmitanāsāgrāya viśuddhasrotasi dakṣiṇahastena
            sneham uṣṇāmbunā prataptaṃ
            rajatasuvarṇatāmramaṇimṛtpātraśuktīnām anyatamasthaṃ śuktyā<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> picunā vā sukhoṣṇaṃ
            snehamadrutam āsiñced avyavacchinnadhāraṃ yathā netre na prāpnoti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.26"><label>ci.40.26</label> snehe 'vasicyamāne tu śiro naiva
            prakampayet | na kupyen na prabhāṣec ca na kṣuyān na haset tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.27"><label>ci.40.27</label> etairhi vihataḥ sneho na samyak
            pratipadyate | tataḥ kāsapratiśyāyaśiro 'kṣigadasaṃbhavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.28"><label>ci.40.28</label> tasya pramāṇamaṣtau bindavaḥ
            pradeśinīparvadvayaniḥsṛtāḥ prathamā mātrā, dvitīyā śuktiḥ, tṛtīyā
            pāṇiśuktiḥ, ityetāstisro mātrā yathābalaṃ prayojyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.29"><label>ci.40.29</label> snehanasyaṃ nopagilet kathaṃ cid api
            buddhimān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.30"><label>ci.40.30</label> śṛṅgāṭakam abhiplāvya nireti
            vadanād yathā | kaphotkleśabhayāccainaṃ niṣṭhīvedavidhārayan || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.31"><label>ci.40.31</label> datte ca punarapi saṃsvedya
            galakapolādīn dhūmamāseveta, bhojayeccainam abhiṣyandi,
            tato 'syācārikam ādiśet;
            rajodhūmasnehātapamadyadravapānaśiraḥsnānātiyānakrodhādīni ca pariharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.32"><label>ci.40.32</label> tasya yogātiyogāyogānāmidaṃ
            vijñānaṃ bhavati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.33"><label>ci.40.33</label> lāghavaṃ śiraso yoge
            sukhasvapnaprabodhanam | vikāropaśamaḥ śuddhirindiryāṇāṃ manaḥsukham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.34"><label>ci.40.34</label> kaphaprasekaḥ śiraso
            gurutendriyavibhramaḥ | lakṣaṇaṃ mūrdhnayatisnigdhe rūkṣaṃ tatrāvacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.35"><label>ci.40.35</label> ayoge vātavaiguṇyamindriyāṇāṃ ca
            rūkṣatā | rogāśāntiś ca tatreṣṭaṃ bhūyo nasyaṃ prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.36"><label>ci.40.36</label> catvāro bindavaḥ ṣaḍ vā
            tathā 'ṣṭau vā yathābalam | śirovirekasnehasya pramāṇam abhinirdiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.37"><label>ci.40.37</label> nasye trīṇyupadiṣṭāni lakṣaṇāni
            prayogataḥ | śuddha(śuddhi)hīnātisaṃjñāni viśeṣācchāstracintakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.38"><label>ci.40.38</label> lāghavaṃ śirasaḥ suddhiḥ srotasāṃ
            vyādhinirjayaḥ | cittendriyaprasādaś ca śirasaḥ śuddhilakṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.39"><label>ci.40.39</label> kaṇḍūpadehau gurutā srotasāṃ
            kaphasaṃsravaḥ | mūrdhni hīnaviśuddhe tu lakṣaṇaṃ parikīrtitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.40"><label>ci.40.40</label> mastuluṅgāgamo
            vātavṛddhirindriyavibhramaḥ | śūnyatā śirasaś cāpi mūrdhni gāḍhavirecite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.41"><label>ci.40.41</label> hīnātiśuddhe śirasi
            kaphavātaghnamācaret | samyagviśuddhe śirasi sarpirnasyaṃ niṣecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.42"><label>ci.40.42</label> (ekāntaraṃ dvyanataraṃ vā
            saptāhaṃ vā punaḥ punaḥ | ekaviṃśatirātraṃ vā yāvadvā sādhu manyate ||) </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.43"><label>ci.40.43</label> mārutenābhibhūtasya vā 'tyantaṃ
            yasya dehinaḥ | dvikālaṃ cāpi dātavyaṃ nasyaṃ tasya vijānatā<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> ||) </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44"><label>ci.40.44</label> avapīḍastu
            śirovirecanavadabhiṣyaṇṇasarpadaṣṭavisaṃjñebhyo
              dadyāc chirocirecanadravyāṇām anyatamam avapiṣyāvapīḍya<ref
              rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> ca,
            śarkarekṣurasakṣīraghṛtamāṃsarasānām anyatamaṃ kṣīṇānāṃ śoṇitapitte ca
            vidadhyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.45"><label>ci.40.45</label> kṛśadurbalabhīrūṇāṃ sukumārasya
            yoṣitām | śṛtāḥ snehāḥ śiraḥśuddhyai kalkastebhyo<ref rend="superscript
              footnote marker">*</ref> yathā hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.46"><label>ci.40.46</label> cetovikārakṛmiviṣābhipannānāṃ
            cūrṇaṃ pradhamet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.47"><label>ci.40.47</label> nasyena parihartavyo
            bhutavānapatarpito 'tyarthataruṇapratiśyāyī garbhiṇī
            pītasnehodakamadyadravo 'jīrṇī dattabastiḥ kruddho garārtastṛṣitaḥ
            śokābhibhūtaḥ ānto bālo vṛddho vegāvarodhitaḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote
              marker">*</ref> śiraḥsnātukāmaś ceti; anārtave
            cābhre nasyadhūmau pariharet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.48"><label>ci.40.48</label> tatra
            hīnātimātrātiśītoṣṇasahasāpradānādatipravilambitaśirasa ucchiṅghato
            vicalato 'bhyavaharato vā pratiṣiddhapradānāc ca vyāpado bhavanti
            tṛṣṇodgārādayo doṣanimittāḥ kṣayajāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.49"><label>ci.40.49</label> bhavataścātra nasye śirovireke ca
            vyāpado dvividhāḥ smṛtāḥ | doṣotkleśāt kṣayāccaiva vijñeyāstā yathākramam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.50"><label>ci.40.50</label> doṣokleśanimittāstu
            jayecchamanaśodhanaiḥ | atha kṣayanimittāsu yathāsvaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.51"><label>ci.40.51</label> pratimarśaścaturdaśasu
            kāleṣūpādeyaḥ; tadyathā talpotthitena, prakṣālitadantena, gṛhānnirgacchatā,
            vyāyāmavyavāyādhvapariśrāntena, mūtroccārakavalāñjanānte, bhuktavatā,
            charditavatā, divāsvapnotthitena, sāyaṃ ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.52"><label>ci.40.52</label> tatra talpotthitenāsevitaḥ
            pratimarśo rātrāvupacitaṃ nāsāsrotogataṃ malam upahanti manaḥprasādaṃ ca
            karoti, prakṣālitadantenāsevito dantānāṃ dṛḍhatāṃ vadanasaugandhyaṃ
            cāpādayati, gṛhānnirgacchatā sevito nāsāseotasaḥ klinnatayā rajodhūmo vā na
            bādhate, vyāyāmamaithunādhvapariśrāntenāsevitaḥ śramam upahanti,
            mūtroccārānte sevito dṛṣṭergurutvamapanayati, kavalāñjanānte sevito dṛṣṭiṃ
            prasādayati, bhuktavatā sevitaḥ srotasāṃ viśuddhiṃ laghutāṃ cāpādayati,
            vāntenāsevitaḥ srotovilagnaṃ śleṣmāṇamapohya bhaktākāṅkṣāmāpādayati,
            divāsvapnotthitenāsevito nidrāśeṣaṃ gurutvaṃ malaṃ cāpohya cittaikāgryaṃ
            janayati, sāyaṃ cāsevitaḥ sukhanidrāprabodhaṃ ceti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.53"><label>ci.40.53</label> īṣaducchiṅghataḥ sneho
            yāvadvaktraṃ prapadyate | nasye niṣiktaṃ taṃ vidyāt pratimarśaṃ pramāṇataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.54"><label>ci.40.54</label> nasyena rogāḥ śāmyanti
            narāṇāmūrdhvajatrujāḥ | indriyāṇāṃ ca vaimalyaṃ kuryād āsyaṃ sugandhi ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.55"><label>ci.40.55</label> hanudantaśirogrīvātrikabāhūrasāṃ
            balam | valīpalitakhālityavyaṅgānāṃ cāpyasaṃbhavam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.56"><label>ci.40.56</label> tailaṃ kaphe savāte syāt kevale
            pavane vasām | dadyātsarpiḥ sadā pitte majjānaṃ ca samārute || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.57"><label>ci.40.57</label> caturvidhasya snehasya vidhirevaṃ
            prakīrtitaḥ | śleṣmasthānāvirodhitvātteṣu tailaṃ vidhīyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.58"><label>ci.40.58</label> ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi
            kavalagrahaṇe vidhim | caturdhā kavalaḥ snehī prasādī śodhiropaṇau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.59"><label>ci.40.59</label> sngidhoṣṇaiḥ snaihiko vāte
            svāduśītaiḥ prasādanaḥ | pitte kaṭvamlalavaṇai rūkṣoṣṇaiḥ śodhanaḥ kaphe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.60"><label>ci.40.60</label> kaṣāyatiktamadhuraiḥ kaṭūṣṇai
            ropaṇo vraṇe | caturvidhasya caivāsya viśeṣo 'yaṃ prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.61"><label>ci.40.61</label> tatra
            trikaṭukavacāsarṣapaharītakīkalkamāloḍya
            tailaśuktasurāmūtrakṣāramadhūnāmanyatamena
            salavaṇam abhiprataptam upasvinnamṛditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśo dhārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.62"><label>ci.40.62</label> sukhaṃ saṃcāryate yā tu mātrā sa
            (sā) kavalaḥ smṛtaḥ | asaṃcāryā tu yā mātrā gaṇḍūṣaḥ sa prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.63"><label>ci.40.63</label> tāvacca
            dhārayitavyo 'nanyamanasonnatadehena yāvaddoṣaparipūrṇakapolatvaṃ
            nāsāsrotonayanapariplāvaś ca bhavati tadā vimoktavyaḥ, punaścānyo grahītavya
            iti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.64"><label>ci.40.64</label> evaṃ
            snehapayaḥkṣaudrarasamūtrāmlasaṃbhṛtāḥ | kasāyoṣṇodakābhyāṃ ca kavalā doṣato
            hitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.65"><label>ci.40.65</label> vyādherapacayastuṣṭirvaiśadyaṃ
            vaktralāghavam | indiryāṇāṃ prasādaś ca kavale śuddhilakṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.66"><label>ci.40.66</label> hīne
            jāḍyakaphotkleśāvarasajñānam eva ca | atiyogān mukhe pākaḥ
            śoṣatṛṣṇāruciklamāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.67"><label>ci.40.67</label> śodhanīye viśeṣeṇa bhavanty eva na
            saṃśayaḥ | tilā nīlotpalaṃ sarpiḥ śarkarā kṣīram eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.68"><label>ci.40.68</label> sakṣaudro dagdhavaktrasya gaṇḍūṣo
            dāhanāśanaḥ | kavalasya vidhirhyeṣa samāsena prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.69"><label>ci.40.69</label> vibhajya bheṣajaṃ buddhyā kurvīta
            pratisāraṇam | kalko rasakriyā kṣaudraṃ cūrṇaṃ ceti caturvidham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.70"><label>ci.40.70</label> aṅgulyagrapraṇītaṃ tu yathāsvaṃ
            mukharogiṇām | tasmin yogamayogaṃ ca kavaloktaṃ vibhāvayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.40.71"><label>ci.40.71</label> tān eva śamayed vyādhīn kavalo
            yān apohati | doṣaghnam anabhiṣyandi bhojayec ca tathā naram ||</l>

          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
            dhūmanasyakavalagrahacikitsitaṃ nāma catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
